Chapter 1: Introduction & Key Concepts

導論與關鍵概念 | p9-p18

ISPE Baseline® Guide: Commissioning and Qualification (2nd Edition) | p9 – p18

本章學習目標

  • 理解 C&Q（Commissioning and Qualification，試車與確效）的核心定義，以及它與傳統 IQ/OQ/PQ 方法的本質差異
  • 掌握 CDE（Critical Design Element，關鍵設計要素）、CA（Critical Aspect，關鍵特性）與 CPP/CQA 之間的層級關係
  • 了解本指引第二版的主要改版邏輯——為何廢除 V-Model、重視 QRM，以及何謂「不重複測試」原則
  • 熟悉本章定義的 15 個關鍵術語，並能區分 Commissioning、Qualification、Verification 三者的異同
  • 理解 Quality Unit（品質單位）在 C&Q 過程中的正確角色定位
1.1 Background（背景）

原文內容 Original Text

It is a universal regulatory expectation that pharmaceutical manufacturing facilities, systems, utilities, and equipment are designed, constructed and qualified to be suitable for the intended purpose. Regulatory authorities have indicated in their guidances and regulations that organizations must build quality into their processes and products. This Guide intends to offer a compliant, integrated commissioning and qualification process that is based on a science and risk-based approach. This process supports Quality by Design (QbD) and ensures that risks to product quality from the systems are adequately addressed.

It is recognized that the terminologies for the commissioning and qualification process are varied. The overall process has traditionally been called commissioning and qualification; ASTM E2500-13 refers to the process as verification. This second edition of the Baseline® Guide focuses on the approach; the terminology used is not as important as the approach. For the purposes of this Guide, the term Commissioning and Qualification (C&Q) is used to describe the process for establishing that facilities, systems, utilities, and equipment are suitable for the intended purpose. The term verification is used to describe an activity performed during the C&Q process to establish suitability for the intended purpose.

Commissioning and qualification differ only in that the qualification process has oversight by the Quality Unit, focused on the system risk to product quality. The Quality Unit ultimately decides whether systems are suitable for the intended purpose, based on the identification, testing, and documentation of the system features deemed critical to product quality.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：C&Q 的本質

Commissioning（試車）：工程師確認系統按設計安裝並正常運作的過程。強調技術符合性，不需要 QA 審批。

Qualification（確效）：在 Commissioning 基礎上，由 Quality Unit 監督，聚焦於產品品質風險，證明系統「適合預定用途」。

兩者的關鍵差異只有一個：Quality Unit 的參與程度。這個洞見是本版 ISPE 指引最重要的訊息之一。

比喻說明：工廠安裝如同蓋新廚房

想像你開一家餐廳，安裝全新廚房設備。
Commissioning = 水電師傅確認瓦斯爐點火正常、冰箱溫度正確——這是工程驗收。
Qualification = 衛生局稽查員確認設備符合食安標準，並核發許可——這是法規合規層面。
藥廠的 C&Q 就是把「工程驗收」和「法規合規」整合成一個有效率的流程，避免重複測試。

重點提示：名稱不重要，方法才重要

ISPE 刻意說「術語不如方法重要」，是因為各公司、各國法規對 IQ/OQ/PQ/FAT/SAT 的叫法差異極大。ISPE Vol.5 2nd Ed. 提供的是一套方法論框架，讓你不管用什麼名詞，都能做到符合法規的確效。

ASTM E2500 將整個過程稱為「verification」，與 ICH Q10 用語不同——這種差異在稽查時常造成混淆，本指引明確統一使用 C&Q 框架。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一台新安裝的 WFI 系統，工程師完成了管路焊接檢查與水質確認，但尚未通知 QA 審核，這個活動屬於 Commissioning 還是 Qualification？為什麼？
  2. 如果一個系統不影響產品品質（例如廠務用自來水管），它是否需要進行 Qualification？請根據本節的定義解釋你的答案。
1.2 Purpose and Objectives（目的與目標）

原文內容 Original Text

This Guide intends to offer a compliant, integrated C&Q approach to making the qualification process efficient and cost-effective. The approach includes a System Risk Assessment process that identifies the Critical Aspects (CAs) and/or Critical Design Elements (CDEs). CDEs are system functions and features identified as having the potential to control risks to product quality and therefore ensure patient safety. Qualification confirms that the CDEs and design risk controls identified through the System Risk Assessment have all been checked, tested, and found to be installed and operating as specified.

This Guide recognizes industry best practices regarding C&Q and presents concepts that can assist organizations in meeting current regulatory expectations for system qualification by:

  • Providing guidance on how to apply Quality Risk Management (QRM) to C&Q to establish CDEs
  • Defining the focus of an integrated C&Q effort to be the CAs/CDEs and Critical Process Parameters (CPPs) which provide the ability to deliver the product Critical Quality Attributes (CQAs)
  • Defining best practices for User Requirements Specification (URS), Design Review (DR), Design Qualification (DQ), and acceptance and release of the system
  • Clarifying the change management processes required to support the C&Q process
  • Providing Good Engineering Practice (GEP) documentation standards
  • Describing where testing should be duplicated and where it is acceptable to test once
  • Addressing integration of equipment automation systems
  • Providing examples of appropriate C&Q deliverables

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：CQA → CPP → CA → CDE 層級關係

這是 ISPE Vol.5 整個框架的邏輯主軸，必須完全理解：

  • CQA（關鍵品質屬性）：藥品必須符合的品質特性，如無菌性、含量、pH
  • CPP（關鍵製程參數）：影響 CQA 的製程參數，如滅菌溫度、充填重量
  • CA（關鍵特性）：製程中必須確保的功能或能力（來自 ASTM E2500）
  • CDE（關鍵設計要素）：設備/系統中直接影響 CA 的具體設計功能或物理特徵

確效的核心任務就是：驗證所有 CDE 都已按設計安裝並正常運作。

關係鏈示意圖

CQA（藥品品質要求）
  ↓ 由 QRM 識別
CPP（製程關鍵參數）
  ↓ 由 SME 分析
CA（系統關鍵特性）
  ↓ 由設計工程師轉化
CDE（設備關鍵設計要素）
  ↓ 由 C&Q 計畫驗證
System Qualification（系統確效）

比喻說明：聚焦 CDE 就像電動車安全稽核

稽核一台電動車的安全性，你不需要測試每一顆螺絲。你只需要確認那些真正影響行車安全的關鍵元件（剎車系統、電池過熱保護、方向盤轉向機構）都按規格安裝並正常運作。

CDE 就是這些「關鍵元件」的藥廠版本——只測試真正重要的，不做無意義的重複測試。

實務應用：CDMO 的 C&Q 效益

對 CDMO 而言，採用 ISPE C&Q 框架的直接商業效益：

  • 縮短驗證時間：FAT 廠驗數據可直接作為 IQ 證據，不需到廠重做
  • 降低成本：只聚焦 CDE，避免對非關鍵元件的過度測試
  • 加速新客戶引進：標準化的 URS → DQ → C&Q 流程，讓客戶稽查更順暢
  • 強化法規辯護性：System Risk Assessment 文件是 FDA 483 最佳防禦工具

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一台新型凍乾機的「擱板溫度均勻性」屬於 CA 還是 CDE？請說明你的分析邏輯。
  2. GEP（Good Engineering Practice）與 GMP 文件要求有何本質差異？ISPE 為何要特別強調 GEP 標準？
1.3 Scope（適用範圍）

原文內容 Original Text

This Guide applies to systems used by pharmaceutical manufacturers of human and veterinary drugs, including biological drug products.

Medical devices have separate regulatory requirements and are outside of the scope of this Guide. For combination devices, this Guide can be applied to the manufacturing equipment for the combination device, but not to the device itself.

The following areas are not in the scope of the C&Q process as described in this Guide:

  • Product and process development, including identification of any process requirements that influence system design
  • Computerized systems software development and testing (refer to ISPE GAMP® 5)
  • Process validation, including Process Performance Qualification (PPQ) and Continued/Ongoing Process Verification (refer to ISPE Good Practice Guide: Practical Implementation of the Lifecycle Approach to Process Validation)
  • Cleaning validation
  • Sanitization and sterilization validation
  • Analytical procedures and methods validation
  • Decommissioning activities (refer to ISPE Good Practice Guide: Decommissioning of Pharmaceutical Equipment and Facilities)

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：C&Q 的邊界劃定

本節最重要的學習是：C&Q 結束的地方，PPQ 才開始。

C&Q 確認的是「系統符合設計規格並適合使用」，而 PPQ（製程性能確認）確認的是「這個系統可以穩定生產出符合規格的產品」。兩者的對象不同：前者是「設備/系統」，後者是「製程/產品」。

重點提示：電腦系統軟體開發不在此範圍

軟體的 V&V（Validation & Verification）屬於 ISPE GAMP 5 的管轄範圍，而非本指引。這個邊界劃定非常重要——當你在確效一台 SCADA 系統時：

  • 硬體部分（感測器、閥門、控制盤安裝）→ ISPE Vol.5 C&Q
  • 軟體部分（控制邏輯、配方管理、稽核追蹤）→ GAMP 5

實務上兩者常需要整合規劃，避免重複測試或遺漏。

比喻說明：C&Q 是交屋驗屋，PPQ 是入住後的試住

C&Q 就像你買新房子時的「交屋驗屋」——確認水電、牆壁、窗戶都按圖施工且正常運作。

PPQ 則是「入住後連住三個月」，確認冬天不漏風、夏天不悶熱、每天用水都足夠。

兩者都必要，但性質完全不同，不能混為一談。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一個新藥品的製造廠正在引進用於生物製劑的單次使用生物反應器（SUB）。請列出哪些活動屬於 C&Q 範圍，哪些不屬於？
  2. 清潔驗證（Cleaning Validation）為何被排除在 C&Q 範圍外？這兩個活動的對象有何本質差異？
1.4 Process Overview and Structure of the Guide（流程概述與指引架構）

原文內容 Original Text

An overview of the integrated C&Q approach is shown in Figure 1.1 (Science and Risk-Based C&Q Process Map).

The inputs to the integrated C&Q process include product and process CQAs/CPPs (established through research and development and/or the technology transfer process) and the application of QRM to define the control strategy.

The steps in the integrated C&Q process are:

  • URS (Chapter 2)
  • System Classification (Chapter 3)
  • System Risk Assessment (Chapter 4)
  • DR/DQ (Chapter 5)
  • C&Q Planning (Chapter 6)
  • C&Q Testing and Documentation (Chapter 7)
  • Acceptance and Release (Chapter 8)
  • Periodic Review (Chapter 9)

Also included are support programs:

  • Vendor Assessment for C&Q Documentation Purposes (Chapter 10)
  • Engineering Quality Process (Chapter 11)
  • Change Management (Chapter 12)
  • Good Documentation Practices for C&Q (Chapter 13)
  • Strategies for Implementation (Chapter 14)

The process begins with the development of the URS. The next step is system classification — categorizing systems as direct impact or not direct impact. Direct impact systems are commissioned and qualified while systems that are not direct impact are commissioned only.

C&Q testing may include pre-delivery inspection, Factory Acceptance Testing (FAT), construction quality document verification, and Site Acceptance Testing (SAT). C&Q planning should identify aspects of the FAT and SAT that will be utilized to satisfy qualification requirements.

Completion of testing leads to acceptance and release, the last phase of C&Q. Systems then go through a Periodic Review to ensure they remain suitable for the intended purpose.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：整合式 C&Q 流程地圖解讀

整個 ISPE C&Q 流程是一個由需求驅動、風險聚焦、迭代執行的架構：

  • URS（第 2 章）→ 定義「我要什麼」
  • System Classification（第 3 章）→ 判斷「這個系統有多重要」
  • System Risk Assessment（第 4 章）→ 識別「什麼地方可能出錯」
  • DR/DQ（第 5 章）→ 確認「設計有沒有滿足需求」
  • C&Q Planning（第 6 章）→ 規劃「怎麼驗」
  • Testing（第 7-8 章）→ 執行驗證並放行
  • Periodic Review（第 9 章）→ 持續確保有效

重點提示：FAT 可作為 IQ 證據！

這是 ISPE Vol.5 最具實務價值的概念之一：在供應商工廠完成的 FAT（工廠驗收測試），可以直接作為 IQ（安裝確認）的部分證據，無需到廠重複測試。

但前提是：

  • FAT 在廠商有明確 QA 監督下執行
  • FAT 協議（protocol）按 C&Q 計畫的 GEP 要求撰寫
  • C&Q 計畫中明確記錄哪些 FAT 結果被接受作為確效證據

比喻說明：直接衝擊系統就像手術室設備

Direct Impact System（直接衝擊系統）：直接影響藥品品質的系統，如純水系統、滅菌釜、充填機。必須執行完整 Commissioning + Qualification。

Not Direct Impact System（非直接衝擊系統）：如辦公室空調、廠務用水管、照明系統。只需 Commissioning，不需 Qualification 文件。

就像醫院只有手術室才需要層流空調稽核，辦公室走廊的通風系統不需要同樣嚴格的驗收程序。

實務應用：整合 FAT/SAT 節省 30-50% 確效時間

CDMO 在規劃新設備導入時，如能在簽訂採購合約時就要求供應商依據 ISPE C&Q 框架撰寫 FAT 協議，並在 FAT 時派遣 QA 人員陪同，可將這些數據直接納入 IQ 報告。

實際案例顯示，與傳統做法相比（FAT 後到廠再做完整 IQ），此方法可節省 30-50% 的驗證工時，並顯著縮短設備啟動時程。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一台新採購的高效液相色層儀（HPLC），其安裝在 QC 實驗室，用於放行檢驗。它是 Direct Impact 還是 Not Direct Impact System？請說明判斷依據。
  2. 廠商在工廠完成了完整的 FAT，記錄了所有感測器的校正資料。如果你是確效工程師，你需要哪些條件才能接受這份 FAT 報告作為 IQ 的一部分？
1.5 Rationale for this Second Edition（第二版改版說明）

原文內容 Original Text

This Guide, the second edition of the ISPE Baseline® Guide: Commissioning and Qualification, has been designed to present industry best practices for C&Q. It also combines concepts from regulatory guidances (e.g., from EMA, FDA, ICH) and the following ISPE documents that are superseded with this revision:

  • ISPE Baseline® Guide: Volume 5 – Commissioning and Qualification (First Edition)
  • ISPE Guide: Science and Risk-Based Approach for the Delivery of Facilities, Systems, and Equipment
  • ISPE Good Practice Guide: Applied Risk Management for Commissioning and Qualification

Certain aspects of the C&Q approach described in the previous edition are retired and replaced:

  • Component Criticality Assessment — Since CDEs are identified as an output of the System Risk Assessment, assessment of the criticality of each system component is unnecessary.
  • Enhanced Commissioning — This Guide describes how the level of testing can be aligned with criticality and intended purpose of the system.
  • Enhanced Design Review — This Guide describes an approach for performing effective DRs using the System Risk Assessment to achieve DQ.
  • Enhanced Documentation — Good Documentation Practices are defined in the Guide.
  • Indirect Impact — The term is not used. The Guide describes C&Q for systems based on whether a system has direct product impact or not.
  • V-Model — The integrated C&Q approach provides a lifecycle C&Q approach and is represented by a different process map. The V-model appropriately represented the links between the design process and testing, but did not incorporate a risk assessment process based on product quality.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

核心概念：V-Model 的終結與新框架的誕生

V-Model（V 型模型）是 1990-2010 年代確效的黃金標準，將設計階段文件與測試階段文件對應成 V 字型：

  • URS ↔ PQ
  • Functional Spec ↔ OQ
  • Design Spec ↔ IQ

ISPE 第二版廢除 V-Model 的原因：V-Model 強調文件對應，但沒有整合「產品品質風險評估」，導致不關鍵的系統也做了大量確效測試，效率極低。

新框架以 QRM（品質風險管理）為核心，只對真正影響產品品質的 CDE 進行確效。

重點提示：「Indirect Impact」術語被廢除

第一版有三分類：Direct Impact / Indirect Impact / No Impact。第二版簡化為兩分類：Direct Impact / Not Direct Impact。

原因：「Indirect Impact」在實務上定義模糊，常造成確效工程師爭議——清潔用水算 Indirect 還是 Direct？廠房 HVAC 呢？

新分類更清晰：「有沒有直接影響產品品質？」只有兩個答案。

比喻說明：從「全身健康檢查」到「針對性精密檢查」

傳統 V-Model 確效就像每年做全身健康檢查：腦部、心臟、腸胃、骨質……每個器官都掃一遍，不管你有沒有症狀。費時費錢。

ISPE 新框架就像根據你的個人健康風險做針對性精密檢查：有心臟病家族史→重點檢查心臟；有糖尿病風險→重點監控血糖。其他沒有風險的部位，例行檢查就夠了。

這就是「Science and Risk-Based C&Q」的本質——聚焦真正的風險。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 你的公司目前用傳統 V-Model 進行確效，有一批老舊的 Legacy 系統（按第一版 ISPE 完成確效）。你的稽查員問：「這些系統需要按第二版重新確效嗎？」本節給了什麼指引？
  2. 為什麼廢除「Component Criticality Assessment（元件關鍵性評估）」能提升效率？請解釋 System Risk Assessment 如何取代它的功能。
1.6 Key Concepts（關鍵概念）

1.6.1 Efficient Approach without Redundant Testing

The foundation of this Guide is based on the expectation that engineers and system vendors ensure systems are installed and operate to meet the design specifications and user requirements. This is commonly referred to as commissioning. Best industry practice is to utilize such an approach when installing any new system.

When a system has direct impact on product quality (direct impact system), the CDEs of the system can be verified by the approach described in this Guide. This approach ensures that identified CPPs are maintained; CPPs ensure that CQAs are attained. Testing of system CDEs is utilized to support qualification of the system. Thus, the documentation of the testing performed in commissioning needs to be acceptable to be presented in a regulatory audit or inspection.

1.6.2 Terminology for Product Impacting Attributes

There is a recognition that critical utilities, such as Water for Injection (WFI) systems, may not have product CQAs but do have compendial requirements and CPPs. These parameters can directly influence the system's ability to deliver product meeting those attributes.

The authors continue to use the terminology of CPPs and CQAs for all systems, including WFI and upstream equipment. It is important for individual organizations/sites to define what is critical for their products, processes, and systems.

1.6.3 Quality Unit Oversight

The Quality Unit is expected to have oversight of the entire validation lifecycle including qualification. Because the Quality Unit is not expected to have expertise in all aspects of pharmaceutical manufacturing systems, identified SMEs (Subject Matter Experts) should be responsible for determining how best to design and test systems to ensure they are suitable for the intended purpose.

The Quality Unit needs to be engaged in the process, be considered part of the C&Q team, approve the appropriate testing plans and documents for systems that directly affect product quality, and approve the final acceptance of the qualified state. The authors see this as a Quality Assurance (QA) role, not a documentation quality control role.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

1.6.1 核心概念：Commissioning 文件 = 可提交稽查的品質文件

這是最容易被誤解的地方。許多工程師認為試車文件是「工程文件」，只要技術上正確就夠，不需要按 GMP 標準撰寫。

ISPE 的立場非常明確：當試車測試用來支持確效時，這些文件必須能接受法規稽查。意思是：

  • 數據必須真實、及時記錄（no backdating）
  • 偏差（Discrepancy）必須有記錄和處理
  • 簽核程序必須完整

工程師完成的試車報告品質直接決定確效效率——好的 FAT 報告可省掉大量重複測試。

1.6.2 重點提示：WFI 系統的 CPP 如何定義？

WFI 系統本身不直接生產藥品，但其輸出水質影響所有使用 WFI 的製程。因此：

  • WFI 的 CQA = WFI 的內毒素限值、導電度、TOC（這些是「中間品質屬性」）
  • WFI 的 CPP = 蒸餾溫度、循環流速、循環壓力
  • WFI 的 CDE = 溫度感測器精度、熱交換器完整性、迴路材質（316L 不鏽鋼）

理解這個延伸應用，有助於確效工程師在面對 utility 系統時不會束手無策。

1.6.3 核心概念：QA 是品質保證角色，不是文件審查機器

ISPE 特別強調：Quality Unit 的角色是 Quality Assurance（品質保證），不是 Documentation Quality Control（文件品管）。

實務意義：

  • QA 不需要逐字審查所有技術細節（那是 SME 的責任）
  • QA 需要確認 C&Q 計畫是否涵蓋了所有產品品質風險
  • QA 負責最終的放行決定，基於風險評估結果，不是基於文件厚度

這個觀念轉變對很多台灣 CDMO 的 QA 部門是重要的文化挑戰。

比喻說明：QA 是法官，SME 是鑑定人

法庭上，法官（QA）不需要自己做 DNA 鑑定，但必須評估鑑定人（SME）提交的報告是否可信、是否足夠支持裁決。

最終放行決定由法官（QA）做出，責任歸屬明確。鑑定人（SME）提供技術判斷，不應該被要求超出自己專業範圍之外。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 一個新的 CIP（就地清洗）系統正在完成 FAT，供應商提交了測試報告，但其中有 3 項偏差未按 ISPE GEP 標準記錄（只有口頭說明，無書面記錄）。作為確效工程師，你應如何處理？
  2. 你的 QA Director 說：「每一份確效報告我都要逐行審查才放心。」根據 ISPE 1.6.3 的精神，這種做法有何風險？應如何調整？
1.7 Key Terms（關鍵術語定義）

原文內容 Original Text

Term Definition
Acceptance Criteria "Measurable terms under which a test result may be considered acceptable" (WHO Annex 5)
Commissioning A well-planned, documented, and managed engineering approach to the start-up and turnover of facilities, systems, utilities, and equipment to the end-user that results in a safe and functional environment that meets established design requirements and stakeholder expectations.
Critical Aspects (CAs) "Functions, features, abilities, and performance or characteristics necessary for the manufacturing process and systems to ensure consistent product quality and patient safety." (ASTM E2500-13)
Critical Design Elements (CDEs) Design functions or features of an engineered system that are necessary to consistently manufacture products with the desired quality attributes. CDEs are identified and documented based on technical understanding of the product CQAs, process CPPs, and equipment design/automation. CDEs are verified through C&Q.
Critical Process Parameter (CPP) "A process parameter whose variability has an impact on a critical quality attribute and therefore should be monitored or controlled to ensure the process produces the desired quality." (ICH Q8)
Critical Quality Attribute (CQA) "A physical, chemical, biological or microbiological property or characteristic that should be within an appropriate limit, range, or distribution to ensure the desired product quality." (ICH Q8)
Design Qualification (DQ) A documented process that verifies the proposed design of the facilities, systems, utilities, and equipment is suitable for the intended purpose.
Design Review (DR) "Formal, documented, comprehensive, and systematic examination of a design to determine if the design meets the applicable requirements, to identify problems, and to propose solutions." (ISO/IEC/IEEE 24765)
Deviation A departure from specification, or a critical discrepancy that cannot be corrected, that affects a CA/CDE. Deviations require Quality Unit approval prior to closure.
Direct Impact System A system that directly impacts product CQAs, or directly impacts the quality of the product delivered by a critical utility system. All other systems are considered to be not direct impact.
Discrepancy "Datum or result outside of the expected range; an unfulfilled requirement; may be called non-conformity, defect, deviation, out-of-specification, out-of-limit, out-of-trend." (FDA 2006 Quality Systems Guidance)
Installation Qualification (IQ) A documented process that verifies that the facilities, systems, utilities, and equipment, as installed or modified, comply with the approved design and the manufacturer's recommendations.
Operational Qualification (OQ) A documented process that verifies that the facilities, systems, utilities, and equipment, as installed or modified, perform as intended throughout the anticipated operating ranges.
Performance Qualification (PQ) A documented process that verifies that the facilities, systems, utilities, and equipment, as connected together, can perform effectively and reproducibly, based on the approved process method and product specification.
Qualification A process to demonstrate and document that the critical manufacturing facilities, systems, utilities, and equipment are suitable for the intended purpose.
Quality Risk Management (QRM) "A systematic process for the assessment, control, communication and review of risks to the quality of the drug (medicinal) product across the product lifecycle." (ICH Q9)
Suitable for the Intended Purpose The system requirements are defined, the design is appropriate for control of the manufacturing process, and the system is fabricated and installed as designed, and performs as intended throughout the anticipated operating ranges.
Verification An activity that is performed within the C&Q process to document that the manufacturing facilities, systems, utilities, and equipment are suitable for the intended purpose.

導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

術語辨析：IQ / OQ / PQ 與 C&Q 的關係

ISPE 第二版保留了 IQ/OQ/PQ 的定義，但在實際執行上，它們是 C&Q 過程的輸出文件，而非獨立步驟。

傳統思維：先做 IQ → 再做 OQ → 再做 PQ（三段式串列）
ISPE 新思維：FAT、SAT、現場測試按邏輯規劃，IQ/OQ/PQ 文件是這些測試的結果整理，不是強制的執行順序。

重點提示：Deviation vs. Discrepancy 的關鍵差異

Discrepancy（偏差事項）：任何不符合預期的結果，可以是輕微的，可能可以直接修正。

Deviation（確效偏差）：ISPE 特別定義為「影響 CA/CDE 的嚴重差異，且無法直接修正」——必須獲得 Quality Unit 批准才能關閉。

在確效報告中混用這兩個術語是常見錯誤，容易在稽查時引發不必要的問題。

術語速查表（繁體中文對照）

C&Q       = 試車與確效（Commissioning and Qualification）
CDE       = 關鍵設計要素（Critical Design Element）
CA        = 關鍵特性（Critical Aspect）
CPP       = 關鍵製程參數（Critical Process Parameter）
CQA       = 關鍵品質屬性（Critical Quality Attribute）
DQ        = 設計確認（Design Qualification）
DR        = 設計審查（Design Review）
FAT       = 工廠驗收測試（Factory Acceptance Testing）
SAT       = 現場驗收測試（Site Acceptance Testing）
IQ        = 安裝確認（Installation Qualification）
OQ        = 操作確認（Operational Qualification）
PQ        = 性能確認（Performance Qualification）
QRM       = 品質風險管理（Quality Risk Management）
SME       = 主題專家（Subject Matter Expert）
URS       = 使用者需求規格（User Requirements Specification）
GEP       = 良好工程規範（Good Engineering Practice）

實務應用：如何在稽查中使用這些定義

當 FDA 查員詢問：「你們如何定義 Direct Impact System？」，最佳回答方式：

  1. 引用 ISPE Vol.5 2nd Ed. 的定義（直接影響產品 CQA 的系統）
  2. 展示你們的 System Classification 工具表（第 3 章）
  3. 說明哪些系統被分類為 Direct Impact，以及判斷依據

事先建立一份系統分類清冊，在每次稽查前更新，可大幅提升稽查效率。

練習思考 Practice Questions

  1. 請將以下系統分類為 Direct Impact 或 Not Direct Impact，並說明理由：(a) 注射用水系統 (b) 廠房壓差監控系統 (c) 無菌室 HVAC (d) 辦公室中央空調 (e) 自動化充填機 PLC
  2. 一台滅菌釜在 PQ 測試中，某個循環的最冷點溫度為 120.8°C（規格 ≥121°C），屬於 Discrepancy 還是 Deviation？這份文件應如何處理？

本章重點回顧 Section Summary

  • C&Q 的核心定義：Commissioning（工程試車）+ Qualification（品質確效）整合為一個科學與風險驅動的流程，核心差異在於 Quality Unit 的參與
  • CDE 是確效的聚焦點：透過 QRM → CQA → CPP → CA → CDE 的層級識別，確保只對真正重要的系統特性進行確效測試
  • 第二版主要改版：廢除 V-Model、廢除「Indirect Impact」分類、廢除 Component Criticality Assessment，以 QRM 整合為核心
  • FAT 可作為確效證據：供應商工廠完成的測試在 GEP 標準下可直接作為 IQ 文件，避免重複測試，縮短確效週期
  • QA 的角色定位：QA 是品質保證的最終決策者，不是文件逐字審查員；SME 負責技術判斷，QA 負責風險評估與放行批准
  • 關鍵術語必記：CDE、CA、Deviation vs. Discrepancy、Direct Impact System 的精確定義是法規稽查時的必備知識
2-3

Chapter 2-3: URS & System Classification

使用者需求規格與系統分類 | p19-p26

ISPE Baseline® Guide Vol.5 — Commissioning and Qualification (2nd Edition)

Chapter 2: User Requirements Specification & Chapter 3: System Classification
第二章：使用者需求規格 & 第三章：系統分類
Pages 19–26  |  ISPE 2019

本節學習目標 Learning Objectives

  1. 說明 URS（使用者需求規格）在 C&Q 流程中的角色，以及它與 CQA、CPP、系統風險評估的關聯。
  2. 區分 URS「應包含」與「不應包含」的內容，並能辨識常見的錯誤寫法。
  3. 理解 URS 核准流程、變更管理要求，以及遺留系統（Legacy Systems）的處置方式。
  4. 解釋「直接衝擊系統」與「非直接衝擊系統」兩類分類方式，並說明為何舊版元件分類已被系統風險評估取代。
  5. 應用 Table 3.1 八個判定問題（Q1–Q8）對給定系統進行分類判斷。

Chapter 2 — User Requirements Specification (URS)

第二章：使用者需求規格  |  pp. 19–22

2.1 Introduction

The User Requirements Specification (URS) brings together system requirements from multidisciplinary sources to support system design, C&Q, operations, and maintenance. Within the C&Q process, it is a foundational document that identifies the product and process requirements for the system. These product quality related user requirements are based on product knowledge (CQAs), process knowledge (CPPs), regulatory requirements, and organization/site quality requirements. The product and process requirements in the URS are inputs to the C&Q process; they provide the science-based knowledge that forms the basis for applying QRM to C&Q.

It is recommended that a URS is developed for each system that has the potential to impact product quality, or a direct impact system (as determined through system classification described in Chapter 3). A formal URS document is not always necessary. A statement of the URS may be contained in various forms, e.g., purchase request, functional specification, change request, or data sheet. For standard off-the-shelf or simple catalog systems, a statement of the URS may be a purchase order, vendor cut sheet, or catalog data. The system would be verified against this document.

Figure 2.1 shows the relationship between the activities and documents in the C&Q process for direct impact systems.

Figure 2.1: Relational Diagram for C&Q Activities and Documents – User Requirements Specification

中文解析 Commentary

核心概念：URS 是什麼？

URS（使用者需求規格）是整個 C&Q 流程的起點文件，由多學科團隊共同制定，整合來自品質、工程、法規、HSE 等各方面的系統需求。

  • CQAs（關鍵品質屬性）→ 來自產品知識，定義最終產品必須符合的品質標準
  • CPPs（關鍵製程參數）→ 來自製程知識，定義必須被控制的製程變數
  • QRM（品質風險管理）→ URS 提供科學依據，使風險評估有所根據

URS 的核心價值：它告訴系統「要做什麼」，而不是「怎麼做」。

日常比喻：蓋房子的需求清單

URS 就像屋主委託建築師前寫的需求清單：「我需要 4 個臥室、2 個浴室、開放式廚房、無障礙坡道」。這份清單說明要什麼，但不說「牆要用哪種磚」或「水管要走哪條路」——那是設計師的事（Basis of Design, BOD）。

重點提示：URS 不一定要是獨立文件

對於標準現貨品或簡單設備，URS 可以是：採購申請單、廠商型錄頁、功能規格書、或變更申請單。重要的是：系統最終必須對照該文件進行驗證。

思考練習

Q1：一家製藥廠採購一台新型生物反應器，URS 應該由哪些部門的人共同制定？各部門應提供哪類需求？

Q2：為什麼 ISPE 說 URS 是「C&Q 流程的基礎文件」？如果沒有 URS，會對後續的 FAT、IQ、OQ 造成什麼影響？

2.2

2.2 Development of the User Requirements Specification

URS 的制定方法  |  pp. 20–22

2.2 Development of the User Requirements Specification

The URS defines the requirements that must be met for a system to be suitable for the intended purpose; it should not detail how those requirements are met. The URS is developed by a project team that includes SMEs (refer to Section 6.4 for an example approval matrix). It can be revised throughout the system lifecycle.

The URS document SHOULD include:

  • Describe the intended purpose of the system
  • State the requirements in verifiable terms without describing how the requirements will be met
  • State the category and source of each requirement
    • Categories may include, for example:
      • Quality
      • Business
      • Health, Safety, and Environmental (HSE)
    • Sources may include, for example:
      • Product and process requirements derived from:
        • Product and process knowledge (CQAs, CPPs, CAs)
        • GMP regulatory requirements
        • Organization/site quality requirements
      • System Risk Assessment (includes CAs and associated CDEs)
      • Range and accuracy for any controlled parameters
      • National, local and site requirements, as applicable
      • Business, HSE, system owner, and SME requirements
      • Engineering specifications and industry standards (e.g., ASME, ASTM, ISO)
      • Project requirements document or project charter
      • Legacy system evaluations

The URS should also include the following:

  • Data integrity requirements
  • Data storage/display requirements
  • Alarm requirements, with identification of the critical alarms
  • System automation requirements
    • If there are any connections (e.g., data archiving) and interactions (e.g., alarm initiation) to a larger automation control system, then that system can have a separate URS. There needs to be clearly defined boundaries between the systems.
Note: System software development and testing is outside of the scope of this Guide. Refer to ISPE GAMP® 5: A Risk-Based Approach to Compliant GxP Computerized Systems.

The URS, which may be further detailed during early project phases, provides the foundation for the Basis of Design (BOD) and becomes a reference used to establish that a system is suitable for the intended purpose. To be suitable for the intended purpose, systems need to meet their URS.

The URS should NOT include the following information as requirements:

  • How a requirement is to be met
  • Detailed design specifications
  • Sequence of operations
  • Generic statements (e.g., must comply with local codes, must meet all GxPs)
  • General references to government/national standards (e.g., nonspecific reference to ASME code, ISO standards)
  • Contractual terms and deliverables
  • Unverifiable parameters
  • Standard functionality of the equipment type

Refer to Chapter 16 (Appendix 2) for an example URS template. It is the responsibility of the organization/site to designate quality impacting elements of their URS in a manner that is most appropriate for their integrated C&Q process.

中文解析 Commentary

核心概念：URS 的三類需求分類

每條需求都應標明類別（Category）與來源（Source）：

  • 品質（Quality）：與 GMP 法規、CQA、CPP 相關的要求
  • 商業（Business）：產能、效率、成本相關要求
  • HSE：健康、安全、環境相關要求

來源標註的重要性：若 QU（品質單位）已核准 CQA/CPP 來源文件，則 URS 可不需 QU 再次核准（見 2.3 節）。

核心概念：CDE 與 CA 是什麼？

CA（關鍵特性, Critical Attribute）：系統的關鍵性質或特徵，若偏離可能影響產品品質。

CDE（關鍵設計要素, Critical Design Element）：系統中用來控制或達到 CA 的具體設計元素。來自系統風險評估（SRA）。

URS 應引用 SRA 的輸出結果（包含 CA 和相關 CDE），確保設計要求有科學風險依據。

重要對比：URS 應包含 vs. 不應包含

應包含 (SHOULD) 不應包含 (SHOULD NOT)
「純水系統出口電導率應 ≤ 1.3 μS/cm」 「純水系統應使用 RO + EDI + 迴流設計」
「CIP 溫度應達到 80°C 並維持 30 分鐘」 「CIP 應符合 GxP 要求」（過於通用）
「壓縮空氣含油量應 ≤ 0.01 mg/m³」 「壓縮空氣應符合 ISO 8573 標準」（無指定等級）
「系統應具備 21 CFR Part 11 稽核追蹤功能」 「操作順序：步驟一、步驟二…」

關鍵原則：URS 說「要什麼結果」，不說「怎麼達到」。

日常比喻：餐廳點餐 vs. 廚房食譜

URS 是顧客的點餐單：「我要一份不加洋蔥、熟度五分的牛排」——這是需求，是可驗證的。廚師如何備料、用什麼鍋、醃幾分鐘，那是廚房的設計規格（DS），不屬於 URS。把「使用鑄鐵鍋煎」寫進顧客點餐單，就是混淆了 URS 與 DS 的邊界。

CDMO 實務應用：制定 URS 的挑戰

在 CDMO（委託開發製造服務）環境中，URS 制定特別複雜，因為：

  • 客戶知識不足：客戶可能對自己產品的 CPP 尚未完全確立（早期臨床階段），URS 需預留彈性。
  • 多產品共用設備：同一系統服務多個客戶的不同分子，URS 需涵蓋最嚴格的需求（worst case）。
  • 資訊保密：客戶 CQA/CPP 屬商業機密，CDMO 需在 NDA 架構下取得足夠資訊以寫出正確 URS。
  • 實務建議：建立標準 URS 範本（含品質需求主清單），再依各客戶/產品需求調整，可大幅提升效率並確保一致性。

思考練習

Q1：以下哪些屬於合格的 URS 需求，哪些不符合規定？（a）「滅菌釜內腔溫度均一性應在設定點 ±1°C 以內」；（b）「滅菌釜應採用重力排氣式設計」；（c）「必須符合所有適用法規」；（d）「SIP 溫度 122°C 應維持至少 30 分鐘」。

Q2：軟體與電腦化系統的開發和測試為何不在本指南範圍內？應參考哪份文件？這對 URS 的撰寫有何影響？

2.3

2.3 Approval of URS and Changes Post-Approval

URS 的核准與核准後變更  |  p. 22

2.3 Approval of User Requirements Specification and Changes Post-Approval

The URS should be approved by the system owner, an appropriate SME, and the Quality Unit. However, if the Quality Unit has already approved the source documents from which the quality requirements within the URS were obtained, then the Quality Unit does not need to approve the URS. Refer to Section 6.4 for an example document approval matrix.

The URS should be updated through the system lifecycle (from development through sustaining operations) until decommissioning of the system. After approval of the URS, changes or additions with the potential to impact product quality are evaluated against the System Risk Assessment (refer to Chapter 4) to confirm if risks are acceptable or to determine if additional risk controls are required. Changes to the URS are performed through change management (refer to Chapter 12).

中文解析 Commentary

核心概念：URS 的核准機制

URS 通常需要三方簽核：

  • 系統擁有者（System Owner）：通常是工程或製造部門主管，對系統的商業和技術需求負責
  • SME（主題專家）：視系統類型，可能是製程工程師、設備工程師、自動化工程師等
  • Quality Unit（品質單位）：確認品質需求已被正確納入

例外條款：若 QU 已核准 CQA/CPP 等來源文件（例如製程描述文件），則 URS 可免 QU 核准。這是風險比例原則的體現。

重點提示：URS 是活文件

URS 在系統整個生命週期中都應保持更新，直到系統退役（Decommissioning）。核准後若有變更：

  • 凡可能影響產品品質的變更 → 須透過系統風險評估（SRA）評估影響
  • 所有變更 → 須走變更管理（Change Management）流程（見 Chapter 12）

這確保 URS 始終反映系統的實際設計意圖，並與 QRM 掛鉤。

思考練習

Q1：一個純水系統在商業生產兩年後，業主希望將產水量從 500 L/hr 提升至 800 L/hr。這個變更是否需要更新 URS？應走哪些流程？

Q2：何種情況下，QU 可以不需要核准 URS？這個例外條款的設計意圖是什麼？

2.4

2.4 Legacy Systems

遺留系統的處理  |  p. 22

2.4 Legacy Systems

For a legacy system without a documented URS, a URS for any scope changes may be developed and incorporated into the C&Q Plan (see Chapter 6) or change record.

Based on the magnitude of the change and the extent of the C&Q required, it may be beneficial to create a new URS. Refer to Chapter 14 for implementation recommendations.

中文解析 Commentary

核心概念：Legacy System（遺留系統）的定義與挑戰

遺留系統是指在本指南方法論建立之前就已運行、且缺乏完整 C&Q 文件（包括 URS）的既有系統。常見情境：

  • 工廠收購或合併時繼承的設備
  • 舊版指南（如第一版 ISPE Vol.5）時期安裝的系統
  • 當時認為不需要正式文件的系統，後來被重新分類為 Direct Impact

處理原則：不需要補全所有歷史文件，但針對任何範圍變更，應制定對應的 URS，並納入 C&Q Plan 或變更記錄中。

日常比喻：老屋翻新的設計圖

遺留系統就像一棟沒有原始建築圖紙的老房子。你不需要重新繪製整棟房子的圖，但如果你要加蓋一間房間（範圍變更），就必須為那個新的部分畫設計圖，並且確保它符合現行建築法規（當前 GMP 要求）。

重點提示：何時應建立全新 URS？

若變更規模很大（例如：系統全面升級、從批次改為連續製程），建立一份全新的 URS 往往比在舊文件上修改更有效率、也更清晰。詳見 Chapter 14（實施建議）。

思考練習

Q1：一家公司於 2008 年安裝了一套純蒸汽系統，當時沒有制定 URS。現在要更換熱交換器並新增一個使用點，應如何處理 URS 文件？

Q2：遺留系統的重新評估應參考本指南哪個章節？決定是否建立全新 URS 的關鍵因素是什麼？

3

Chapter 3 — System Classification

第三章：系統分類  |  pp. 23–26

3.1 Introduction

This Guide presents an approach for classifying systems into two categories depending on the system capability to impact product quality. System classification establishes whether a system is commissioned and qualified or only commissioned, as follows:

  • Direct impact systems are commissioned and qualified
  • Not direct impact systems are commissioned
Note: In the previous edition of this Baseline® Guide, component classification could be carried out as a subset of system classification. Component classification is no longer necessary since the System Risk Assessment (as described in Chapter 4) identifies CDEs for the system in a more efficient manner.

For systems that are not direct impact, the scope of commissioning is determined by SMEs and is based on the business and HSE criticality of the system. For example, a chilled water system serving an administrative building (not direct impact) may be balanced only. Meanwhile, a chilled water system (not direct impact) serving direct impact process equipment may be balanced, with the balancing confirmed at the minimum and maximum design flow rates to ensure reliable system performance during operation.

中文解析 Commentary

核心概念：兩類系統分類

ISPE Vol.5 第二版將系統分為兩類（取代舊版的三類）：

分類 英文 C&Q 要求
直接衝擊系統 Direct Impact System 試車（C）+ 確效（Q）
非直接衝擊系統 Not Direct Impact System 僅試車（C）

這個二分法的核心問題是：「這個系統的故障是否直接影響最終產品品質或病人安全？」

重要變更：元件分類（Component Classification）已廢除

舊版（第一版）ISPE Vol.5 允許在系統分類之後，進一步對系統內的元件進行分類（Critical / Non-critical）。

第二版已取消此做法，理由是：系統風險評估（SRA，第四章）以更有效率的方式識別出 CDE（關鍵設計要素），直接替代了元件分類的功能。

換言之：SRA 做得更細、更有科學依據，不需要再額外做元件分類這個中間步驟。

日常比喻：機場管制 vs. 停車場

機場的跑道燈光系統（直接影響飛機起降安全）= Direct Impact，需要嚴格的試車 + 確效。機場停車場的照明系統（不影響飛機安全）= Not Direct Impact，只需要基本試車（燈能亮就好）。兩者都是「燈光系統」，但因衝擊程度不同，監管要求完全不同。

思考練習

Q1：一套服務注射劑填充間的 HVAC 系統，與一套服務倉庫的 HVAC 系統，分類結果會相同嗎？為什麼？

Q2：為什麼 ISPE 第二版取消了元件分類？SRA（系統風險評估）如何替代了這個功能？

3.2

3.2 System Boundaries

系統邊界的定義  |  pp. 23–24

3.2 System Boundaries

Projects are commonly divided up into systems to facilitate construction management, document collation, turnover, and C&Q. System boundaries are markings on design drawings to distinguish systems from one another; this includes all components and piping to logically define what is included and what is not included within the system. System boundaries should be defined and documented early on in the project (at the BOD phase) to enable development of the systems list and subsequent execution of System Risk Assessments. The systems are usually listed in the C&Q Plan (refer to Chapter 6). System boundaries should be defined such that the systems cover the entirety of the project scope; this is typically documented in the system Process and Instrumentation Diagram (P&ID) or Process Flow Diagram (PFD).

The scope of supply from vendors is often used as the basis for defining system boundaries; however, these boundaries should be carefully reviewed as there may be benefits in defining the boundaries differently. For example, boundary considerations for a direct impact compressed air system are as follows:

  • A Point of Use (POU) filter is typically outside the vendor scope of supply for a compressed air system but may or may not be included in the system boundaries.
  • The POU filter could be included within the boundaries for the compressed air distribution system. All compressed air testing and verification activities would be part of the compressed air system.
  • Alternatively, the POU filter could be included in the process system for which the air is being supplied to. All compressed air testing and verification activities for the POU filter would then be part of the process system.

During the early stages of a project, system boundaries may also be subdivided to facilitate development of C&Q documentation by different suppliers. For example, the URS for a compressed air system can include generation and distribution sections, each of which may have its own set of C&Q documentation.

The optimum approach for the project should be evaluated and then defined in the C&Q Plan. In the compressed air system example discussed earlier, it may be simpler to provide a URS/C&Q package for the generation system from one supplier and a separate URS/C&Q package for the storage and distribution system that is built on-site by a separate supplier.

Regardless of the C&Q documentation strategy, systems need to meet their URS.

中文解析 Commentary

核心概念：系統邊界的定義

系統邊界（System Boundaries）是在設計圖（P&ID 或 PFD）上標示的範圍，明確界定：

  • 哪些設備、管道、儀表屬於這個系統（included）
  • 哪些不屬於這個系統（excluded）

邊界應在 BOD（設計基準）階段就定義清楚，並列入 C&Q Plan 的系統清單中。

邊界定義直接影響：

  • 系統風險評估的範圍
  • IQ/OQ 測試的範圍
  • 文件整包（C&Q package）的責任歸屬

核心概念：P&ID 與 PFD 的差異

P&ID（管道與儀表圖）：顯示所有管道、儀表、控制閥、設備連接關係，是系統邊界標示的主要圖面，細節程度高。

PFD（製程流程圖）：顯示物料流向與主要設備，較概念性，用於早期設計階段。

系統邊界通常以雲線（cloud/bubble）或邊界線標示在 P&ID 上。

日常比喻：POU 過濾器的歸屬問題

壓縮空氣末端使用點（POU）過濾器就像公寓大樓的電錶：它可以屬於「大樓公共系統」，也可以屬於「個別住戶系統」——兩種做法都合理，但必須明確選擇一種，不能模糊。ISPE 的核心訊息：邊界怎麼劃不是最重要的，重要的是必須清楚說明並記錄在 C&Q Plan 中。

實務警示：廠商供貨範圍 ≠ 系統邊界

很多工程師直接用廠商的供貨範圍（Vendor Scope of Supply）當系統邊界，這可能造成問題：

  • POU 過濾器、管道接頭、控制面板等可能落在供貨範圍之外，但功能上屬於同一系統
  • 若邊界定義不清，驗證文件會出現「空白地帶」——沒有人負責的設備

建議：以功能完整性為原則定義邊界，再對照廠商供貨範圍調整。

CDMO 實務應用：多供應商系統的邊界管理

在 CDMO 新建廠或擴建案中，壓縮空氣系統往往由多個供應商分段建造（主機組 + 廠內管路 + POU 過濾器）。建議做法：

  • 在 C&Q Plan 中明確列出每個子系統的邊界，並標示在 P&ID 上
  • 若分拆為多個 URS/C&Q 包，確保各包的邊界相接處有明確的交接驗證要求
  • 主系統 URS 中應說明各子系統 URS 的關係（例如：「壓縮空氣主機組 URS 見 DOC-001，配氣管路 URS 見 DOC-002」）
  • 無論如何分拆，所有系統最終都必須符合其 URS

思考練習

Q1：一個注射用水（WFI）系統的 P&ID 應在哪個設計階段被定義出系統邊界？邊界劃定後應記錄在哪份文件中？

Q2：若 WFI 系統的 POU 取水點被劃入製程設備系統邊界，而非 WFI 分配系統邊界，會對 IQ/OQ 測試產生什麼影響？哪種做法更合理？

3.3

3.3 Criteria for System Classification — Table 3.1 (Q1–Q8)

系統分類判定標準  |  pp. 24–26

3.3 Criteria for System Classification

This Guide presents criteria for system classification that consist of eight questions; a YES response to at least one question indicates that the system is a direct impact system. Table 3.1 lists the questions that can be used to determine system classification for a given system.

These criteria should be used to inform a judgment based on a comprehensive understanding of the product, process, and the nature of the system. They should not be used to replace the exercise of informed judgment by appropriately qualified personnel.

Table 3.1: Criteria for System Classification

No. Question Additional Information
Q1 Does the system contain CAs/CDEs or perform functions that serve to meet one or more process requirements (CQAs) including CPPs?
  • There are two inputs to this question: product and process knowledge (CQAs and CPPs)
  • If the system controls or monitors a CPP, then the answer to this question should be a YES
Q2 Does the system have direct contact with the product or process stream and does such contact have the potential to impact the final product quality or pose a risk to the patient?
  • Risk factors to consider:
    • GMP requirement that product contact materials are non-reactive, non-additive, and non-absorptive such that the safety, identity, strength, quality, or purity of the drug product is not affected
    • Whether the materials that contact the manufacturing process can corrode and impart corrosion products into the manufacturing process
  • If any of these risk factors is an inherent part of the system, then the answer to this question should be a YES
Q3 Does the system provide an excipient or produce an ingredient or solvent (e.g., WFI) and could the quality (and compliance with the required specifications thereof) of this substance impact the final product quality or pose a risk to the patient?
  • Risk factors to consider:
    • Whether the excipient, ingredient, or solvent needs to be of defined requirements in order to produce a quality product
    • Whether the excipient, ingredient, or solvent can introduce excipients into the process stream (e.g., microbial contamination, corrosion products, residues from improper cleaning of the system)
  • If any of these risk factors is an inherent part of the system, then the answer to this question should be a YES
Q4 Is the system used in cleaning, sanitizing, or sterilizing, and could malfunction of the system result in failure to adequately clean, sanitize, or sterilize such that a risk to the patient would result?
  • Risk factors to consider:
    • Whether proper functioning of cleaning, sanitizing, and sterilizing systems is critical to product quality (YES in most cases)
    • Whether the quality of the substance used to perform the cleaning, sanitizing, or sterilizing (e.g., WFI, purified water, pure steam, cleaning or sterilizing chemicals):
      • Imparts any impurities to the process equipment
      • Impacts the effectiveness and repeatability of the cleaning, sanitizing, or sterilizing process
  • If any of these risk factors is an inherent part of the system, then the answer to this question should be a YES
Q5 Does the system establish a proper environment (e.g., nitrogen blanket, closed process, exposed filling zone air quality, maintenance of temperature, humidity when such parameter is part of the product CPPs) for the process and could failure of the system to function properly pose a risk to the patient?
  • At different stages of a process, there may be requirements for a controlled temperature, humidity, aseptic, oxygen-free, or pressurized environment; systems that provide this environment (including providing sterile air, unidirectional flow/HEPA filtered air in a clean room or nitrogen that contacts a process stream) would fall into this category
  • If failure of the system to function properly or to provide the required environment of requisite quality means that a risk to product quality exists, then the answer to this question should be a YES
Q6 Does the system use, produce, process, or store data used to accept or reject product, CPPs, or electronic records subject to 21 CFR Part 11 and EU GMP Vol. 4, Annex 11 or the local equivalent?
  • This criterion is aimed at firmware, software, PLC, SCADA, PCS, BAS, networks, spreadsheets, and databases
Q7 Does the system provide container closure or product protection, the failure of which would pose a risk to the patient or degradation of product quality?
  • Risk factors to consider:
    • Whether the system provides the closure or seal
    • Whether the system controls or provides the outside environment during shipping or product movement
  • If any of these risk factors is an inherent part of the system, then the answer to this question should be a YES
Q8 Does the system provide product identification information (e.g., lot number, expiration date, counterfeit prevention features) without independent verification or is the system used to verify this information?
  • Risk factors to consider:
    • Whether any packaging components, if compromised, would lead to an impact on product quality or identity
    • Systems that perform operations such as label verification of lot number/expiration date and proper packaging insert
  • If any of these risk factors is an inherent part of the system, then the answer to this question should be a YES

Note: BAS, Building Automation System; PCS, Process Control System; PLC, Programmable Logic Controller; SCADA, Supervisory Control and Data Acquisition.

Refer to Chapter 17 (Appendix 3) for an example system classification form. Refer to Chapter 18 (Appendix 4) for an example list of direct impact systems with typical CQAs and CPPs.

中文解析 Commentary

核心概念：Q1–Q8 分類邏輯

判定規則：任一題答「是（YES）」→ 直接衝擊系統（Direct Impact）。全部答「否（NO）」→ 非直接衝擊系統（Not Direct Impact）。

八個問題涵蓋的風險維度：

  • Q1：系統功能是否控制/監測 CQA 或 CPP？（功能關聯）
  • Q2：系統與產品或製程物流是否直接接觸？（接觸污染）
  • Q3：系統是否產製輔料、原料或溶劑？（供給品質）
  • Q4：系統是否用於清潔/消毒/滅菌？（清潔完整性）
  • Q5：系統是否建立受控環境？（環境控制）
  • Q6：系統是否處理用於放行判定的資料？（數據完整性）
  • Q7：系統是否提供容器密封或產品保護？（包裝完整性）
  • Q8：系統是否提供或驗證產品身分資訊？（產品標識）

Q1–Q8 實例對照：常見系統的分類

系統主要觸發問題分類
注射用水（WFI）系統Q3（製造溶劑）、Q2Direct Impact
SIP / 純蒸汽系統Q4（滅菌）、Q3Direct Impact
填充間 HVAC（A/B 級）Q5（環境控制）Direct Impact
CIP 系統Q4（清潔）、Q3Direct Impact
SCADA/PLC（製程控制）Q6（數據）、Q1Direct Impact
西林瓶封蓋機Q7（容器密封）Direct Impact
標籤驗證系統Q8（產品標識）Direct Impact
行政大樓冷凍水系統全部為 NONot Direct Impact
廠務純水（工業用）視用途而定需個案判斷

重點提示：分類須依賴專業判斷

ISPE 明確聲明：Q1–Q8 是「輔助判斷的工具」，而非「機械式清單」。分類必須基於對產品、製程、系統本質的全面理解。

例如：同樣是冷凍水系統，服務行政大樓 → Not Direct Impact；服務生物反應器冷卻套管 → 需評估 Q1（CPP 溫度控制）→ 可能是 Direct Impact。

分類應由「具備適當資格的人員」執行——不能只靠工程師，必須有品質與製程專家參與。

日常比喻：醫院分診八問

Q1–Q8 就像急診室的分診問卷：護士依序問「有沒有胸痛？有沒有呼吸困難？有沒有昏迷？」——只要任一項「有」，就進急救室（= Direct Impact，需完整 C&Q）。全部「沒有」，才能去普通候診區（= Not Direct Impact，只需試車）。分診問卷是輔助工具，最終還是需要醫師判斷。

CDMO 實務應用：系統分類工作坊

在 CDMO 新建廠案中，系統分類通常透過跨部門工作坊進行：

  • 參與者：工程（設計）、製程開發、品質、法規事務、HSE
  • 工具：系統清單（Systems List）+ 分類表（Chapter 17 範本）+ P&ID
  • 流程：逐一對每個系統回答 Q1–Q8，記錄判定依據（特別是 YES 的原因）
  • 常見挑戰：
    • 壓縮空氣系統：工廠壓縮空氣（Not DI）vs. 製程壓縮空氣（DI）— 邊界劃分至關重要
    • HVAC：依區域等級不同，同一建築內可能有 DI 和 Non-DI 系統並存
    • BMS/SCADA：Q6 的觸發點是「用於放行判定的數據」，需確認數據流向
  • 文件輸出：系統分類紀錄，連同 Q&A 依據，存入 C&Q Plan 附件

思考練習

Q1：一套氮氣保護系統（在原料藥結晶槽上方提供氮氣保護，防止氧化），應對 Q1–Q8 哪幾個問題回答「YES」？最終分類為何？請說明理由。

Q2：一套倉庫溫濕度監控系統（監測成品儲存條件，數據用於批次放行決策），主要觸發哪個問題（Q1–Q8）？這與一般倉庫空調系統有何本質差異？

本節重點摘要 Section Summary

  • URS 是 C&Q 的基礎文件，整合 CQA、CPP、法規要求與組織品質需求，說明系統「要做什麼」而非「怎麼做」。
  • URS 應包含：意圖目的、可驗證需求、類別與來源標示（品質/商業/HSE）、數據完整性、關鍵警報等；不應包含：設計規格、操作順序、通用聲明、不可驗證參數。
  • URS 須由系統擁有者、SME 及品質單位核准，並在系統整個生命週期中維持更新；變更須走 SRA 評估與變更管理流程。
  • 遺留系統若無原始 URS，應針對任何範圍變更制定 URS，並納入 C&Q Plan 或變更記錄。
  • 系統分類採用兩類制：直接衝擊系統（C+Q）vs. 非直接衝擊系統（C only）；第二版已廢除元件分類，由 SRA 替代。
  • 系統邊界應在 BOD 階段定義，記錄於 P&ID/PFD，並列入 C&Q Plan；廠商供貨範圍不等於系統邊界。
  • Q1–Q8 提供系統分類的判定架構：任一題 YES → Direct Impact；須結合專業判斷，不能機械式套用。

4

Chapter 4: System Risk Assessment

系統風陽評估 | p27-p34

ISPE Baseline® Guide Vol.5: Commissioning and Qualification (2nd Edition)

Chapter 4: System Risk Assessment ／ 系統風險評估
Pages 27–34  |  Sections 4.1 – 4.4  |  ISPE 2019
4.1 Introduction 4.1.1 Rationale 4.1.2 Purpose & Benefits 4.2 SRA Process 4.2.1 Baseline Draft 4.2.2 Performing SRA 4.2.3 Templates 4.3 Timing 4.4 SRA Format ★ Summary

🎓 本章學習目標 Learning Objectives

  1. 理解系統風險評估（SRA）在 C&Q 流程中的核心角色，以及它如何取代傳統 IQ/OQ 方法的冗贅測試。
  2. 掌握 SRA 兩步驟流程：小組草案（Baseline Draft）與擴大團隊審查（Broader Team Review），以及各自所需人員組成。
  3. 區分三個風險等級（低/中/高）的定義，並能舉出製藥設備的實際範例。
  4. 說明 SRA 的執行時機——從概念設計完成後到 IFC 圖面可用時——以及「事件驅動型」（event-triggered）生命周期管理的重要性。
  5. 了解如何以既有 SRA 作為新系統草案的起點，提升 CDMO 或多廠擴建時的效率與一致性。

4.1 Introduction

The System Risk Assessment is the application of QRM (Quality Risk Management) to examine the product quality risk controls for direct impact systems. This assessment identifies the critical design controls (CAs/CDEs) and procedural controls that are required to mitigate system risks to an acceptable level. It is important for the project team performing the System Risk Assessment to include technical SMEs that understand the science behind the process and the risks associated with the CQAs.

System Risk Assessments should be developed for direct impact systems (as determined through system classification described in Chapter 3). For standard off-the-shelf or simple catalog systems, some organizations may consider it unnecessary to perform the System Risk Assessment; a simple protocol or report (e.g., Installation and Operational Verification) could be used to provide the documented evidence that the installation and operation meet the system requirements.

Figure 4.1 shows the relationship between the activities and documents in the C&Q process for direct impact systems. C&Q inspection and testing activities can take place during fabrication and construction as well as during the commissioning/testing activities.

Figure 4.1: Relational Diagram for C&Q Activities and Documents – System Risk Assessment

After the System Risk Assessment is completed, the URS should be checked to ensure that the CAs/CDEs have been included; if they are not included, then the URS should be revised to add them. Procedural control elements should be added to the C&Q scope.

Acceptance and release of the system (described in more detail in Chapter 8) involves confirming that the controls identified in the System Risk Assessment are in place as follows:

  • The design controls (CAs/CDEs) have been shown to operate as specified
  • The procedural controls are in place
講語解析 Commentary

📚 核心概念：什麼是 SRA？

系統風險評估（System Risk Assessment, SRA）是將 ICH Q9 品質風險管理（QRM）原則具體應用於某一直接影響系統的結構化文件。

它回答一個核心問題：「這套系統的哪些設計特性和操作程序，是保護藥品品質的關鍵防線？」

  • CAs（關鍵特性）：直接影響 CQA 的系統屬性（如滅菌溫度、過濾孔徑）
  • CDEs（關鍵設計要素）：用以控制 CA 的設計元件（如溫度感測器位置、濾膜材質選擇）
  • Procedural Controls（程序控制）：以 SOP/作業程序來管理風險（如定期校驗、操作員訓練）

💡 比喻：SRA 就像建築物的結構計算書

蓋一棟房子前，結構工程師會計算哪些梁柱是承重關鍵（=CAs/CDEs），哪些只是裝飾（=間接影響）。SRA 就是製藥廠房設備的「結構計算書」——只有被列為關鍵的部分，才需要進行完整的確認測試。

⚠️ 重點提示：與 URS 的雙向關係

SRA 完成後，必須回頭檢視並更新 URS，確保所有 CAs/CDEs 都已納入需求文件。這是一個「先評估、再補充需求」的迭代流程，與傳統「先寫需求、再測試」的線性思維不同。

💬 思考練習

Q1：一台用於無菌製造區的純水系統（WFI system），它屬於「直接影響系統」嗎？為什麼？

Q2：如果你是工廠的 QA 代表，在 SRA 會議中，你最關心哪類「procedural controls」有沒有被識別出來？

4.1.1 Rationale

The traditional approach to qualification did not directly utilize commissioning documentation; instead, it often relied on an additional set of documents, the Installation Qualification (IQ) and Operational Qualification (OQ) protocols. These protocols provided the documented evidence that the system was installed and operating according to its specification. The scope of the IQ/OQ was determined by various elements such as organization/site established guidelines, vendor specifications, user requirements, and regulatory and guidance documents.

This traditional approach to qualification often resulted in IQ/OQ activities covering more scope than was necessary and repeating successful tests already performed during engineering start-up and commissioning. Furthermore, commissioning activities were commonly not robust enough or well documented since engineering teams anticipated that additional or repeat testing would be performed during qualification activities.

This Guide proposes a more streamlined approach to C&Q. Engineering documentation (i.e., commissioning inspection and testing documentation) is used to provide the documented evidence that the system has been installed and operates to meet the specifications. The CQAs and related CPPs are documented for the system, and a System Risk Assessment is developed to define potential risks to the CQAs and identify design (CAs/CDEs) and procedural controls used to mitigate these risks. Qualification confirms the system is suitable for the intended purpose and that the risk controls (design and procedural controls) are in place and functioning as specified.

講語解析 Commentary

⚠️ 傳統方法的三大問題

  1. 重複測試：IQ/OQ 測試在工廠已做過的項目再做一遍，浪費時間與資源。
  2. 委託文件缺乏嚴謹性：工程師知道「反正後面 QA 還要重測」，所以試運轉（commissioning）文件寫得馬虎、不夠詳細。
  3. 範圍不聚焦：IQ/OQ 測試什麼、不測什麼，缺乏基於風險的理由，往往按照範本「全部都測」。

📚 新方法的核心邏輯

ISPE Vol.5 的改革精神：

  • 工程文件 = 確認文件：試運轉的結果，只要文件品質夠好，可直接作為確認的依據
  • SRA 決定範圍：只有被 SRA 識別為 CAs/CDEs 的部分才需要確認測試
  • 確認（Qualification）的重新定義：確認的重點是「風險控制措施是否到位且有效」，而非「所有規格是否符合」

💡 比喻：廚師備料 vs. 食安稽查

傳統方法像是：廚師做完菜後，食安官員從頭到尾把每個步驟再做一遍確認。新方法像是：食安官員事先指定「哪些步驟是食安關鍵」（=SRA），然後只稽查這些關鍵步驟，廚師做好的備料紀錄也可以直接引用。

💬 思考練習

Q1：在你的工廠，有沒有哪個 IQ/OQ 測試項目，其實在 FAT（工廠驗收測試）就已經測過且通過了？這代表什麼？

Q2：工程試運轉（commissioning）文件要達到什麼「品質標準」，才能被接受為確認的依據？

4.1.2 Purpose and Benefits

The System Risk Assessment has multiple purposes and is a means to:

  • Identify, assess, and record the quality risks to CQAs and associated controls
  • Identify and document the design and procedural controls that are required to control and manage the identified risks
    • The rationale for these controls can also be documented in the System Risk Assessment
    • Testing of the design controls (CAs/CDEs) and verification of procedural controls provides the documentation used to support system qualification
  • Provide guidance for the scope of the DQ, i.e., the scope covers the design of the CAs/CDEs
  • Provide the information that is required for the basis of acceptance and release
  • Provide a focus for Quality Unit oversight

The System Risk Assessment establishes (if not available in other documents) and documents the CAs/CDEs of the system operation and design that can impact product quality. It identifies the design and procedural controls that would mitigate those risks to product quality to an acceptable level. By verifying these controls, the system is confirmed to match that risk profile.

講語解析 Commentary

📚 SRA 的五大用途整理

#用途對應活動
1識別與記錄品質風險FMEA / 危害分析
2識別設計與程序控制措施決定 CAs/CDEs / SOP 清單
3指導 DQ 範圍設計審查僅聚焦 CDEs
4提供放行依據Chapter 8 接受與放行
5QA 單位的監督焦點稽核清單、CAPA 優先排序

📚 何謂「Risk Profile」（風險等級輪廓）？

風險等級（Risk Profile）是 SRA 完成後，描述一個系統「在所有控制措施到位後的殘餘風險狀態」的整體描述。

重要：風險等級是動態的——只有在所有 CAs/CDEs 驗證完成後，才算是「已確認的風險等級」；在此之前，稱為「暫定風險評估（Provisional Risk Assessment）」。

🏛 CDMO 應用場景

在 CDMO（合約開發製造）環境下，SRA 同時服務多個客戶：

  • 第一個客戶的藥品使用生物反應器，SRA 需識別溶氧控制為 CA
  • 第二個客戶的藥品對溫度更敏感，SRA 需額外識別夾套溫控 CDEs
  • QA 可利用 SRA 清楚告知每個客戶，系統的哪些設計特性是為其產品提供保護的

💬 思考練習

Q1：SRA 說「為 DQ 提供範圍指引」，這代表如果某個設計元件沒有出現在 SRA 中，DQ 就不需要審查它嗎？

Q2：QA 單位的「監督焦點（oversight focus）」如何因 SRA 而改變？可以給出一個具體例子嗎？

4.2 System Risk Assessment Process

As a prerequisite, the CQAs and associated CPPs should be identified and documented in the URS.

This Guide presents the following approach to performing the System Risk Assessment:

  • A small team develops an initial baseline draft that includes development of the process description and identification of design and procedural controls
  • A broader team reviews this initial baseline draft, making any necessary revisions to ensure the information is correct and no risks or controls have been omitted, and assigns the system risk profile

As a general guide, the initial session by the small team and the review session by the broader team should not exceed more than a few hours each if the preparation work is complete and teams with the correct level of expertise are used.

An example System Risk Assessment format is presented in Section 4.4.

講語解析 Commentary

📚 SRA 兩步驟流程

ISPE Vol.5 明確規定兩個會議階段，避免單一大型會議耗時失控：

步驟參與者主要產出
Step 1
小組草案會議		 主持人 + QA + SME
（3~4 人）		 初版 SRA 草案：流程描述、潛在危害、初步控制措施清單
Step 2
擴大審查會議		 運營/生產、維護、工程、製程開發、供應商代表 修訂草案、確認無遺漏風險、賦予各項目風險等級

⚠️ 先決條件很重要

指南明確要求：CQAs 和 CPPs 必須先記錄在 URS 中，才能開始執行 SRA。若在 SRA 階段才發現 CQA 不清楚，必須先退回澄清，否則評估結果的品質無法保證。

💡 比喻：兩階段評審就像設計審查流程

小組草案 = 設計師先把初稿畫好（準備充分、效率高）。擴大審查 = 跨部門評審會議（更多角度、找出遺漏）。分開做，比起一開始就召集 10 個人坐在那裡空想要有效率得多。

💬 思考練習

Q1：為什麼指南說「每個會議不應超過數小時」？如果會議超過半天，可能代表什麼問題？

Q2：供應商代表（vendor representative）在 Step 2 的擴大審查中，可以提供哪些傳統 QA 或工程師無法提供的視角？

4.2.1 Developing the Baseline Draft

The small team that develops the initial baseline draft should consist of the following:

  • Experienced facilitator to guide the process
  • Quality Unit representative
  • Process/system SME (may be one SME or could additionally include a system vendor representative)

Refer to Chapter 19 (Appendix 5) for an example baseline System Risk Assessment.

講語解析 Commentary

📚 三個關鍵角色的職責

  • 主持人（Facilitator）：確保會議結構化進行，避免發散；需有 SRA 方法論的經驗，但不必是製程專家
  • QA 代表：確保法規要求被納入考量；判斷哪些風險屬於 GMP 必須控制的範疇
  • SME（主題專家）：提供系統技術細節；了解實際失效模式；可包含設備供應商代表

⚠️ 「主持人」的重要性常被低估

一個缺乏經驗的主持人，容易讓 SRA 會議變成「技術討論會」而非「風險識別會」。好的主持人應當：

  • 控制會議節奏，不讓單一議題過度討論
  • 確保每個操作步驟都被系統性地審查
  • 將技術討論引導回「風險—控制措施」的框架

🏛 CDMO 應用場景

在 CDMO 的新設備引進時，小組草案成員建議：

  • 主持人：C&Q 項目工程師（有跨案例經驗）
  • QA：負責該客戶製程的 QA 工程師
  • SME：設備供應商的應用工程師 + 內部製程工程師

供應商工程師對於自家設備的已知失效模式最清楚，是初版草案不可或缺的資訊來源。

💬 思考練習

Q1：小型公司（如臨床階段的新創）若沒有專職的「主持人」，可以如何因應？

Q2：為什麼草案階段只用「小組」，而不直接召集所有相關人員？這樣做的風險是什麼？

4.2.2 Performing the System Risk Assessment

After the initial baseline is completed, a broader team reviews the document and determines the risk profile. This review team generally consists of representatives from a broader group with different experiences to provide a balanced perspective; this team could include:

  • Operations (Production)
  • Maintenance
  • Engineering
  • Process development
  • Vendor representatives
Note: The time taken for the review generally increases with the number of people in the team, thus maintaining a balance between experience and the number of team members is important.

Prior to determining the risk profile, the team identifies the sources of the risks (potential failure modes) along with design aspects and/or procedural controls that would mitigate or eliminate the risk. Risk profiles are assigned per definitions shown in Table 4.1.

Table 4.1: Risk Level Definitions

Risk Level Definition
Low Considered acceptable with no actions needed. The likelihood of the risk occurring with the defined controls operating is considered low, and the detection is robust.
Medium Normally considered unacceptable and requires mitigation through design (CAs/CDEs) and/or procedural controls. However, the SME reviewers may consider a medium risk as acceptable for the specific process/system and decide to accept the risk.
High Considered unacceptable and requires mitigation through design and/or procedural controls. In certain situations, the SME reviewers may determine that these controls are not appropriate, e.g., implementation costs outweigh the incurred costs if the risk occurred, operational challenges, or other reasons. The SMEs may recommend acceptance of the system with the high risk; in this case, the assessment needs to be accepted by high-level management.
Note: The risk level is defined considering the overall process; thus, if the process is changed, the System Risk Assessments may need to be reviewed/updated. This aspect should be addressed through change management (see Chapter 12).

Determination of the risk profile should also be based on the SME's experience with the process/system. While defining the risk of the failure or hazard occurring, the SME should consider that the controls listed are in place and operating as intended.

The design controls (CAs and/or CDEs) defined during the System Risk Assessment are considered part of the system requirements and should be included in the URS. After the System Risk Assessment is completed, the URS should be updated to include these controls. If a Traceability Matrix is used as a tool to manage the C&Q execution process, the CDEs could be added to the Traceability Matrix only and updating the URS would not be needed.

Procedural controls identified during the System Risk Assessment need to be included in the C&Q Plan scope and could also be added to the Traceability Matrix.

講語解析 Commentary

📚 Table 4.1 風險等級解讀——製藥實例

等級定義要點製藥設備實例
低（Low） 控制措施在位時，發生可能性低且偵測可靠 WFI 系統水槽外殼塗裝顏色（對 CQA 無影響）
中（Medium） 通常不可接受，需要設計或程序控制；但 SME 可依情境接受 凍乾機腔體溫度均一性——需 CDEs（溫度感測點位置）+ SOP（負荷驗證）
高（High） 不可接受，必須有緩解措施；若接受高風險，需高層管理者批准 無菌灌裝機的 HEPA 過濾完整性——若失效直接導致污染，屬最高優先 CA

⚠️ 「高風險可被接受？」的邏輯

指南允許 SME 在特殊情況下建議「接受高風險」——例如某個老舊設備的改造成本極高。但這個決定必須：

  • 有充分的書面理由
  • 經過高層管理者（high-level management）批准簽署
  • 納入變更管理追蹤

這體現了 ICH Q9 的精神：風險管理不是消除所有風險，而是讓風險在被理解和接受的基礎上被管理。

📚 追溯矩陣（Traceability Matrix）的角色

Traceability Matrix（追溯矩陣）是一個將 URS 需求 ↔ SRA 風險控制 ↔ 測試文件 三者連結起來的管理工具。

指南提供了一個靈活選項：若公司使用追溯矩陣，CDEs 可以只加入矩陣而不需要更新 URS，減少文件維護負擔。

實務建議：大型跨功能項目（如新廠建設）適合使用追溯矩陣；小型設備改造則直接更新 URS 更為簡便。

🏛 CDMO 應用場景：風險等級指派的一致性

CDMO 面對多客戶多品種時，同一套設備對不同客戶的風險等級可能不同：

  • 高活性原料藥客戶：噴霧乾燥機密封性 = High（直接影響 OEL 與產品純度）
  • 一般固體劑型客戶：同一台設備密封性 = Medium

因此 CDMO 的 SRA 必須按製程/客戶分開評估，不能共用同一份風險等級結論。

💬 思考練習

Q1：在 SRA 會議中，SME 在評估風險等級時，應假設「控制措施已在位且正常運作」——這個假設為什麼重要？若不這樣假設，結果會如何？

Q2：「Program 控制」（程序控制）被列入 SRA 後，應如何確保它在設備放行前確實存在（例如 SOP 已發布並完成人員訓練）？

4.2.3 Using Completed Assessments as a Starting Point for New System Baseline Drafts

The experience and documentation gained from completing System Risk Assessments can be applied to future systems. In addition, many systems used for pharmaceutical manufacturing and packaging are standard systems that have been in use for a reasonable period of time, have built-in control strategies, and are developed by experienced vendors with established engineering quality systems. Therefore, any new systems that are identical to or similar to existing systems can utilize the completed System Risk Assessments as a starting point.

The small team that develops the baseline draft (as described in Section 4.2.1) should assess the new system against the completed System Risk Assessment for the existing system that is identical/similar. The SMEs should determine if the system under review has different functionality and/or components. If the SMEs determine that these differences may introduce additional or different risks, then the baseline draft needs to be updated to include the risks and associated risk controls.

The remainder of the System Risk Assessment process would proceed as described in Section 4.2.2. The broader team reviews the baseline draft and determines the risk profile for the new system.

The use of completed assessments as a starting point for new system baseline drafts can improve the efficiency and consistency of the process.

講語解析 Commentary

📚 「模板化 SRA」的流程邏輯

本節提供了一個非常實用的效率化機制：

  1. 拿出既有（完成且核准的）SRA 作為起點
  2. 小組比較新舊系統的差異（功能、元件、配置）
  3. 僅針對「差異點」更新風險識別與控制措施
  4. 其餘不變的部分直接沿用
  5. 完整的擴大審查仍需進行，確認整體評估正確

重要：這不是「複製貼上」——每份 SRA 最終仍必須獨立審查與批准。

⚠️ 「相同」與「類似」的判斷標準

以下差異可能引入新風險，需要更新 SRA：

  • 製程參數範圍擴大（如更高溫度或壓力）
  • 不同製造商或型號（即使功能相同）
  • 新增或移除控制迴路（如由手動改為自動）
  • 安裝位置不同（如潔淨等級不同的房間）
  • 用於不同的 CQA 或產品類型

🏛 CDMO 的重大實務效益

CDMO 的競爭優勢之一就是標準化能力。「模板化 SRA」讓 CDMO 可以：

  • 第 1 條相同設備線的 SRA：需要完整資源（假設 3 天）
  • 第 2、3、4 條線（相同設備）：以差異化分析為主（假設 0.5 天）
  • 引進類似但不同品牌的設備：以現有 SRA 為基礎，重點審查差異（假設 1~1.5 天）

這不僅節省時間，更確保了多條線之間的風險識別一致性——這對 FDA/EMA 稽查是明顯的優勢。

💬 思考練習

Q1：你公司引進了與現有系統「型號相同但控制軟體版本不同」的設備，這算「identical」還是「similar」？應如何處理 SRA？

Q2：使用舊 SRA 作為模板的最大風險是什麼？如何在制度上降低「舊 SRA 錯誤被繼承」的風險？

4.3 Timing of System Risk Assessments

4.3.1 Development of the System Risk Assessment

The System Risk Assessment can be developed after completion of concept design and prior to the start of detailed engineering. It can be updated later as required. The System Risk Assessment can be completed when the Issued for Construction (IFC) design drawings and specifications are available, whether for new or modified systems. These drawings and specifications represent what will be built including any incorporated changes made through the DR/DQ process. Therefore, the System Risk Assessment can be confirmed and approved at this stage.

Note: Depending on the level of product and process knowledge, some of the CDEs associated with CAs may be known while the balance of the CDEs will be identified during the engineering design lifecycle (and can be documented as part of the DQ). All CDEs should be listed in the System Risk Assessment.

The System Risk Assessment defines the system risk profile, i.e., what it will be after the risk controls have been verified to be in place and operating as specified. Until the verification is completed, it is considered a provisional risk assessment.

For novel systems, starting the System Risk Assessment earlier in the design process can be beneficial since this allows for any identified risks to be controlled by design. Most risk control is achieved through system design; a procedural control is not considered as robust.

For standard or catalog systems where the potential risks are well understood and design controls are built in where possible, the System Risk Assessment could be performed at any time before the final DR of the system. Alternatively, an Installation and Operational Verification document could be used. DQ can also confirm that the system risk controls are adequate.

The sequence of activities for direct impact systems is shown in Figure 4.2.

Figure 4.2: Sequence of Activities for Direct Impact Systems

4.3.2 Lifecycle of the System Risk Assessment

Depending on the project size, timing, and complexity, additional product/process or system knowledge may become available after completion of the System Risk Assessment. If this additional knowledge impacts the system risk profile, the System Risk Assessment needs to be reviewed and updated.

System Risk Assessments are not subject to time-based periodic review; it is more efficient to reassess the risk profile in the event of a deviation related to the system performance and determine if an update is required. The System Risk Assessment can also be used as a reference document for assessing potential changes to a system.

For any changes to the system, the URS and System Risk Assessment should both be reviewed as part of the change management process (refer to Chapter 12). If the proposed change introduces additional risks or impacts existing risk controls, the System Risk Assessment (and associated URS) needs to be reviewed and updated.

講語解析 Commentary

📚 SRA 的時間軸：從概念設計到放行

階段SRA 狀態行動
概念設計完成後 可開始起草 初版草案，識別主要風險
詳細工程設計中 持續更新 隨 CDEs 逐步識別而補充
IFC 圖面發布後 可確認批准 最終版 SRA 核准（仍為暫定）
驗證活動完成後 正式確認 暫定 → 已確認之風險等級

📚 關鍵術語：IFC（Issued for Construction）

IFC（建造用圖發布）是工程設計流程中一個關鍵里程碑：代表設計圖面已完成所有審查（包括 DR/DQ），是最終將用於施工的版本。

ISPE 選擇 IFC 作為 SRA 最終核准時機，因為此時「我們要建什麼」已完全確定，風險控制措施也可以準確對應到具體設計元件。

📚 「暫定風險評估」的意義

Provisional Risk Assessment（暫定風險評估）：SRA 核准後、驗證完成前的中間狀態。

這是一個重要的法規概念：SRA 的「核准」代表「我們計畫如何控制風險」，但它必須等到所有 CAs/CDEs 都驗證通過後，才能被認為是「已實現的風險等級」。在此之前，系統還不能被正式放行用於商業生產。

⚠️ 行業思維重大轉變：事件驅動，非定期審查！

這是本章最重要的管理概念之一：

傳統觀念（錯誤）：「每年要重新審查一次 SRA」

ISPE 指南（正確）：SRA 是事件驅動型（event-triggered）文件——只有在下列情況才需要審查更新：

  • 系統發生偏差（deviation）且與系統效能有關
  • 提出系統變更（change control）
  • 獲得新的產品/製程知識，影響風險判斷

這個轉變大幅減少了不必要的文件負擔，讓 QA 資源可以集中在真正需要審查的地方。

💡 比喻：汽車保固 vs. 事故報告

傳統「定期審查」像是每年硬性規定讓汽車進廠做一次「全車系統風險重評」（即使沒有任何異常）。ISPE 的「事件驅動型」像是：車子發生事故或重大改裝時，才重新評估風險——平時保持現有的維護計畫即可。這不是「降低標準」，而是「把注意力放到真正需要的地方」。

🏛 CDMO 應用場景：變更管理觸發 SRA 更新

CDMO 常見觸發 SRA 審查的情境：

  • 客戶要求修改製程參數範圍（如溫度上限提高）
  • 設備控制系統升級（軟體版本更新，可能影響警報設定）
  • 微生物偏差調查發現某個系統設計有潛在問題
  • 引進類似但更大規格的設備（scale-up）

每次變更管理（Change Control）啟動時，應自動觸發一個評估步驟：「這個變更是否影響現有 SRA？」

💬 思考練習

Q1：「新穎系統（novel systems）」為什麼應該在設計流程更早期就開始 SRA？這與「設計控制優於程序控制」的原則有什麼關係？

Q2：如果你的工廠目前有「每年審查 SRA」的 SOP，你將如何向管理層說明改為「事件驅動型審查」是更符合指南精神且更有效率的做法？

4.4 Example System Risk Assessment Format

This Guide presents an example System Risk Assessment format that consists of thirteen columns. Table 4.2 summarizes the risk assessment process and how the contents of the example System Risk Assessment are developed.

Refer to Chapter 19 (Appendix 5) for an example of a baseline System Risk Assessment.

Table 4.2: Contents of Example System Risk Assessment Format

* Regulatory requirements (e.g., labeling, dating, batch coding) can be addressed in the same manner as CQAs. Controls will normally be incorporated into the design and verified to work to ensure the regulatory requirement is met.

Col # Column Name Description
1 Reference Number Item reference number.
2 Operations Sequence / Process Flow List the entire operational sequence of the system if the system operates in a sequential manner. Include cycles such as Clean-in-Place (CIP) or Sterilize-in-Place (SIP). When the system operates continuously (e.g., for a critical utility system), then a process flow is appropriate.
3 Process Description Add a brief description of the process that applies to the sequence.
4 CQA * List the CQA that is relevant for this step of the sequence/process. If none at this point, enter N/A.
5 CPP This entry should map to the corresponding CQA in the same row. List the CPP whose variability has an impact on the CQA and can be monitored or controlled for that row. If none, enter N/A.
6 Impact on CQA Enter direct or indirect, based on the impact of the established CPP on the CQA. For example, direct impact is where the CPP directly impacts the CQA. This entry is used to establish the criticality of any associated alarms.
7 How CQA can be Impacted Add a brief description on how the CQA can be impacted at this step of the sequence/process, e.g., due to incorrect or out of range conditions of the CPP. This entry is used to define the possible hazard(s) to the CQA at this point of the sequence/process; it serves as an aid in the SME determination of risk.
8 Critical Aspect (CA) List the Critical Aspect(s) (CAs) associated with the CPP. CAs are measurable or observable attributes of the system that, if outside the defined limits, can directly affect the ability of the system to perform its function. Enter N/A if no CA applies.
9 Critical Design Element (CDE) List the Critical Design Element(s) (CDEs) associated with the CA in the same row. CDEs are the specific design features, components, or parameters that ensure the CA is met. These become the focus of the DQ and commissioning verification activities.
10 Procedural Control List the procedural controls (e.g., SOPs, work instructions, training requirements, monitoring schedules) that mitigate or eliminate the identified risk. These controls must be in place and verified before system acceptance/release.
11 Risk Level Assign the risk level (Low / Medium / High) per Table 4.1 definitions. The risk level is assigned by the broader review team and considers the controls in columns 9 and 10 as being in place and functioning as intended.
12 Rationale for Risk Level Provide a brief justification for the assigned risk level. This documents the team's reasoning and is particularly important for Medium and High risk assignments, or where a risk is accepted without full mitigation.
13 Remarks / Actions Record any additional actions required (e.g., additional testing, design changes, SOP creation) or references to related documents (e.g., URS section, DQ report, validation protocol). Also used to track open action items until closure.

Reading Table 4.2 — The Logic Flow Across Columns

Each row in the SRA table follows a structured logic flow:

Col 2–3: Define what the system does at each step (operational context).

Col 4–6: Link the operation to product quality — which CQA is at stake, which CPP controls it, and whether the impact is direct or indirect.

Col 7: Describe how a failure could occur — the failure mode or hazard pathway.

Col 8–10: Document the controls — both design-based (CAs/CDEs) and procedural.

Col 11–12: Assign and justify the risk level considering the controls are in place.

Col 13: Track open actions to closure and cross-reference related documents.

講語解析 Commentary

📚 Table 4.2 十三欄的邏輯結構

十三欄可以分為四個功能群組：

  • 欄 1–3（背景脈絡）：這步驟在做什麼？
  • 欄 4–7（品質連結）：與哪個 CQA 有關？如何影響？
  • 欄 8–10（控制措施）：設計上如何控制（CAs/CDEs）？程序上如何控制（SOP）？
  • 欄 11–13（風險決策）：整體風險等級為何？理由？還有哪些未完成事項？

⚠️ 欄 6「直接/間接影響」的實務意義

「直接影響（Direct）」：CPP 直接決定 CQA 數值，如灌裝速度直接影響裝量準確性。

「間接影響（Indirect）」：CPP 通過中間環節影響 CQA，如壓縮空氣壓力影響閥門動作速度，進而影響裝量。

這個區分影響警報分類：直接影響的警報通常被設計為高優先警報（critical alarm）。

💡 比喻：SRA 表格像一張偵探調查表

每一行就像一個案件：欄 2-3 是案發現場，欄 4-7 是受害者與犯案手法，欄 8-10 是已有的防護措施，欄 11-12 是對整體危害程度的最終判斷，欄 13 是待辦的後續調查行動。

🏛 CDMO 應用：SRA 表格模板標準化

CDMO 可以為常見設備類型建立「預填式 SRA 模板」：

  • WFI 系統：欄 2（TOC 偵測步驟）+ 欄 4（CQA: 微生物限度）預填完成
  • 滅菌櫃：欄 2（SIP 循環步驟）+ 欄 8（CA: 滅菌溫度）預填完成
  • 無菌灌裝機：欄 9（CDE: HEPA 完整性測試裝置）預填完成

新客戶引進時，只需更新 欄 4（對應新產品的 CQA）和 欄 11（結合客戶製程知識重評風險等級）。

💬 思考練習

Q1：在 SRA 表格的「欄 11 風險等級」中，評估團隊應「假設欄 9 和欄 10 的控制措施均已到位」。若某項 CDE 在設計上尚未確認可行，評估者應如何標記？

Q2：「欄 13 備註/行動」是一個活性追蹤欄位。它完成（close out）的條件應該是什麼？由誰負責核實關閉？

🏛 本章重點摘要 Chapter 4 Summary

  • SRA 的本質：將 QRM 原則應用於直接影響系統，識別 CAs/CDEs（設計控制）與程序控制，取代傳統 IQ/OQ 測試範圍不當的問題。
  • 兩步驟流程：小組（主持人 + QA + SME）先建立草案；擴大團隊（生產/維護/工程/製程開發/供應商）審查並賦予風險等級，每次各僅需數小時。
  • 三個風險等級：Low（可接受）/ Medium（需緩解或 SME 接受）/ High（需緩解，接受時需高層批准），均需考量控制措施已到位的前提。
  • 執行時機：最早可在概念設計完成後開始；最晚在 IFC 圖面發布後確認核准；驗證完成前均為「暫定風險評估」。
  • 事件驅動型生命周期：SRA 不做定期審查，而是在偏差、變更管理或新知識獲取時才觸發審查更新——這是行業思維的重要轉變。
  • 模板化應用：相同或類似系統可以既有 SRA 為起點，只更新差異部分，大幅提升效率與一致性——對 CDMO 尤其有價值。
  • Table 4.2 十三欄結構：從操作背景（欄 1-3）→ 品質影響（欄 4-7）→ 控制措施（欄 8-10）→ 風險決策與追蹤（欄 11-13），形成完整的風險評估邏輯鏈。
5

Chapter 5: Design Review & Design Qualification

設計審查與設計確認（DQ） | p35-p40

ISPE Baseline® Guide Vol.5 — Commissioning and Qualification (2nd Edition)

Chapter 5: Design Review and Design Qualification 設計審查與設計確認
Pages 35–40  |  Sections 5.1 – 5.5

🎓 本章學習目標 Learning Objectives

  1. 理解設計審查（DR）與設計確認（DQ）的根本區別：DR 涵蓋所有設計面向，DQ 僅聚焦於直接影響系統的 CAs/CDEs，並需 Quality Unit 核准。
  2. 掌握三階段設計流程（概念 → 設計基礎 BOD → 詳細設計）及各階段產出文件（IFD、IFC）的意義。
  3. 了解 ASTM E2500-13 對設計審查的定義，以及跨職能 SME 團隊在 DR 中的角色與 QA 出席建議。
  4. 說明 DQ 的三大目標、前提要件（URS、SRA、completed DRs）及最終 DQ 報告應包含的內容。
  5. 能夠解讀 Table 5.1 所示的專案階段與 DR/DQ 交付成果時序，並應用於 CDMO 資本專案規劃。

📄 本章結構

5.1 Introduction 5.2 Design Process 5.3 Design Review 5.4 Design Qualification 5.5 Timing (Table 5.1) 章節總結
5.1

Introduction — 簡介

DR and DQ: purposes, scope, and the critical distinction

5.1 Introduction (p.35)

This chapter provides guidance for performing and documenting Design Reviews (DRs) and Design Qualification (DQ). This Guide emphasizes the importance of DRs leading to DQ as a continual process throughout all phases in the design of new or modified systems.

DRs provide assurance that the design deliverables are consistent with the URS and the mitigation control strategies developed during the System Risk Assessment. When properly performed, DRs reduce the need for costly design-related change orders.

DQ is performed only for direct impact systems (as determined through system classification described in Chapter 3). DQ involves more formal documentation, with Quality Unit approval, to show traceability of the CAs and relevant CDEs in the design to the CPPs and CQAs.

DR and DQ are not intended to be separate activities, but rather separate documentation in which DQ is focused on CAs/CDEs and involves the Quality Unit as an approver. There should be minimal duplication of work; the final report from DR is a key input into the DQ process.

解讀視观 Commentary

🔑 核心概念：DR vs. DQ 根本區別

設計審查 DR（Design Review）：涵蓋所有設計面向，包含工程、操作、安全、品質——所有系統皆適用。

設計確認 DQ（Design Qualification）：只針對「直接影響系統（Direct Impact Systems）」，且聚焦於 CAs（關鍵特性）和 CDEs（關鍵設計要素）——需要 Quality Unit 核准，屬正式驗證文件。

💡 記憶口訣：DR 看全局；DQ 看品質關鍵點，只限直接影響系統。

⚠ 重點提示：「非各別活動，而是各別文件」

原文這句話在實務中的意思：DR 和 DQ 在時間上可以重疊，工程師不需要「做完 DR 再做 DQ」。

實務運作：DR 會議記錄 → 整理出 CAs/CDEs → DQ 報告直接引用 DR 結果，避免重複紀錄。DQ 不是另起爐灶，而是對 DR 的聚焦與升格（加入 QA 核准）。

📚 比喻：建築審查 vs. 消防安全認證

DR 如同全面建築審查：結構、水電、消防、美觀一起看。DQ 如同消防安全認證：只針對消防相關設計（逃生出口、噴淋系統）做正式認可，並由主管機關（Quality Unit）蓋章。兩者共用同一套建築圖，不需要畫兩次。

5.2

Design Process — 設計流程

Three phases: Concept → BOD → Detailed Design; GEP and risk-based approach

5.2 Design Process (p.35–36)

The design process can be divided into several phases to ensure the design deliverables are sufficiently developed, the risks are identified and mitigated, and the project (as defined) meets financial objectives. The phases of the design process are:

  1. Concept
  2. Basis of Design (BOD)
  3. Detailed Design

The concept and BOD phases define the Scope of Work (SOW) for the project.

In the concept phase, several approaches (scope options) to meeting the URS may be evaluated. These alternatives should be evaluated for their impact on the business objective, project cost, and risk to quality. The project stakeholders should select the preferred scope option; the project then progresses to the BOD phase.

In the BOD phase, additional engineering work provides a more developed SOW. The BOD design package contains Issued for Design (IFD) documents; it is the basis for the detailed design phase which delivers Issued for Construction (IFC) documents.

5.2.1 Importance of Good Engineering Practice

During the design process, it is important to follow GEP to support the integrity of related data and documentation. DR activities include evaluating deliverables against engineering standards and business, operations, and quality requirements as well as identifying gaps and proposing required corrective actions. Documenting these activities using Good Documentation Practice concepts (as described in Chapter 13) supports the overall effort to ensure the system is suitable for the intended purpose.

5.2.2 Science and Risk-Based Approach to Design Reviews

A quality risk assessment of the manufacturing process (including the environmental conditions supporting the process and/or critical systems) is a significant activity outside of the C&Q scope that can influence the early phase of design. Design stage System Risk Assessment typically uses knowledge from process risk assessments and other process knowledge to evaluate system design with respect to process control failure modes. These assessments are an integral part of the science and risk-based C&Q approach.

Design stage quality risk reviews are an iterative process that is linked to the design development of the process system. The review of the System Risk Assessments and how the results affect the proposed design should be included in the scope of DRs.

解讀視观 Commentary

🕐 三階段設計流程圖解

1. 概念階段（Concept）：評估多種方案，選出最符合 URS、成本與品質風險平衡的方案。

2. 設計基礎階段（BOD）：輸出 IFD（Issued for Design，設計用圖），確立工程範圍（SOW）。

3. 詳細設計階段（Detailed Design）：輸出 IFC（Issued for Construction，建造用圖），可直接用於施工。

DR 在三個階段都應執行；DQ 通常在詳細設計完成後正式執行。

🔧 術語解析：IFD vs. IFC

  • IFD（Issued for Design）：尚在設計階段，供工程師內部使用、審查，可能仍有修訂。
  • IFC（Issued for Construction）：已完成設計審查、凍結版本，可交付給承包商施工。

IFD 是 DR 的主要審查對象；IFC 是 DQ 的最終確認對象。

📚 GEP 在設計審查中的角色

GEP（良好工程規範）不是一份法規文件，而是工程界公認的最佳實踐標準。DR 的功能之一就是確認設計符合 GEP：對照業界規範（如 ASME、ASTM、ISO 標準）找出缺口並提出修正行動。

GEP 加上良好文件實踐（GDP）= 確保「系統適合其預期用途」的基礎。

🧠 5.2.2 迭代風險評估的重要性

設計階段的風險評估不是「做一次就結束」。隨著設計從概念演進到詳細設計，新的失效模式可能浮現。DR 應定期納入最新的系統風險評估（SRA）結果，確保設計決策與風險控制策略保持一致。

💡 實務提示：將 SRA 版本號列入每次 DR 的審查範圍，確保可追溯性。

5.3

Design Review — 設計審查

Objectives, SME roles, process, and outcome including Figure 5.1

5.3.1 Objectives of Design Review (p.36)

DRs are defined in ASTM E2500-13 [5] as follows:

"Planned and systematic reviews of specifications, design, and design development and continuous improvement changes performed as appropriate throughout the life-cycle of the manufacturing system. Design reviews evaluate deliverables against standards and requirements, identify problems, and propose required corrective actions."

DRs include both quality critical and non-critical aspects of the system design.

The documented results of the DR should be the basis for any design modifications/additions performed to correct any deficiencies in the design under review.

5.3.2 Role of Subject Matter Experts and Quality Unit

Throughout the design process, a cross-functional project team (refer to Section 6.4 for example approval matrix) reviews the design of the system to ensure that the product and process user requirements, GMP, and regulatory requirements are included. Thus, it is important that this team includes technical SMEs that have the appropriate experience and correct knowledge of the process, process equipment, control strategies, and facilities to ensure that the design under review will meet the requirements of the URS, function efficiently, and consistently produce quality product.

If the system being reviewed is direct impact, then the team should also include a Quality Unit representative to ensure that all quality requirements are met. This can help to facilitate the review and approval of the DQ.

5.3.3 Design Review Process (p.36–37)

Prior to the DR, design documents should be circulated to the DR project team for their review to ensure a comprehensive review process. It is the responsibility of the project manager and the design leads to ensure that the appropriate participants are part of the DR. Senior management from the Quality Unit, operations, and production are responsible for ensuring the proper representatives with the appropriate experience are present during the DR.

The project team should define the method for conducting DR according to the system type, size, and risk. This method should be documented and approved in applicable plans (e.g., Project Execution Plan, C&Q Plan).

The effort, formality, and documentation of DRs should follow the ICH Q9 [3] principles of being commensurate with the level of risk. DR documentation may take the form of engineering meeting minutes or notes. For highly critical novel systems, DRs may be more focused and detailed.

For off-the-shelf equipment, DR should consider the complexity and/or risk to system or facility operation and to quality. Vendor documents are typically used to conduct these reviews and, if necessary, a technical vendor representative could attend the DR. The focus should be on the CPPs controlled by the equipment and the CAs/CDEs required for the product.
