DRs focus on both engineering design and quality aspects of the design.

The engineering design focus is the technical aspects of the system; the objective is to verify the operability, maintainability, and safety aspects of the system. Technical SMEs, system owners, and any other stakeholders need to be present. It is optional for the Quality Unit to attend these reviews that focus on the technical aspects; however, their presence is beneficial and can simplify the DQ step.

The quality focus of the DRs is on compliance elements and the CAs/CDEs of the system design that affect product quality; the objective is to verify that all regulatory requirements are addressed by the design. It is strongly recommended the Quality Unit attends these reviews with quality focus, and that these reviews are documented.

5.3.4 Design Review Outcome (p.37)

The DR project team should have appropriate methods for recording and distributing the results of the DRs and managing any consequent changes. The results should confirm the continuing suitability of the design and confirm that the design is suitable for the intended purpose.

The team is responsible for communicating to their management any issues affecting design.

Figure 5.1 provides an overview of the DR process. The figure illustrates a sequential process flow: starting from design deliverables, proceeding through the DR meeting (with SME and QA participation), generating action items / open issues, resolving deficiencies, and concluding with a documented DR report that feeds into the DQ process.

Note (from Figure 5.1): The Traceability Matrix is a document format which compares the product and process requirements for the system with the CAs/CDEs.

Refer to Chapter 20 (Appendix 6) for examples of DR reports.

解讀視观 Commentary

📚 ASTM E2500-13 定義解析

ASTM E2500-13 是美國材料試驗協會發布的製藥設備驗證標準，其 DR 定義強調三個關鍵詞：

  • Planned（計劃性）：非臨時性，應事先排程並有明確範圍。
  • Systematic（系統性）：有結構的審查方法，非隨意瀏覽文件。
  • Throughout the life-cycle（貫穿全生命週期）：包含新建、改造、持續改善。

重點：DR 涵蓋品質關鍵與非關鍵兩類設計面向，這與 DQ（只看 CAs/CDEs）形成對比。

👥 SME 與 Quality Unit 的角色分工

SME（主題專家）：來自工程、製程、設備、設施等各領域，確保設計技術上可行且符合操作需求。

Quality Unit（品質部門）：

  • 工程技術導向 DR → 出席為可選（但有益）
  • 品質合規導向 DR → 強烈建議出席，並應記錄
  • 直接影響系統的 DR → 必須有 QA 代表參與

💡 QA 提早介入 DR，可大幅簡化後續的 DQ 核准流程。

⚡ ICH Q9 原則在 DR 中的應用

DR 的投入程度（effort）、正式程度（formality）、記錄詳細度，應與系統風險等級相稱：

  • 低風險輔助系統 → 會議記錄即可（engineering meeting minutes）
  • 高度關鍵新型系統 → 需要更聚焦、更詳細的 DR 文件
  • 現貨設備（off-the-shelf）→ 以供應商文件為基礎進行審查

這體現了 ISPE Vol.5「基於科學與風險」的核心哲學。

📄 Figure 5.1 流程說明（無圖版）

雖然原文圖示無法嵌入，其流程可描述如下：

設計交付物 → DR 規劃（確定範圍/參與者）→ DR 會議（SME + 可能含 QA）→ 產生行動項目/開放問題 → 問題解決/設計修訂 → DR 報告（記錄審查結果）→ 輸入至 DQ 流程（若為直接影響系統）

其中「追溯矩陣（Traceability Matrix）」在 DR 報告中用於比對 URS 需求與 CAs/CDEs。

🔍 追溯矩陣（Traceability Matrix）簡介

追溯矩陣是一個表格工具，橫向連結：

  • URS 中的產品/製程需求
  • 系統設計中對應的 CAs/CDEs
  • 驗收標準（acceptance criteria）

它不是法規強制要求，但是強大的專案管理工具，確保每個品質需求都有對應的設計控制，且不遺漏。

5.4

Design Qualification — 設計確認

Objectives, prerequisites, DQ process, and final DQ report

5.4.1 Objectives of Design Qualification (p.38)

DQ provides documented verification that the design of a new or modified direct impact system will result in a system that is suitable for the intended purpose. The objectives of DQ are to:

  • Verify the design will meet the quality user requirements as listed in the URS
  • Verify the design will adequately control risks to product quality and patient safety, as identified during the System Risk Assessment
  • Verify the CAs/CDEs necessary to implement these requirements and risk controls

5.4.2 Prerequisites

The prerequisites for DQ include:

  • Approved URS
  • Functional requirements (for automated systems)
  • System Risk Assessments with identification of design (CAs/CDEs) and procedural controls that will be used to mitigate the unacceptable risks
  • Completed DRs, with verification that all open design issues that affect CAs/CDEs, CPPs, and CQAs are closed and included in the final design

It is the responsibility of the project manager to ensure that all prerequisites have been completed and are made available to the participants prior to the DQ for their review. The DQ should be scheduled to allow adequate time for preliminary review of the material to be covered.

5.4.3 Design Qualification Process (p.38–39)

DQ is the documented process for the review and approval of the final system design to verify the following:

  • All process and product requirements in the system URS have been incorporated into the design
  • Quality and regulatory requirements in the system URS have been incorporated into the design
  • Any changes to the design approach for the CAs and any associated CDEs have been reviewed, as appropriate

The DR documentation should be reviewed to confirm the Quality Unit was included in the DR, as defined in the project plan, and has provided the appropriate input to the design.

The approach for performing DQ should be defined in planning documents. For small projects, there may be one DQ performed after all the design is completed. For larger projects, the design may be broken into several areas or functions, with the DQ performed when each design is completed.

A formal protocol document to check requirements against the design is not a regulatory requirement. However, the following information should be defined: plan for conducting the DQ, scope of the DQ, and Quality Unit approval of the DQ. This information could be documented for individual systems or for specified integrated systems.

A Traceability Matrix can be used to document traceability of the CAs and any associated CDEs, and CPPs to the CQAs. The CA and CDE acceptance criteria can also be documented in the Traceability Matrix.

5.4.4 Final Design Qualification Report (p.39)

The final DQ report should include or refer to the following, as applicable:

  • Any needed risk reviews to document the incorporation of design control elements to support quality product manufacturing
  • Identification of each CDE (critical aspect of the physical and functional design) that serves to control identified potential process failures
  • Description of each CA and any supporting CDEs in terms that are verifiable through inspections or testing (acceptance criteria)
  • The CDEs that serve to meet a product or process user requirement in terms that are verifiable (mainly through performance testing)

A final DQ report should be issued stating the design is suitable for the intended purpose; the report should be approved by representatives (from the appropriate level) in Engineering, Manufacturing and the Quality Unit.

Figure 5.2 provides an overview of the DQ process: beginning with DQ prerequisites (approved URS, completed SRA, completed DRs), proceeding through the DQ review of CAs/CDEs against URS requirements, using the Traceability Matrix, and concluding with the final DQ report bearing tri-party approval.

Refer to Chapter 20 (Appendix 6) for an example of a DQ summary.

解讀視观 Commentary

🎯 DQ 三大目標深度解析

DQ 的三個目標形成一個完整的驗證邏輯鏈：

  • 目標一（符合 URS）：連結 URS → 設計，確保每條品質需求都被「設計進去了」。
  • 目標二（風險控制）：連結 SRA 識別的風險 → 設計中的控制措施（CAs/CDEs），確保無遺漏。
  • 目標三（CAs/CDEs 確認）：明確列出哪些是關鍵特性/關鍵設計要素，為後續 IQ/OQ/PQ 的測試計劃奠基。

💡 DQ 是「設計與驗證之橋」：它確保進入建造/採購前，品質需求已被完整設計進去。

📋 DQ 前提要件清單

在啟動 DQ 前，專案經理必須確認以下文件已完成且可取得：

  • ✅ 已核准的 URS
  • ✅ 功能需求（自動化系統適用）
  • ✅ 含 CAs/CDEs 識別的系統風險評估（SRA）
  • ✅ 已完成的 DR，且所有影響 CAs/CDEs/CPPs/CQAs 的開放問題均已關閉

💡 實務提示：建立 DQ 入場檢查表（DQ entry checklist），提前確認所有前提要件，避免 DQ 被迫中斷。

📄 追溯矩陣在 DQ 中的應用

追溯矩陣在 DQ 中扮演核心工具角色，典型欄位包括：

  • URS 需求編號 & 描述
  • 對應的 CA（關鍵特性）
  • 對應的 CDE（關鍵設計要素）
  • CPP（關鍵製程參數）
  • CQA（關鍵品質屬性）
  • 驗收標準（acceptance criteria）
  • 後續測試引用（IQ/OQ/PQ 協議編號）

再次強調：非法規強制要求，但強烈建議使用。它讓稽核員一眼看清需求→設計→驗證的完整追溯鏈。

🖊 最終 DQ 報告的三方核准

DQ 報告需要由三個部門的適當層級代表核准：

  • 工程（Engineering）：確認設計技術上可行且完整
  • 生產（Manufacturing）：確認設計符合操作需求
  • 品質（Quality Unit）：確認設計符合品質、法規要求

三方核准使 DQ 報告成為正式的「品質系統文件」，不同於 DR 報告（可能只是工程會議記錄）。

🏢 CDMO 應用：DQ 在資本專案中的定位

在 CDMO 的資本專案中，DQ 通常落在以下節點：

  • IFC 圖發布後：設計已凍結，可進行最終 DQ 審查。
  • 採購/長交期設備訂單前：確認設計中的 CAs/CDEs 已鎖定，避免事後設計變更（costly change orders）。
  • FAT 前：DQ 核准代表設計面已完整驗證，FAT 可聚焦於製造品質確認。

DQ 報告也是 FDA/EMA 稽查時「設計文件包」的核心元件之一。

5.5

Timing of DR and DQ — 時序規劃

Table 5.1: Project phases and DR/DQ deliverables

5.5 Timing of DR and DQ — Table 5.1 (p.40)

Table 5.1 summarizes the key project phases and the corresponding DR and DQ deliverables. The table illustrates the timing of these activities throughout the design lifecycle, from project initiation through detailed design completion.

Deliverable / Activity Project Initiation Concept BOD (Basis of Design) Detailed Design
URS Initiated Developed & Approved Reviewed / Updated Final / Approved
System Classification — Preliminary Confirmed Finalized
System Risk Assessment (SRA) — Initiated Developed (IFD-based) Updated & Finalized
Design Review (DR) — Concept DR BOD DR (IFD documents) Detailed Design DR (IFC documents)
Design Documents Project brief Concept drawings / scope options IFD package (P&IDs, layouts, specs) IFC package (construction-ready)
Design Qualification (DQ) — — — (DQ planning may begin) DQ executed & approved (direct impact systems only)
C&Q Plan — Initiated Developed Approved
Traceability Matrix — — Draft (CAs/CDEs identified) Finalized (acceptance criteria defined)

Note: Table 5.1 content reconstructed from Chapter 5 descriptions. Original table appears on p.40 of ISPE Baseline Guide Vol.5, 2nd Edition.

解讀視观 Commentary

🕐 Table 5.1 關鍵洞察：時序的重要性

Table 5.1 傳達了一個核心訊息：DR/DQ 活動要與設計進度同步推進，而非在設計完成後才補做。

  • 概念階段：已開始 URS 和概念 DR——早期識別設計方向的品質風險。
  • BOD 階段：以 IFD 文件進行 DR——這是最重要的 DR 時機，因為此時設計變更成本最低。
  • 詳細設計階段：DR 確認最終 IFC 文件；DQ 正式執行——這是直接影響系統的品質「里程碑關卡」。

⚠ 常見錯誤：過晚執行 DR

許多企業的 DR 只在 IFC（建造用圖）完成後才進行，此時發現設計缺陷的修改成本極高：

  • 設計變更單（Change Orders）費用高昂
  • 施工進度被迫延誤
  • 可能觸發重新採購已訂購的設備

💡 最佳實踐：在 IFD 階段即進行關鍵 DR，趁設計還有彈性時解決問題。

🏢 CDMO 資本專案時序應用

典型 CDMO 新建工廠或改造專案的 DR/DQ 里程碑建議：

  • FEL-1（Front-End Loading 1） = 概念階段 → 完成概念 DR
  • FEL-2（BOD 完成） → 完成 BOD DR，確認所有系統分類和 SRA
  • FEL-3（詳細設計完成） → 完成最終 DR；對直接影響系統執行 DQ；取得三方（Engineering/Mfg/QA）核准
  • FAT/SAT 前 → DQ 報告必須已核准，作為進入 IQ/OQ 的先決條件

💰 思考練習

在您的機構中，DR 是否有跟上設計進度？以下是自我評估問題：

  • 上次 DR 是在 IFD 還是 IFC 之後才做？
  • DR 有 QA 代表參與嗎（至少品質導向的 DR）？
  • DR 結果有被整合進追溯矩陣，並連結到後續 IQ/OQ/PQ 測試嗎？
  • DQ 是正式的三方核准文件，還是只是一份工程報告？

💡 整章總結比喻

把整個 C&Q 設計驗證過程想像成蓋房子：

  • URS = 屋主的需求清單（幾房幾廳、要有停車位）
  • SRA = 風險評估（土地是否有問題、颱風設計標準）
  • DR = 建築師審查圖紙（所有人一起看，確認沒有設計缺陷）
  • DQ = 消防局/結構技師的正式認可（只看安全關鍵項目，蓋章核准）

DQ 的「蓋章」讓建造得以正式啟動，後續 IQ/OQ/PQ 才能按計劃進行。

📚 章節總結 — Chapter 5 Key Takeaways

  • DR vs. DQ 的根本區別：DR 覆蓋所有設計面向，適用所有系統；DQ 只針對直接影響系統的 CAs/CDEs，需 Engineering + Manufacturing + QA 三方核准。兩者是「各別文件」而非「各別活動」，應最小化重複工作。
  • 三階段設計流程：概念 → BOD（含 IFD 文件）→ 詳細設計（含 IFC 文件）。DR 應在每個階段進行，DQ 在詳細設計完成後正式執行。
  • DR 基於 ICH Q9 原則：DR 的投入程度與記錄詳細度應與風險等級相稱。低風險系統可用會議記錄；高度關鍵系統需更詳細的 DR 文件。QA 應至少出席品質導向的 DR。
  • DQ 的四項前提要件：(1) 已核准 URS；(2) 功能需求（自動化系統）；(3) 含 CAs/CDEs 的 SRA；(4) 所有相關開放問題已關閉的 DR 記錄。
  • 追溯矩陣（Traceability Matrix）：非法規強制要求，但是連結 URS 需求 → CAs/CDEs → 驗收標準的最佳工具，在 DQ 中強烈建議使用，也為後續 IQ/OQ/PQ 奠定基礎。
  • 時序是關鍵：Table 5.1 顯示 DR/DQ 應與設計進度同步，而非事後補做。在 BOD/IFD 階段即進行關鍵 DR，可大幅降低後期設計變更成本。
6

Chapter 6: C&Q Planning

C&Q 計劃 | p41-p48

ISPE Baseline Guide Vol.5 — Commissioning and Qualification (2nd Edition)

Chapter 6: C&Q Planning
Pages 41–48  |  Chapter 6 of ISPE Baseline Vol.5

學習目標 (Learning Objectives)

  1. 理解 C&Q Plan（確效與委試計畫） 的目的、效益，以及在整體專案生命週期中的角色與位置。
  2. 掌握 C&Q Plan 的審批時序規則（計畫 → 測試指令 → 執行），並了解為何此順序在業界常被違反。
  3. 了解 C&Q Plan 的核心內容要素：範疇、策略、文件管理、測試描述，以及差異處理程序。
  4. 熟悉 Table 6.1 核准矩陣的架構與使用方式，包括事前審批者（Pre-Approver）與事後審批者（Post-Approver）的區別。
  5. 將 C&Q Planning 的原則應用於 CDMO 實務場景，例如新充填線安裝或公用系統擴建專案。

本章節目錄

6.1 Introduction 6.1.1 Purpose & Benefits 6.2 C&Q Planning Approach 6.2.1 Timing 6.2.2 Lifecycle 6.2.3 Elements 6.3 C&Q Plan 6.3.1 Scope 6.3.2 Strategy 6.3.3 Documentation 6.3.4 Contents 6.4 Approval Matrix
6.1

Introduction

Why planning is essential — C&Q as a managed engineering activity from URS to acceptance

Original Text (English)

6.1 Introduction

C&Q is a planned, documented, and managed engineering activity that starts with the establishment of the URS and continues to start-up and acceptance and release of systems. A well-planned program is essential and leads to an efficient, "right the first time", and cost-effective C&Q effort; the result is the delivery of systems that operate in a safe manner, meet established design requirements and stakeholder expectations, and are suitable for the intended purpose.

Planning provides the ties between process understanding and system design; it focuses qualification efforts to enhance the likelihood that the system will deliver quality products while maintaining a controlled operating state. It also acts as a means for communication between members of the multidisciplinary project team.

This chapter focuses on the formal C&Q Plan. There are other plans that can be generated, such as overall project plans or cleanliness plans, which have great value but are not covered in this chapter. Refer to Chapter 21 (Appendix 7) for a listing of supporting plans and general concepts for each.

Regulatory expectations for C&Q planning are described in Chapter 15 (Appendix 1).

中文解說 Commentary

C&Q 的本質：有計畫的工程活動

ISPE 強調 C&Q（Commissioning and Qualification，委試與確效）不是一個「做完測試就結束」的程序，而是一個有計畫、有文件、有管理的工程活動，從 URS 寫好的那一天起，一直延伸到系統正式接收釋放為止。

這個視角很重要：它把 C&Q 定位為工程專案的一部份，而不是質量部門在最後補做的文書工作。

比喻：蓋房子的施工計畫

C&Q Planning 就像建設公司在動工前要先做的「施工計畫書」。

你不能邊做邊想：「今天澆混凝土，明天再決定要不要驗收」。每一道工序都要排程、明確誰負責、何時完成、驗收標準是什麼。

C&Q Plan 就是那份施工計畫書，確保整個團隊（工程、品保、生產、廠商）都照同一份劇本走。

注意：本章聚焦正式 C&Q Plan

書中提醒讀者，還有很多其他計畫（例如清潔計畫、整體專案計畫），但本章只討論正式的 C&Q Plan。其他計畫請參考 Chapter 21（Appendix 7）。

6.1.1

Purpose and Benefits

Integrated schedule, critical path method, cross-team communication, and stakeholder expectations

Original Text (English)

6.1.1 Purpose and Benefits

A well-conceived and executed C&Q Plan can greatly facilitate a timely and cost-effective qualification effort. It is essential to have excellent communication, planning, and coordination between the Quality Unit, vendors, operations, automation, engineering, construction, commissioning, and qualification personnel, to name a few, to deliver a project on time, within budget, and meeting all expectations. A C&Q plan facilitates this communication.

An important secondary goal of the C&Q Plan is to foster an interdisciplinary team approach to C&Q. Well-planned project logistics are crucial to the success of every project. A well-coordinated effort leads to a high quality, effective, and efficient C&Q project.

A single, integrated, overall schedule should be developed with input from the entire project team. This schedule should cover all systems (utilizing defined system boundaries as discussed in Section 3.2) and phases of the projects lifecycle from construction to Process Validation/PPQ completion. This schedule should be updated and issued regularly. These updates should not drive a C&Q Plan revision, but the C&Q Plan should identify how the schedule updates will be captured and communicated.

An integrated schedule, using a critical path method, can increase the awareness of dependent activities and provide a clear understanding of the critical path. Including all project team members in the schedule development will engage the team members and foster better planning. All team members should comprehend the schedule format. Ordering long delivery time items early can help timelines, but consideration should be made to ensure the process requirements for those items are understood and included in the requisition. Understanding when to engage support for C&Q helps to support the success of the project.

A well-planned effort can ensure that the user, business, regulatory, and patient expectations are met. All efforts to ensure the system is suitable for the intended purpose (e.g., start-up, balancing, trial runs, establishing maintenance programs) should be included in the planning phase since this is where the formality of the documentation can be established. These expectations include:

  • Systems are delivered on time and within budget
  • Systems meet approved user requirements and are suitable for the intended purpose
  • Stakeholder needs, including speed to market, are met
  • Products produced from the systems meet defined quality standards
中文解說 Commentary

C&Q Plan 的三大效益

  • 跨部門溝通橋樑：讓品保、廠商、生產、自動化、工程、施工等不同團隊，有共同遵循的計畫文件
  • 跨學科團隊整合：打破部門壁壘，建立一個整合性的 C&Q 專案團隊
  • 利害關係人期望管理：準時交付、符合預算、符合預期用途、確保產品品質

關鍵術語：Critical Path Method（關鍵路徑法）

CPM 是專案管理中常用的排程技術。它找出專案中最長的依賴活動鏈，這條鏈上任何一個活動的延遲，都會直接導致整個專案延遲。

在 C&Q 中的意義：例如，HVAC 調試必須在無菌充填區 IQ 之前完成；IQ 完成才能做 OQ；OQ 完成才能做 PQ。這條鏈就是關鍵路徑。提早辨識它，才能及早採購長交期設備、安排人力資源。

比喻：排程失控的後果

想像一條填充線安裝專案，業主希望 10 月開始 PQ，但沒有人提前排好關鍵路徑：結果 8 月才發現水系統的 EP（認可廠商評估）還沒做，設備還沒到廠，OQ 就不能開始。

Critical Path Method 的目的，就是讓這種「到最後才發現問題」的狀況，在計畫階段就被發現和處理。

重點：排程更新 ≠ 計畫修訂

ISPE 特別指出：定期更新排程是正常的，但排程更新不應觸發 C&Q Plan 的版本修訂。C&Q Plan 應說明排程更新如何被紀錄與傳達，而非每次更新排程就重新審批計畫。這是很實用的操作建議。

6.2

C&Q Planning Approach

Level of planning based on project size, complexity, and risk — when a separate C&Q Plan is needed

Original Text (English)

6.2 C&Q Planning Approach

The amount of planning, documentation, reporting, and level of detail of the C&Q Plan should be based on expectations of the organization/site, size and complexity of the system or project, and the potential impact on product quality and patient safety.

A C&Q Plan should not repeat details that are in other documents but needs to capture the organization of those documents in order to facilitate an efficient project execution.

A separate C&Q Plan is not always necessary. Aspects of C&Q planning can be included with other documents, such as a validation plan or change control. For example, the simple change of adding a small system would not need a separate C&Q Plan; the requirements could be incorporated into a change control plan. More complex systems would benefit from a separate C&Q Plan, for example, the installation of a filling line with terminal sterilization and secondary packaging or the doubling in capacity of a manufacturing site including additional utilities to support the expansion.

中文解說 Commentary

計畫深度應與專案規模成比例

ISPE 採取風險比例原則（risk-proportionate approach）：計畫的詳盡程度取決於：

  • 組織/廠址的期望（公司內規）
  • 系統或專案的大小與複雜度
  • 對產品品質和病患安全的潛在影響

什麼情況需要獨立的 C&Q Plan？

不需要獨立計畫（納入變更管制即可）：
新增一台小型輔助設備（例如，更換一台蠕動泵）

需要獨立 C&Q Plan：

  • 新安裝含最終滅菌和二次包裝的充填線
  • 廠址產能倍增，含公用系統擴建（WFI、純蒸汽、潔淨空調）

判斷標準：專案越複雜、影響越大，越需要一份獨立的正式計畫文件來統籌管理。

C&Q Plan 不應重複其他文件

計畫的功能是「組織文件架構」，而非「複製文件內容」。它告訴讀者「哪個文件在哪裡、誰負責、什麼時候要完成」，而不是把 URS 或 SRA 的內容再抄一遍。

6.2.1

Timing of C&Q Plan

The approval sequence rule: C&Q Plan approved BEFORE test instructions, test instructions approved BEFORE execution

Original Text (English)

6.2.1 Timing of C&Q Plan

In an overall scheme, the creation of the C&Q Plan falls in the process map as shown in Figure 1.1 (Chapter 1).

It is important to note that C&Q planning begins prior to the creation of any formal written plans. C&Q planning starts during the planning and design phase of a project and continues through project implementation. A documented strategy may be developed as a precursor to a C&Q Plan, to help align team members with the process and personnel who will be responsible for C&Q.

A C&Q Plan should begin early in a project in the concept or early basic engineering phase.

The C&Q Plan needs to be approved before the respective testing documents (i.e., test instructions) are approved, and such test instructions need to be approved before test execution starts to support qualification. This is recommended for commissioning plans and test instructions.

The C&Q Plan should address how existing test documentation and test results from commissioning (including FAT, SAT, etc.) are referenced in qualification documents, as appropriate.

中文解說 Commentary

審批時序規則（業界最常被違反的規定之一）

ISPE 明確規定了三個必須依序進行的審批步驟：

  1. C&Q Plan 審批完成（計畫核准）
  2. 測試指令（Test Instructions）審批完成（IQ/OQ/PQ Protocol 核准）
  3. 開始執行測試

這個序列不能顛倒，更不能跳過。

為什麼業界常違反這個規則？

在實際 CDMO 或設備安裝專案中，常見情況：

  • 設備到廠了，工程師急著「先跑一下 IQ」，Protocol 還在品保審批中
  • C&Q Plan 還沒最終核准，但委試工程師已開始 FAT
  • 為了趕上 Launch 時程，OQ 執行完才補做 Protocol 審批

這些行為在法規稽查時，都可能被認定為程序不合規（Protocol not approved prior to execution）。一旦被 FDA 483 或 Warning Letter 點名，補救成本遠大於當初多等幾天審批的時間。

計畫應從概念階段或基本工程初期開始

C&Q 計畫不是在設備到廠前幾週才開始寫的文件。ISPE 建議在概念階段（Concept Phase）或基本工程初期（Early Basic Engineering）就開始規劃。

這是因為：URS 的品質要求、系統分類結果、SRA 的 CDE 辨識，都必須在計畫階段就確定，才能定義測試的範疇與接受標準。

6.2.2

Lifecycle of C&Q Plan

Kept up-to-date through the project; minor departures documented in Qualification Summary Report

Original Text (English)

6.2.2 Lifecycle of C&Q Plan

The C&Q Plan is not finalized until after the risk management process has reached a point to capture the impact of product quality decisions or of establishing the CDEs.

C&Q Plans are expected to be kept up-to-date as changes to the project are made. Revisions of the C&Q Plan may be necessary as new information is learned or as modifications to the design are made, e.g., changes in scope (additions or removals), timing, or identification of additional CAs/CDEs.

Approval is recommended for these early plans and for subsequent changes made by the revision process; this ensures agreement at various stages of the C&Q approach. Changes to the C&Q Plan should be reviewed and approved by the original approvers (or their designate) and a revision history should be maintained of significant changes to the Plan.

It should be noted that revisions may not always be necessary. Minor departures from the C&Q Plan may be documented in the Qualification Summary Report with appropriate justification and rationale, as deemed appropriate by the project team.

At the end of a project, a written document capturing the completion and closure of the project should be created. See Chapter 8 for more details regarding acceptance and release.

Changes to the C&Q Plan should be handled under change management (as discussed in Chapter 12) to ensure that as changes are implemented, the impact to C&Q efforts is addressed.

中文解說 Commentary

C&Q Plan 是活文件（Living Document）

C&Q Plan 不是寫完就鎖起來的文件。隨著專案進展，當設計變更、範疇調整、新的 CDE 被辨識時，計畫需要相應更新。

版本修訂原則：

  • 有重大變更 → 啟動正式版本修訂，由原核准者（或其代理人）審批
  • 輕微偏離 → 可記錄在 Qualification Summary Report（確效總結報告）中，加上理由說明，不一定要重改計畫

關鍵術語：Qualification Summary Report（確效總結報告）

確效總結報告是在整個確效活動完成後，彙整所有測試結果、偏差處理、執行摘要的最終報告文件。

ISPE 允許將輕微偏離 C&Q Plan 的情況記錄在這份報告中（加上說明），而不需要每次都修訂 C&Q Plan。這是一個務實的彈性規定。

計畫變更須走變更管理

C&Q Plan 的任何修訂都應透過變更管理（Change Management，Chapter 12）處理，以確保變更對 C&Q 工作的影響被適當評估和記錄。

這防止了「私下改計畫卻沒通知品保」的情形發生。

6.2.3

Elements to be Addressed

Scope of testing, document source identification, coordination with overall project execution plan

Original Text (English)

6.2.3 Elements to be Addressed

This section is intended to be a discussion of the elements that need to be addressed as part of C&Q planning, not the documents where they are captured.

6.2.3.1 Scope of Testing

System classification (as described in Chapter 3) identifies which systems require qualification. The System Risk Assessment (as described in Chapter 4) identifies which elements in those systems require qualification. The URS (as described in Chapter 2) and System Risk Assessment establish the scope of testing for qualification. The equipment specifications establish the scope of testing for commissioning.

The testing approach is based on the most efficient method to test the system and should be captured in the C&Q Plan. If systems are tested separately, the C&Q Plan should include a final test verifying that all systems are able to work together prior to acceptance and release. If PPQ is included in a separate plan, the linkage to the execution of that critical phase should be captured.

6.2.3.2 Identification of Document Source

Engineering firms, vendors, contractors, quality, engineering, and owners provide the documentation necessary for design, construction, commissioning, qualification, operation, and technical support of the systems. It is important to identify the documentation source early in the process so the impact on the testing of the system is understood and thus the quality of the documentation understood. This understanding will allow for utilization of the documentation to support qualification.

For example, the decision should be made during planning if any FAT, construction, SAT, or commissioning testing results and documentation will be used to satisfy the requirements to declare the system qualified or suitable for the intended purpose. This decision is based on vendor assessments for C&Q documentation purposes (as described in Chapter 10) and the criticality of the testing. It is often desirable to minimize the amount of retesting performed.

The C&Q Plan may also address the expectations of the documentation. It should be noted that pristine documentation, i.e., documentation that has minimal errors or corrections, is not essential but the documentation needs to be easy to follow and understand.

6.2.3.3 Coordination with Overall Project Execution Plan

Another important aspect is working with the project manager to ensure that the planning of C&Q activities, whether a separate plan or part of another plan, fits seamlessly into the overall Project Execution Plan. C&Q activities should be properly reflected in the Project Execution Plan at an appropriate level of detail to be able to identify interdependencies between C&Q as well as to other project activities. Commissioning is normally occurring throughout construction and needs to occur when it is appropriate; e.g., commissioning the agitation system cannot be completed until it is energized.

Having these activities in the Project Execution Plan supports:

  • Coordination of test activities among C&Q to prepare for FAT or SAT events
  • Ability to schedule sequence of testing for multiple systems (e.g., electrical supply before energizing a system)
  • Schedule review cycles for qualification documents with Quality Unit representatives
中文解說 Commentary

測試範疇的決定邏輯

測試範疇（Scope of Testing）由以下文件決定：

  • 系統分類（System Classification） → 決定哪些系統需要確效（直接影響 vs 非直接影響）
  • 系統風險評估（System Risk Assessment, SRA） → 決定系統中哪些元素需要確效（CDE 的辨識）
  • URS + SRA → 共同建立確效測試的範疇
  • 設備規格 → 決定委試（Commissioning）的測試範疇

文件來源決策（Document Source）

規劃階段必須決定：FAT、SAT、或委試文件是否可以用來支援確效結論？

這個決定的依據是：

  • 廠商評估（Vendor Assessment）的結果 → 廠商文件品質是否足夠？
  • 測試的關鍵性 → 是否涉及 CDE？

目的是減少重複測試（minimize retesting）。如果 FAT 已有充分記錄，就不需要到廠再做一次相同測試。

文件不需要完美無缺

ISPE 明確指出：「Pristine documentation is NOT essential.」 文件允許有更正記錄，重點是易於閱讀和理解。這是一個務實的立場，避免因過度追求「無更正文件」而浪費資源，或更糟糕地：將更正直接消除而非正式記錄。

與整體 Project Execution Plan（PEP）的協調

C&Q 活動必須整合進整體 PEP（專案執行計畫），這樣才能：

  • 識別 C&Q 活動與建設、採購、操作之間的相依性（interdependencies）
  • 合理排序多系統的測試順序（先供電，才能啟動）
  • 為品保文件審查排出時間窗口（QA review cycle）

CDMO 實務上，這意味著 C&Q 計畫工程師需要參加 PEP 的排程會議，而不是單獨在品保部門內部討論。

6.3

C&Q Plan

Typical contents of a C&Q Plan — the 8 key elements

Original Text (English)

6.3 C&Q Plan

The C&Q Plan typically encompasses:

  • Description of the scope of the plan (identification of the systems included)
  • Description of the C&Q execution strategy
  • C&Q related documentation requirements for each identified system (e.g., URS, FAT, SAT, Installation/Operational Testing, PQ, SOPs, etc.)
  • Roles and responsibilities, e.g., approval matrix (see Section 6.4 for example)
  • Reference necessary C&Q document templates (e.g., test instructions, test scripts, reports, discrepancy form)
  • Planned inspections and tests
    • Documentation requirements for the inspection and test results
    • Reference procedures for inspections and tests to be performed
    • Identification of SMEs for review of the inspection and test results
    • For tests to be used to support qualification, include the acceptance criteria to be met for all CDEs (Note: The plan may defer to individual test instructions)

The specific structure and content of the C&Q Plan is typically driven by organization/site requirements.

中文解說 Commentary

C&Q Plan 的典型內容架構

一份完整的 C&Q Plan 應包含以下主要元素：

  1. 計畫範疇（系統清單）
  2. 執行策略與方法
  3. 各系統的文件需求清單（URS、FAT、SAT、IQ/OQ/PQ、SOP）
  4. 角色與責任（含核准矩陣）
  5. 文件範本參考
  6. 計畫中的檢查與測試（含驗收標準、負責 SME、測試程序參考）

CDMO 應用：新充填線 C&Q Plan 範例架構

以 CDMO 承接新無菌充填線安裝專案為例，C&Q Plan 可能包含：

  • 範疇：充填機、凍乾機、去熱原烘箱、CIP/SIP 系統、隔離器（直接影響）；HVAC、純水系統、壓縮空氣（直接影響）；冷卻水（非直接影響）
  • 策略：凍乾機採 FAT（在廠商場地）+ SAT + IQ/OQ/PQ；充填機採廠商 FAT + 現場 IQ/OQ/PQ
  • 文件矩陣：列出每個系統的文件清單、負責部門、預計完成日期
  • 核准矩陣：依 Table 6.1 格式，明確每份文件的事前/事後核准者

CDE 的接受標準可延伸到個別測試指令

計畫中對 CDE 測試的接受標準，可以「轉引」（defer）至個別的測試指令（test instructions）中定義，不一定要在 C&Q Plan 中一一列明。這給了實際操作上的彈性。

6.3.1

Scope of the Effort

Both direct and not-direct impact systems; PQ for utilities; cycle development considerations

Original Text (English)

6.3.1 Scope of the Effort

The scope captures all systems that are covered within the scope of the project. This includes both direct impact and not direct impact systems (as described in Chapter 3). More details are provided below.

6.3.1.1 Additional Scope Considerations

PQ activities may be included in a C&Q Plan for pharmaceutical grade utilities (e.g., WFI, Purified Water), support systems (e.g., autoclaves, depyrogenation ovens, washers), environments (e.g., non-environmental monitoring in clean rooms), and non-product PQ (e.g., media fills for filling lines). Individual organizations/sites need to decide if these are in qualification or a separate validation program.

Cycle development for areas such as sterilization and cleaning also need to be considered. Cycle development can identify factors that require qualification or that modify the qualification. These are often executed after the equipment qualification effort. It is recommended to not perform the final qualification testing until after cycle development since changes identified by cycle development can be captured in the Engineering Change Management system (see Chapter 12). Individual organizations/sites need to decide if cycle development is part of the C&Q effort and capture the decision in the C&Q Plan.

中文解說 Commentary

範疇包含直接與非直接影響系統

C&Q Plan 的範疇不能只列直接影響（Direct Impact）系統。非直接影響（Not Direct Impact）的系統（如冷卻水、普通壓縮空氣）雖然不需要正式確效，但仍在 C&Q 計畫的管理範圍內，需要委試（Commissioning）。

PQ 活動可納入 C&Q Plan

以下項目的 PQ（Performance Qualification，性能確效）可以（但不強制）納入 C&Q Plan 管理：

  • 藥品級公用系統：WFI（注射用水）、純水（PW）
  • 支援系統：高壓滅菌器、去熱原烘箱、清洗機
  • 環境：無菌室的環境確認（非環境監控）
  • 非產品 PQ：無菌模擬充填（Media Fill）

各廠址需自行決定這些是否納入 C&Q 計畫，或另立獨立驗證計畫（Validation Program）。

周期開發應在最終確效測試之前完成

ISPE 特別建議：不要在 Cycle Development（周期開發）完成之前就進行最終確效測試。因為周期開發（如滅菌周期、清潔周期）可能發現需要修改設計的問題。若先做確效再改設計，就必須重做確效，成本很高。

正確順序：Cycle Development → 確認無設計變更 → 最終 IQ/OQ/PQ

6.3.2

Strategy and Approach

Commissioned-only vs commissioned+qualified; vendor documentation criteria; testing dependencies

Original Text (English)

6.3.2 Strategy and Approach

The C&Q Plan needs to define C&Q strategy and approach to aid in overall project planning. The C&Q Plan captures whether systems will be commissioned only or commissioned and qualified. The system classification (as described in Chapter 3) and System Risk Assessment (as described in Chapter 4) have identified the CPPs and CDEs that need to be supported by the C&Q effort.

The rigor of testing depends on the user requirements, CDEs, and system characteristics (e.g., packaged system, modular, or installed system) as well as experiences with the vendor.

An aspect that needs to be captured in the C&Q Plan is the identification of the documentation source that will be utilized to satisfy the C&Q requirements. Appropriate prerequisites, means, and checks should be described in the plan to ensure reliable results, e.g., the pre-approval of vendor/manufacturer documents by an SME. If vendor-provided documentation or testing is to be accepted to support qualification, the criteria for determining if it can be utilized needs to be established in the Plan. Refer to Chapter 10 for details regarding vendor assessments for C&Q documentation purposes.

The C&Q Plan should also capture if individual pieces of equipment or systems will be tested separately because they are delivered and installed at different times by different vendors or if testing will be executed once all components are installed. Dependencies within the scope of work (e.g., if one system needs to be tested before another system is tested) should also be included.

中文解說 Commentary

策略決策：只做委試，還是委試＋確效？

C&Q Plan 必須明確定義每個系統的策略：

  • Commissioned Only（僅委試）：適用於非直接影響系統（如冷卻水、普通電力）
  • Commissioned + Qualified（委試＋確效）：適用於直接影響系統（如無菌充填線、WFI 系統）

決定依據：系統分類（Chapter 3）＋ SRA 的 CDE 辨識結果。

確效嚴格度取決於多項因素

測試的嚴格程度（rigor of testing）受以下因素影響：

  • 使用者需求（URS 的要求）
  • CDEs 的數量和關鍵性
  • 系統特性（套裝系統 vs 模組化 vs 現場安裝）
  • 與廠商的過往合作經驗（有認可的廠商，文件可更多採用）

廠商文件使用標準：提前在計畫中定義

如果計畫採用廠商文件（如 FAT 報告、廠商 IQ）來支援確效結論，必須在計畫中預先定義使用標準，例如：

  • 廠商文件須由 SME 事前審批（pre-approval）
  • 廠商評估報告（Vendor Assessment）需達到什麼標準才能採用其文件
  • 接受哪種程度的廠商資質（Audit 結果、ISO 認證等）

這些標準必須在計畫中寫明，而非事後補救。

測試依賴性（Dependencies）必須明確記錄

例如：HVAC 系統的 OQ 必須在無菌室壓差和換氣次數確認之後，充填線的 IQ 才能開始。這種依賴關係必須在 C&Q Plan 中明確記載，以支援正確的測試排序。

6.3.3

Documentation

Document matrix, electronic storage, 14-item tracking list

Original Text (English)

6.3.3 Documentation

The C&Q Plan should capture document planning and control as well as execution of testing. The C&Q Plan should reference appropriate document control and content procedures to satisfy engineering, commissioning, qualification, operations, and maintenance requirements. Utilizing electronic storage of documents is recommended as it allows for searching and easier retrieval. If electronic storage will be utilized, ensure the vendors and contracting companies are aware and can support the delivery of their documentation in that means.

The Plan should define responsibilities for document preparation, collection, review and approval, and how the documents will be organized. This Guide recommends that a document matrix be considered as a means of planning and communicating these responsibilities. Documents also need to be tracked to ensure they are completed when they are needed.

Documents that are typically tracked include:

  • URS
  • System Risk Assessments
  • Drawings
  • Equipment specifications including any automation specifications (e.g., functional specifications)
  • Vendor correspondence and transmittals
  • Requests for information
  • Submittals (e.g., shop drawings, manufacturers data sheets, user manuals)
  • Required procedures (e.g., equipment operating procedures, maintenance)
  • Change management (see Chapter 12)
  • Schedules
  • Open items / punch list
  • Commissioning/qualification execution documents
  • Discrepancies
  • Turnover packages
  • Project reports
中文解說 Commentary

關鍵術語：Document Matrix（文件矩陣）

Document Matrix（文件矩陣）是一份表格，列出專案中所有需要的文件，以及每份文件的：

  • 負責編寫部門/人員
  • 審批者（含事前/事後）
  • 預計完成日期
  • 文件狀態追蹤

它是 C&Q Plan 中最實用的工具之一，讓專案經理能一眼掌握所有文件的進度。

關鍵術語：Turnover Package（移交文件包）

Turnover Package（TOP）是施工或安裝完成後，由承包商/廠商移交給業主的文件集合，通常包含：

  • As-built 竣工圖
  • 材質証書（Material Certificates）
  • 焊接記錄（Weld Records）
  • 設備手冊（User Manuals）
  • 校正記錄（Calibration Records）
  • 測試報告（FAT/SAT Reports）

TOP 是 IQ（安裝確效）的重要輸入文件，必須在確效開始前完成並通過審查。

15 類需追蹤的文件

ISPE 列出的追蹤清單涵蓋了整個 C&Q 生命週期的文件類型，從設計前的 URS 到最後的 Project Reports，確保沒有任何文件被遺漏。

特別值得注意的是清單中包含了：

  • Punch List（待辦清單）：施工中發現的缺失項目
  • Discrepancies（偏差）：測試中的偏差記錄
  • Turnover Packages（移交文件包）：正式的系統移交文件

建議採用電子文件儲存

ISPE 建議使用電子儲存（如 EDMS，電子文件管理系統）。但要注意：若使用電子系統，必須提前告知所有廠商和承包商，確保他們能以電子格式提交文件。

實務上，在 CDMO 的大型建設專案中，光是追蹤和管理廠商文件，就需要一個專職的文件控制工程師（Document Control Engineer）。

6.3.4

C&Q Plan Contents

System overview, installation phase, operational phase, discrepancy handling

Original Text (English)

6.3.4 C&Q Plan Contents

The C&Q Plan should define the systems that will be commissioned and qualified based on the system or area boundaries. The plan should include a description of systems including their means of automation. The system overview should be a high-level process narrative, including system boundaries, based on operational/functional requirements. The C&Q team representatives should provide input in defining system boundaries (which can be in a system description, marked on P&IDs, or highlighted on system drawings) in the early project phases to develop an executable plan. It is often possible to gather much of the system overview information from other project documentation.

The C&Q Plan should address the level of testing for each system. This may range from detailed descriptions to references to standard tests. An alternative is to provide only high-level descriptions in the C&Q Plan and leave the detailed descriptions to execution documents. The selected approach should increase the level of efficiency and effectiveness. The plan should also include project schedules by system (as defined by the system boundaries) that capture the dependencies between systems.

Commissioning is an important aspect that requires planning, documentation, and managed resources. Commissioning encompasses testing from FAT, testing during construction, SAT, installation testing, and much of the start-up activities of a project lifecycle including those that will be used to assess the qualification of a direct impact system.

Testing during commissioning should be used to support qualification. If commissioning documentation will be used to support qualification, it is critical to involve the leader of the qualification effort and the Quality Unit in the planning and coordination of commissioning activities and deliverables. A periodic commissioning planning and status meeting should be established.

The C&Q Plan needs to include C&Q steps. There are two typical phases:

  • Installation: Documentation supporting installation is successfully completed. This may include FAT and SAT documentation as well as site commissioning for systems built at the site.
  • Operational: Documentation supporting the functionality and performance of the system after the system has been mechanically completed. This may include testing performed in FAT and SAT.

The plan should address the steps to follow when test results do not meet the expected results or acceptance criteria (discrepancy). There should be a predefined methodology for how discrepancies should be handled (see Section 7.4).

中文解說 Commentary

系統概述（System Overview）的作用

系統概述是一個高層次的系統描述，說明系統的功能、邊界（System Boundary）、及自動化方式。

它可以標示在：

  • 文字說明中
  • P&ID（管道與儀表圖）上劃定範圍
  • 系統圖紙上標示邊界

早期定義系統邊界，是確保後續 IQ/OQ/PQ 不會「有漏網之魚」或「測試範疇過大」的關鍵。

兩個典型測試階段

階段 英文 對應確效活動 包含文件
安裝階段 Installation Phase IQ（安裝確效） FAT、SAT、現場安裝委試
運行階段 Operational Phase OQ（運行確效） 功能測試、性能測試（含部分 FAT/SAT）

委試文件用於確效的必要條件

若委試文件要用來支援確效結論，ISPE 強調：

  • 確效負責人和品質部門必須從計畫階段就參與委試活動的規劃與協調
  • 需要定期召開委試計畫與進度會議

這是因為委試文件的品質（格式、接受標準、審批程序）必須符合確效要求，而這只能在事前約定，不能事後補救。

差異處理程序（Discrepancy Handling）

C&Q Plan 必須預先定義：當測試結果不符合期望或接受標準時，應遵循的處理步驟。

這個「差異處理程序（Discrepancy Handling Procedure）」必須在執行前就寫好（predefined），而不是等到出現偏差才臨時決定怎麼做。詳見 Section 7.4。

6.4

Example Approval Matrix — Table 6.1

Who needs to sign what: Pre-Approvers and Post-Approvers for each C&Q document

Original Text (English)

6.4 Example Approval Matrix

Table 6.1: Example Approval Matrix

General Note: A = Approver

Document Pre-Approvers Post-Approvers Typical Document Preparation Guide Chapter Reference
Quality Unit Production User Technical1 Quality Unit Production User Technical1
C&Q Plan Not applicable A A A1 — — Technical Chapter 6
User Requirements Specification (URS) Not applicable2 A A A1 — — Technical Chapter 2
System Classification Not applicable A A A1 — — Technical Chapter 3
System Risk Assessment (SRA) Not applicable A A A1 — — Quality Unit3 Chapter 4
Design Review (DR) Not applicable — A A1 — — Technical Chapter 5
Design Qualification (DQ) Not applicable A A A1 — — Quality Unit3 Chapter 5
Commissioning inspection/testing documentation (e.g., FAT, SAT) A A1 A A1 — — Technical Chapter 7
Qualification testing documentation where used4 A A A1 A A A1 Quality Unit3 Chapter 7
Turnover Package (TOP) Not applicable — A A1 — — Technical Chapter 7
Commissioning Acceptance and Release Report Not applicable — A A1 — — Technical Chapter 8
Qualification Acceptance and Release Report (including testing from commissioning) Not applicable A A A1 — — Quality Unit3 Chapter 8
Traceability Matrix Not applicable Not applicable — — — — Technical Chapter 8
Vendor Assessment (when vendor documentation utilized for C&Q) Not applicable — A A1 — — Technical Chapter 10

Notes:

  1. Technical includes Engineering, Process, and SME. SME may be Engineering, Automation, Validation, Research and Development, Safety, or Manufacturing Technical Lead; therefore, a second signature is not required from the same discipline.
  2. If the Quality Unit has already approved the source documents from which the quality requirements within the URS were obtained, then the Quality Unit does not need to approve the URS. Quality approval is not required for systems that are not direct impact systems (e.g., boilers).
  3. In many cases, the responsibility for developing the document is given to Technical or Validation.
  4. If IQ and OQ test protocols are required by the organization/site policy, many organizations also require that these protocols are pre and post-approved by the Quality Unit.
中文解說 Commentary

關鍵術語：Pre-Approver vs Post-Approver

事前審批者（Pre-Approver）：在文件執行或發放之前完成審批。確保計畫合理、標準正確、執行前已獲授權。

事後審批者（Post-Approver）：在文件執行完成後審批。確認結果符合要求、偏差已處理、可以接受結論。

最嚴格的文件（如確效測試文件）同時需要事前和事後審批，代表「執行前批准計畫，執行後批准結果」。

核准矩陣的三個角色

  • Quality Unit（品質部門）：負責確保法規符合性和品質標準
  • Production User（生產用戶）：確保系統符合操作需求
  • Technical1（技術）：包含工程、製程、SME（學科專家）；同一學科只需一個簽名

Table 6.1 重要觀察

1. 確效測試文件最嚴格：IQ/OQ/PQ 文件同時需要所有三方（QA、User、Technical）的事前和事後審批，顯示其最高的法規重要性。

2. C&Q Plan 只需事前審批：計畫文件只有「事前」審批，完成後不需要再次審批（因為計畫本身是用來指導後續工作的，不是「結果文件」）。

3. 追溯矩陣不需要正式審批：Traceability Matrix 的核准欄位全部是 "Not applicable"，因為它是技術部門內部使用的追蹤工具。

4. 品保對 URS 的審批有條件性（注2）：若品保已批准過 URS 的來源文件（如品質需求文件），則 URS 本身可不需品保二次審批。

關鍵術語：Traceability Matrix（追溯矩陣）

追溯矩陣是一份文件，將每個 URS 需求項目，追溯到對應的設計文件、風險評估、測試項目，和測試結果。

它回答了「我的每一個使用者需求，是否都有對應的測試驗證？」這個問題。Table 6.1 顯示它不需要正式的 Pre/Post-Approval，由 Technical 負責製作即可。

CDMO 實務：如何使用核准矩陣

對 CDMO 的品保部門而言，Table 6.1 提供了一個最低限度的參考架構。實際操作時：

  • 公司 SOP 可以比 Table 6.1 要求更嚴格（增加更多審批者），但不應比它寬鬆
  • 稽查時，稽查員可能要求展示核准矩陣，並驗證實際簽名記錄是否符合
  • 若某文件缺少 Pre-Approval 就已執行，屬於重大程序違規（Protocol executed without prior approval）
  • 建議在新專案啟動時，以 Table 6.1 為基礎，製作公司特定的核准矩陣

本章重點摘要 (Chapter Summary)

  • C&Q Plan 是專案的核心治理文件，定義範疇、策略、文件要求、角色責任，和測試方法。
  • 審批時序規則：C&Q Plan 核准 → 測試指令核准 → 開始執行。此順序在業界常被違反，但稽查時後果嚴重。
  • 計畫深度應與風險成比例：簡單變更納入變更管制即可；複雜系統（填充線、公用系統擴建）需要獨立的正式 C&Q Plan。
  • C&Q Plan 是活文件：隨專案進展更新；輕微偏離可記錄在 Qualification Summary Report 中，不必每次修訂計畫。
  • Document Matrix（文件矩陣）是管理所有文件進度的最有效工具。
  • Turnover Package（移交文件包）是 IQ 的重要輸入，必須在確效開始前完成。
  • Table 6.1 核准矩陣明確定義了每份文件的事前/事後審批者，是 CDMO 建立公司特定核准程序的最佳參考範本。
  • 確效測試文件是唯一同時需要所有三方（QA、User、Technical）事前和事後審批的文件。
7a

Chapter 7a: C&Q Testing & Documentation (Part 1)

C&Q 測試與文件（上） | p49-p56

pp. 49–56  |  Sections 7.1 – 7.3.2.1

📚 本節學習目標 Learning Objectives

  1. 理解 C&Q 測試的整體方法與範疇——從設計階段起始、以系統驗收結束，靜態與動態測試的分工。
  2. 掌握七大測試原則（工程驅動、預定義標準、培訓、見證要求、供應商評估、變更管理、偏差管理），並能在實務中套用。
  3. 理解品保單位（Quality Unit）在 CDE 測試文件中的四種監督模式，以及多功能 C&Q 團隊的四個角色定位。
  4. 掌握移交文件包（TOP）的目的、15 項典型內容與格式要求，以及「先期交貨檢查（PDI）」的時機與價值。
  5. 能運用 Table 7.2 判斷不同設備類型（高壓滅菌器、HVAC、凍乾機、秤量器、WFI 製造/分配）應採用哪些測試/檢查文件組合。

本節目錄

7.1 Introduction 7.1.1 Approach & Scope 7.1.2 Principles/Concepts 7.1.3 QU Oversight 7.1.4 Roles & Responsibilities 7.2 Prerequisites 7.2.1 Planning 7.2.2–7.2.5 7.3 Execution 7.3.1 Vendor & Construction Docs 7.3.1.1 TOPs 7.3.1.2 Cleaning 7.3.2 Installation Testing 7.3.2.1 PDIs Section Summary
7.1

Introduction

Purpose and safety scope of C&Q testing

Original Text (English)

This chapter provides guidance on C&Q testing and inspection activities and associated documentation for recording the results of the testing/inspection. The goal of testing and inspection is to confirm that the system has been installed and operates to meet the requirements.

Although this chapter provides some general guidance on the safety aspects (e.g., pre-start-up checks), the specific requirements for safety aspects and any local requirements (e.g., signage, access control, equipment protection, Material Safety Data Sheets) are outside the scope of this Guide. It is the responsibility of the system designer to produce a system that is compliant with any related local regulations.

中文解說 Commentary

📌 核心目標

本章聚焦於「測試與檢查」本身及其記錄文件。終極目標簡潔明確：確認系統已按規範安裝，且能按要求運作。

安全面向（如標示、門禁、MSDS）屬各地法規管轄，不在本指南討論範圍內——這是 ISPE 指南常見的「範疇劃定」做法，讀者應特別留意。

💡 比喻說明

C&Q 測試就像新房屋的「竣工驗收」——水電管線有沒有接對、門窗能不能關緊、消防設備是否達標。「安裝符合規範」是 IQ 的任務，「運作符合要求」是 OQ/PQ 的任務，兩者都要有書面記錄才算完成。

7.1.1

Approach and Scope

From design to release — static, dynamic, integrated system testing

Original Text (English)

C&Q testing and documentation starts as early as design and ends with the acceptance and release of the system to the end-user. The process includes planning, document review, and static and dynamic testing of the installation, function, and performance, including testing of any defined worst-case scenarios.

The requirements and stage of the testing/inspection should be predefined in the planning phase to avoid duplication of testing. Testing should only be repeated if necessary. For example, retesting may be necessary if there are changes that may impact a test result, e.g., differing utilities or disconnecting equipment and control systems after FAT to facilitate shipping.

For systems where the automation is an integral part of the system (typical for manufacturing equipment, e.g., WFI storage and distribution system with a dedicated control panel), the entire system is tested as an integrated system comprising the mechanical, electrical, and associated automation.

The scope of testing varies depending on the project scope, but for a new process area would include facilities, utilities, manufacturing equipment and their associated automation or process control systems.

Testing activities and rigor will depend on the type of system (e.g., manufacturing, automated, utilities), potential to impact product quality, and on the project (e.g., green field, brown field, relocation, stick-built, modular, off-the-shelf system).

中文解說 Commentary

📐 靜態 vs 動態測試

  • 靜態測試（Static Testing）：文件審查、圖面核對、材料符合性驗證——設備「靜止」狀態下的確認。
  • 動態測試（Dynamic Testing）：設備實際運轉，測試功能表現與最壞情境——設備「動起來」的確認。

兩者都是 C&Q 的一部分，不可偏廢。

⚠️ 重點：避免重複測試

計劃階段預先定義測試要求，是節省成本的關鍵。但以下情況必須重新測試：

  • FAT 後設備拆解出廠（斷開自控系統）
  • 現場公用設施規格與原設計不符
  • 任何可能影響測試結果的後續變更

🔗 整合系統測試

WFI 分配系統（機械管路 + 電氣 + SCADA）必須作為一個整體來測試，不能只驗機械部分，因為控制邏輯才是實際運作的核心。ISPE 特別強調此點，因為工廠往往分包機械承包商與自動化承包商，容易出現「各自測試、整合漏洞」的問題。

💡 Green field vs Brown field

  • Green field（綠地）：全新廠址，從零開始建設
  • Brown field（棕地）：既有廠址改建或擴建，舊有設備與新建工程並存
  • Modular / Off-the-shelf：模組化採購或現成設備，測試深度相對較低

專案類型直接影響測試嚴格程度（rigor）的設定。

7.1.2

Principles / Concepts

Seven foundational principles for C&Q testing — with Tables 7.1 & 7.2

Original Text (English)

The C&Q testing and documentation approach described in this Guide is based on the following principles:

  • Testing is an engineering driven activity that produces the documented evidence that the installation and operation meet the requirements
  • Documentation standards need to be predefined (see Chapter 13)
  • Training on the documentation standards need to be completed
  • Test witness and the associated notification requirements need to be predefined
  • Where vendor data will be used to support qualification, a vendor assessment needs to be performed (see Chapter 10)
  • System changes need to be managed through Engineering Change Management after approval of the design (see Chapter 12)
  • The process used to manage test failures needs to be predefined (see Section 7.4)

GEP should be defined and applied to all phases of C&Q to provide a high degree of assurance that the system meets user requirements while being cost-effective, compliant with regulations, and appropriately documented.

Organizations/sites may use different terminology and deliverables for C&Q testing/inspection. Table 7.1 provides a comparison of the documentation terminology and Table 7.2 provides example options for inspection/test record documents depending on the system type.

Table 7.1: C&Q Testing and Inspection — Documentation Terminology Comparison

Document Type Description / Context Oversight Level
Document Reviews Confirming that the testing/inspection has been carried out and is recorded per agreed Good Documentation Practices standards (e.g., material certifications, vendor documentation) —
FAT / SAT Testing to demonstrate that a system meets established design requirements and contractual obligations Vendor involvement and technical oversight
Testing and Balancing Reports Testing to demonstrate that a system meets established design requirements Technical oversight
Qualification (CAs/CDEs) Testing to demonstrate that the CAs/CDEs meet established design requirements Quality Unit oversight

Table 7.2: Example Options for Testing/Inspection Record Documents

System Type Option 1 Option 2
Autoclave
  • FAT
  • SAT
  • Cycle Development
  • PQ
  • FAT
  • Installation and Operational Testing Summary
  • Cycle Development
  • PQ
HVAC
(Air Handling Unit up to the final filters)
  • Turnover Package
  • Testing and Balancing Report
  • Turnover Package
  • Commissioning
Lyophilization
  • FAT
  • SAT
  • Cycle Development
  • PQ
  • FAT
  • Commissioning
  • Cycle Development
  • Installation and Operational Testing Summary
  • PQ
Scale

  • Calibration Report
  • Installation Testing Summary

WFI Generation
  • FAT
  • SAT
  • PQ1
  • SAT
  • PQ1
WFI Distribution
  • Turnover Package
  • PQ1*
  • Turnover Package
  • Receipt Inspection

*PQ1 refers to the initial stage of PQ used to demonstrate that the water from the use points meets the specifications. It is completed before the system is used for production.

Other documentation required to support acceptance and release (e.g., drawings and procedures) is managed through other processes (see Chapter 8).

中文解說 Commentary

📋 七大 C&Q 測試原則

  1. 工程驅動（Engineering Driven）：測試是工程活動，產生文件化證據——不是品保「事後審查」，而是工程實作的一部分。
  2. 預定義文件標準：測試前必須確立文件規範（格式、簽名要求等），防止後期補救。
  3. 培訓先行：執行測試前，相關人員需完成文件標準的培訓。
  4. 見證與通知要求預定義：哪些測試需要 QA/客戶見證？通知期多長？都要事先書面規定。
  5. 供應商評估（Vendor Assessment）：若採用廠商數據支持驗證，需先評估廠商能力（見第 10 章）。
  6. 工程變更管理：設計批准後的所有更動，必須走正式的工程變更管理流程。
  7. 偏差管理流程預定義：測試失敗的處理程序需在執行前明確規定（見 7.4 節）。

⚠️ Table 7.1 解讀：三層監督架構

ISPE 用三種「監督深度」區分文件類型：

  • 文件審查（Document Review）：最基本，確認做了且有記錄
  • FAT/SAT：需要廠商參與 + 技術監督
  • 資格確認（Qualification）：需要品保單位監督——這是法規要求的核心

監督層級越高，代表對產品品質影響越直接（CDE 越重要）。

🏭 Table 7.2 實務應用指南

這張表是 CDMO 採購/驗證規劃的實用參考工具：

  • 高壓滅菌器 & 凍乾機：複雜設備，兩個選項都需要 FAT + PQ；Option 2 以 「Installation and Operational Testing Summary」整合 SAT 功能。
  • HVAC（AHU 至末端過濾器）：不一定需要正式 SAT/PQ，以 Turnover Package + Testing and Balancing Report 為主。
  • 秤量器（Scale）：最簡單，Receipt Inspection + Calibration 即可，不需 FAT。
  • WFI 製造系統：Option 2 可省略 FAT（若廠商能在廠內預先完成 SAT）。
  • WFI 分配系統：以 TOP 為核心；Option 2 增加 Receipt Inspection 和 Operational Testing Summary，適合較複雜的迴路設計。

關鍵點：「哪個選項都可以」——重要的是在 C&Q Plan 中提前決定並文件化。

💡 GEP（良好工程實踐）

GEP = Good Engineering Practice，是 ISPE 的核心概念。它不是一份標準文件，而是業界認可的「工程常識」——確保系統設計、安裝、測試兼顧功能、成本、合規與文件品質。

可參考 ISPE GPG: Good Engineering Practice 專刊（文中注 [22]）。

7.1.3

Quality Unit Oversight

Four methods for QA oversight of CDE testing documentation

Original Text (English)

To ensure that the deliverables meet quality expectations, it is good practice to ensure engagement of the Quality Unit as part of an integrated team during the generation of test documentation that will be used to support qualification.

The organization/site needs to determine how Quality Unit oversight will be provided for the testing and associated documentation of the CAs/CDEs. There are several appropriate methods, some of which are described below:

  • Procedures that define GEP and the approach that will be used can be approved by the Quality Unit
    • Standard test procedures (test scripts) and the associated results templates can be pre-approved by the Quality Unit
  • Test strategy and acceptance criteria can be defined in the C&Q Plan for the Quality Unit to approve; the Quality Unit can then review the results as part of the development of the C&Q summary report
  • Testing used to demonstrate that the CAs/CDEs identified in the System Risk Assessment can be covered in an Installation and Operational Qualification (IOQ) protocol for Quality Unit pre and post-execution review and approval
  • Inspection and test records can be marked up to show the tests that are used to demonstrate the CAs/CDEs identified in the System Risk Assessment, or these tests can be assembled in a subsection of the test document for Quality Unit pre and post-execution review and approval
中文解說 Commentary

📊 品保單位監督 CDE 測試的四種模式

ISPE 明確提供四種不同深度的 QA 介入方式，企業可依組織規模與系統風險選擇：

  1. 模式一：程序預核（GEP SOP + 測試腳本預批准）
    QA 事先批准定義 GEP 的 SOP，以及標準測試程序（test scripts）與結果模板。測試期間 QA 不需逐一參與，事後審核結果即可。
    適用：成熟廠房，已建立標準化測試程序的組織
  2. 模式二：C&Q Plan 批准 + 摘要報告審核
    QA 批准 C&Q Plan（含測試策略與接受標準），之後審核 C&Q 摘要報告中的結果。
    適用：中型專案，QA 資源有限，希望分散介入時間點
  3. 模式三：獨立 IOQ 協議（前後審批）
    針對 SRA 識別的 CDE，單獨寫成 IOQ Protocol，QA 執行前批准、執行後審核。最傳統的驗證路徑。
    適用：直接影響系統，法規審查風險較高的場合
  4. 模式四：標記法（Marking up）
    在工程測試記錄上直接標注哪些測試涵蓋哪個 CDE，或將 CDE 相關測試集中於子章節，供 QA 前後批准。最輕量的整合模式。
    適用：商業化廠商設備，測試記錄已相當完整

⚠️ 重點提醒

四種模式並非互斥——同一個專案中，不同系統可採用不同模式。關鍵是在 C&Q Plan 中明確說明選擇哪種模式以及理由。

「整合團隊（integrated team）」的概念貫穿本章：QA 不是在測試完成後才出現的「審判者」，而是從文件生成階段就參與的夥伴。

7.1.4

Roles and Responsibilities

The four C&Q team roles — coordinator, user, technical expert, quality unit

Original Text (English)

The planning, execution, and closeout of testing should be performed by a multidisciplinary team (which includes vendors, engineering, and users) with appropriate Quality Unit oversight. Refer to Section 6.4 (Example Approval Matrix) for an example of the roles and responsibilities for the review and approval of deliverables.

The following roles are typically included in a C&Q team:

  • Testing Coordinator
  • Production user (system user)
  • Technical experts (engineering, automation, validation, or other SME)
  • Quality Unit representative

The testing coordinator represents the project manager in this scope of work. In small projects it is possible that the testing coordinator and the system owner is the same person, whereas for large projects it may be reasonable to designate the role to another individual. The testing coordinator is responsible for the coordination of all testing and ensuring that all tests are completed to meet the schedule.

Production users represent the system owners who will operate the system. In large construction projects, this group may be the engineering representatives that designed the system, due to their knowledge of the planned operation and requirements. Production users are responsible for ensuring the system operates as expected and that documentation (such as operational procedures and batch records) are developed so that they are approved for acceptance and release.

Technical experts are part of or support the testing team, as appropriate. Where testing activities are performed by vendors or third parties, the responsibilities between both parties need to be defined and documented.

The Quality Unit representative provides oversight to ensure that all CAs/CDEs identified in the System Risk Assessment are tested.

中文解說 Commentary

👥 C&Q 團隊四大角色

角色中文名稱核心職責
Testing Coordinator 測試協調員 代表專案經理，協調所有測試活動，確保如期完成
Production User 生產使用者／系統所有人 確保系統運作符合預期；負責 SOP、批次記錄開發至批准
Technical Experts 技術專家（工程/自動化/驗證/SME） 提供專業支援；若由廠商或第三方執行，需書面定義雙方責任
Quality Unit Rep. 品保代表 監督所有 SRA 識別的 CDE 均已測試

💡 角色彈性：小專案 vs 大專案

ISPE 特別說明：小型專案中，Testing Coordinator 與 System Owner 可以是同一人。這體現了指南的務實精神——強調職責被履行，而非強制要求人員分設。

在 CDMO 場景中，測試協調員通常由驗證工程師（Validation Engineer）或專案工程師擔任，而 Production User 則由製造部門的製程工程師代表。

⚠️ 第三方執行測試時的注意事項

當廠商或第三方執行測試時，必須以書面定義雙方責任範圍（例如：誰簽名、誰見證、誰發現問題由誰負責 CAPA）。這通常寫入合約或測試計劃（Test Plan）的 Roles & Responsibilities 章節中。

7.2

Prerequisites

Activities to be completed prior to C&Q testing execution

Original Text (English)

This section describes the activities that should be completed prior to execution of C&Q testing.

中文解說 Commentary

📋 測試前提條件概覽

7.2 節涵蓋五項前提條件：計劃（7.2.1）、培訓（7.2.2）、設計審查/設計確認（7.2.3）、廠商文件運用（7.2.4）、變更管理（7.2.5）。這五項缺一不可，任何一項未完成都可能導致測試結果無效或需要重做。

7.2.1

Planning

PDI and FAT supporting on-site inspection; minimizing repeat testing

Original Text (English)

When C&Q testing is executed as a planned, documented, and managed engineering approach to the start-up and turnover of systems, the result is a safe and functional environment that meets established requirements and stakeholder expectations in a cost-effective way. Where such systems are direct impact (as determined through system classification described in Chapter 3), qualification is required.

The optimum test strategy can minimize repeat testing and help to reduce time in project schedules. For example, Pre-Delivery Inspection (PDI) and FAT may be used to support on-site inspection if appropriate approvals are obtained prior to execution. Components such as instruments can be verified (for aspects such as, e.g., manufacturer, model number, materials of construction) at the vendor site during a PDI or FAT. These checks can be used to support qualification activities, and do not need to be repeated provided there is justification that the functionality will not be affected by any subsequent activities prior to acceptance and release.

See Chapter 6 for details regarding C&Q planning.

中文解說 Commentary

🎯 「最佳測試策略」的核心邏輯

計劃階段的目標是設計一套能最小化重複測試的策略。關鍵工具是 PDI 和 FAT——在廠商廠房完成的測試，若有適當核准，可以作為現場資格確認的依據，不需要到現場重做。

⚠️ 「不需重複」的前提條件

PDI/FAT 數據可替代現場測試，必須滿足：

  1. 測試執行前取得適當批准（appropriate approvals prior to execution）
  2. 有書面理由說明：後續作業（如拆解運輸、現場重新組裝）不會影響已測試的功能

若設備拆解出廠，功能性測試通常需要在現場重做。

🏭 CDMO 採購實務應用

在採購合約中，應明確要求廠商提供 PDI 機會，並列明哪些項目可以在 PDI 期間完成驗證。這能節省現場啟動時間——在廠商廠房發現問題，修復成本遠低於設備到現場後才發現。

7.2.2–5

Training / DR-DQ / Vendor Documentation / Changes

Remaining prerequisites before C&Q test execution

Original Text (English)

7.2.2 Training

Each individual taking a role in the scope of C&Q testing needs have the appropriate training and experience to be able to complete their tasks effectively. Additional training may be required for setup and operation of a specific system, safety, and documentation standards required for a project.

7.2.3 Design Review / Design Qualification

DR/DQ should be completed with approval of the design before purchasing or starting construction of the system. This approved design then provides the basis for any subsequent engineering changes.

Fast track projects may proceed with construction or assembly at risk. However, the basis for approving system design and initiating change management needs to be clearly defined and, for direct impact systems, approved by the Quality Unit.

See Chapter 5 for details regarding DR and DQ.

7.2.4 Use of Vendor Documentation and Testing

Vendor documentation, including protocols and/or test plans (e.g., FAT, SAT), can be used. The strategy should be captured in the C&Q Plan. It is acceptable for the vendor to use their own format for conducting and documenting the testing provided that the vendor company documentation standards are acceptable. The protocol or test plan should be reviewed and approved by the owner and vendor (and Quality Unit if necessary, see Section 7.1.3) before the testing starts.

See Chapter 10 for details regarding the use of vendor documentation.

7.2.5 Changes

Before testing, it is recommended that the relevant System Risk Assessment and change management records are reviewed to ensure that the testing documents reflect the installed system and no changes have been made that may impact the testing.

See Chapter 12 for details regarding change management.

中文解說 Commentary

🎓 7.2.2 培訓要求

「適當的培訓與經驗」是執行 C&Q 測試的基本前提。培訓範圍包含：

  • 特定系統的設置與操作（設備相關）
  • 安全事項（safety）
  • 文件標準（documentation standards）

在法規稽查中，稽查員常會要求查看「執行測試人員的培訓記錄」。這是基本的文件要求，不可輕忽。

💡 7.2.3 DR/DQ 為變更管理的基準點

DR（Design Review）＝ 設計審查（工程內部）
DQ（Design Qualification）＝ 設計確認（品保介入，適用直接影響系統）

批准的設計文件是「基準線（baseline）」——此後所有變更都必須對照這份文件，走工程變更管理（ECM）程序。

快速軌道（Fast Track）風險：若在設計批准前就開始採購或施工（「at risk」執行），組織必須清楚定義風險由誰承擔，且直接影響系統需 QA 批准。

⚠️ 7.2.4 廠商文件的可接受條件

廠商可以用自己的格式進行並記錄測試，但必須滿足：

  1. 廠商的文件標準是可接受的（需事先評估）
  2. 協議/測試計劃在測試開始前由業主和廠商雙方審核批准
  3. 若必要，QA 也需批准（依 7.1.3 的四種模式判斷）

「事後補簽」是稽查常見缺失，應極力避免。

🔄 7.2.5 測試前的變更審查

執行測試前，必須回顧：

  • 系統風險評估（SRA）：確認 CDE 清單是否有更新
  • 變更管理記錄：確認實際安裝的系統與測試文件所描述的一致

這一步驟防止「測試文件版本落後於實際安裝狀態」的常見問題。

7.3

Execution

Testing and inspection activities — scope, sequencing, and phase transitions

Original Text (English)

This section describes the testing and inspection activities. Each organization/project should dictate the testing and inspection required, when it should be performed, and the titles of the record documents.

Tests should be planned and performed so that the results remain valid throughout subsequent phases of the project. Where this is not possible, there should be an evaluation to identify necessary retesting that may be required.

It is not necessary to complete each stage before proceeding to the next (e.g., moving from installation testing to operational testing) as long as:

  • Any outstanding activities and critical discrepancies are noted and tracked with scheduled completion dates.
  • There is documented evidence that the outstanding activities and critical discrepancies will not impact the subsequent work. For direct impact systems, this justification should be approved by the Quality Unit.

See Chapter 8 for information on the review and closure of testing documentation.

中文解說 Commentary

📋 階段轉換的彈性原則

ISPE 允許在前一階段未完全結束時就進入下一階段（例如：安裝測試有少數未完項目，但可以先開始操作測試），前提是：

  1. 所有未完項目必須被記錄並設定完成期限
  2. 書面確認：這些未完項目不會影響後續工作
  3. 直接影響系統：上述確認需 QA 批准

這體現了 ISPE 的風險基礎思維——不是教條式的「一定要完成才能繼續」，而是「有理由、有文件」地管理風險。

⚠️ 「Punch List」管理

未完成項目通常記錄在「Punch List（缺失清單）」中。CDMO 常見實務：分為「關鍵缺失（Critical）」和「非關鍵缺失（Non-Critical）」兩類——關鍵缺失須在下一階段開始前解決，非關鍵缺失可設定後續完成日期。

7.3.1

Vendor and System Construction Phase Documents

Turnover Packages and construction cleaning requirements

7.3.1.1

Turnover Packages (TOPs)

Purpose, typical contents (15 items), and format requirements

Original Text (English)

The purpose of the Turnover Package (TOP) is to provide complete documentation on system components, equipment, and setup. This documentation should also include as-built documentation (agreed upon data, drawings, software, etc.) turned over to the end-user. The TOP may be used throughout the system lifecycle, including ongoing maintenance, system change management, and retirement.

TOPs should be reviewed to ensure that they are complete and represent the installed system. Once completed, the TOP should be accepted and approved. Updates to the TOP should be included in the change management of the system where appropriate. Where documentation from the TOP is used to support operations or represent the basis for qualification, they should be stored in a suitable location that provides adequate control and access.

Contents of the TOP

The TOP contents are usually determined by factors such as organization/site procedures, end-user preferences, GEP, system type, and contracts with the vendors. Information included in a TOP should ensure controlled operation, maintenance, and change. A complex novel system would, therefore, require more types of information than a simple off-the-shelf pump. Due to the variability of systems, vendors, and documentation, the TOP contents need to be flexible.

A typical TOP may include the following lifecycle related documents:

  • Vendor-provided SOPs
  • Spare parts lists
  • Maintenance requirements
  • Maintenance records for work conducted prior to turnover
  • As-built drawings
  • Material of construction certificates
  • Construction test and inspection records (e.g., pressure tests)
  • Loop calibration documentation
  • Material safety data sheets
  • System start-up and shutdown information
  • Warranties
  • Records of adjustable settings
  • Any specific documentation required by local regulations

The TOP contents should be clearly set out and agreed upon by all parties prior to placement of orders. The delivery of the documentation requirements should not present a risk to the project at a later stage, from either content or timing aspects.

TOP Formats

System vendors typically have their own format for TOPs, but the owner organization should clearly define a standardized format that aligns with their document control processes. This can help to ensure consistency between the various TOPs that are submitted. The owner organization can propose a standard format or accept the vendor format if it meets internal requirements. The format might be system-based. The format of TOPs should ensure that they are user friendly with tabulated sections. TOPs should be obtained for all operating systems. To facilitate storage, electronic versions of these documents are often required by the owner organization.

中文解說 Commentary

📦 TOP（移交文件包）是什麼？

TOP 是系統從承包商/廠商移交給業主時所附帶的完整文件集合。它記錄了系統在移交當下的完整狀態，是系統全生命週期（安裝、操作、維護、變更、除役）的重要參考基礎。

TOP 的核心價值：

  • 驗證基礎：As-built 圖面是 IQ 的重要依據
  • 維護支援：備品清單、維護要求讓 PM 部門有所依循
  • 變更管理：設備更改時，TOP 是基準文件
  • 法規合規：材料符合性證書（CoC）支持法規申報

🏭 TOP 15 項清單：CDMO 採購合約必備

下表整理 TOP 典型內容，建議列入採購合約的「Document Requirements」章節：

#TOP 項目用途說明
1廠商提供的 SOP操作、清潔、維護程序
2備品清單（Spare Parts List）採購備品、確保持續供應
3維護要求預防性維護計劃制定
4移交前維護記錄設備歷史記錄起點
5竣工圖面（As-built）IQ 依據、設備更改基準
6材料符合性證書（CoC）法規申報材料符合性驗證
7施工測試/檢查記錄（壓力測試等）IQ 支持性文件
8迴路校正文件（Loop Calibration）儀表校正記錄，CDE 驗證依據
9物質安全資料表（MSDS/SDS）安全合規、廢棄物管理
10啟動/停機程序日常操作指引
11保固文件（Warranties）設備缺陷索賠依據
12可調設定記錄PID 設定值、警報閾值等
13地方法規要求的特定文件依當地法規彈性增補

注意：原文清單共 13 項條目（部分合併計算），總體涵蓋上述所有面向。

⚠️ 關鍵實務：合約下單前確認 TOP 內容

原文明確指出：「TOP 內容應在下訂單前清楚確定並由各方同意」。這是非常重要的採購管理原則：

  • 若等到設備快要交貨才要求廠商補充文件，往往面臨廠商不配合、文件不完整或延遲交付的問題
  • 建議：在 RFQ（報價邀請書）中即列出 TOP 文件清單作為合約要求
  • 付款條款可與 TOP 文件完整性掛鉤

💡 Loop Calibration（迴路校正）是什麼？

Loop = 一個完整的量測/控制迴路，例如：溫度感測器 → 傳輸器 → DCS 訊號輸入卡 → 顯示值。

Loop Calibration 驗證的是這整個迴路的準確性，而非只是感測器本身。這對 CDE（如 WFI 系統溫度、高壓滅菌器壓力）尤其重要，因為任何環節的誤差都可能導致製程失控。

7.3.1.2

Cleaning

Clean construction and post-construction cleaning requirements

Original Text (English)

Where appropriate, the specifications should include clean construction or post-construction cleaning requirements to ensure that systems are ready to test and/or turn over to the owner organization.

Clean construction cleaning requirements may include pre-installation checks/inspection, sealing all openings during construction, etc. Post-construction cleaning may include system cleaning, flushing, sanitation, and passivation, where applicable. The activities should be documented.

Cleaning of any systems that will be moved into a classified area should be performed to prevent contamination.

中文解說 Commentary

🧹 兩種清潔策略

策略定義措施示例
Clean Construction（潔淨建設） 施工過程中即保持潔淨 施工前進行預安裝檢查；施工期間封閉所有開口；分區施工管制
Post-Construction Cleaning（施工後清潔） 施工完成後執行清潔 系統清洗（cleaning）、沖洗（flushing）、殺菌（sanitation）、鈍化（passivation）

⚠️ 進入潔淨區系統的特別注意

移入潔淨區的設備，必須事先進行清潔以防止污染——這不只是文件要求，也是防止整個潔淨區受損的預防措施。此要求應反映在「移入程序（Move-in Procedure）」中，並記錄清潔活動。

7.3.2

Installation Testing

Acceptance Testing, Commissioning, and Qualification phases — mechanical, construction, automation scope

Original Text (English)

The verification of installation provides documentation that the system (or system components) is installed correctly, is ready to start-up, and meets the design requirements including those identified as CDEs.

Testing may be conducted within a single record/plan or separated into FAT, SAT, commissioning, and qualification phases.

The scope of installation testing includes all system installation requirements within the system boundaries, as defined in the specifications or C&Q Plan. Installation testing should include all mechanical, electrical, and automation components, and verify that they are in a state that as-built drawings and punch lists may be established.

Mechanical aspects may include, but are not limited to:

  • Connection to appropriate utilities, services, and IT infrastructure
  • Installation (e.g., pressure testing, slope verification, valve drain verification)
  • System walk down with results marked to record the current system status, redline drawings updated, and identified issues captured as discrepancies

Construction records may include, but are not limited to:

  • Component details
  • Room finishes, e.g., flooring, coving, doors, windows, ceilings, drains, panels, penetrations (wall, ceiling, floor), etc. are installed as specified
  • Construction records, e.g., welding records, material verification, leak/pressure test records, passivation records, component certificates of conformity

Automation and electrical records may include, but are not limited to:

  • Electrical drawing walk down, e.g., data communication, alarm systems connections, cable trays, and conduits are installed and labeled
  • Electrical cabinet construction and installation, e.g., are of appropriate waterproof classification
  • Software version and configuration settings identification and backup
  • Control panel wiring diagrams
  • Screen navigation testing
  • Hard-wired alarm and interlock testing
  • Power/utility loss and recovery testing
  • Communication loss and recovery testing
  • Loop testing, calibration, or tuning
  • Data integrity and audit trail testing
中文解說 Commentary

🏗️ 安裝測試三大範疇

安裝測試（Installation Testing）覆蓋三個面向，缺一不可：

  • 機械面（Mechanical）：管線連接、坡度驗證、壓力測試——確認「裝好了」
  • 施工記錄面（Construction Records）：建築完成度、焊接記錄、材料符合性——確認「裝得對」
  • 自動化/電氣面（Automation & Electrical）：軟體、接線、警報、資料完整性——確認「控制系統正確」

⚠️ 自動化 10 項清單重點解析

  • 軟體版本與備份：必須記錄版本號並建立備份，這是 GAMP 5 的基本要求
  • Hard-wired alarm and interlock testing：硬接線警報（如超溫切斷）必須獨立於軟體測試，確認即使 PLC 故障也能動作
  • Power/Communication loss and recovery：停電或通訊中斷後的系統恢復行為，是製藥設備的關鍵安全測試
  • 資料完整性 & 稽核追蹤（Audit Trail）：FDA/EMA 法規重點，任何人工輸入或系統事件都必須有不可篡改的記錄

💡 Audit Trail（稽核追蹤）是什麼？

Audit Trail 是系統自動記錄的操作日誌，例如：「2026-01-15 14:32, 操作員 A 將溫度設定值從 121°C 改為 123°C」。

FDA 21 CFR Part 11 與 EMA Annex 11 都要求：

  • 記錄不可刪除或修改（只能新增，不能覆蓋）
  • 記錄應包含：時間戳記、使用者 ID、舊值、新值、變更原因（若有）
  • 測試時必須驗證 Audit Trail 功能正確運作且防止篡改

🏭 FAT vs SAT vs Commissioning vs Qualification 的關係

階段地點目的QA 介入
FAT廠商廠房驗收設備符合設計要求視系統而定
SAT業主現場驗收現場安裝視系統而定
Commissioning業主現場系統功能性調試、系統交付工程主導
Qualification (IQ/OQ/PQ)業主現場法規要求的書面確認QA 批准

安裝測試可以整合在一份文件中，也可以分散於各階段——由 C&Q Plan 決定。

7.3.2.1

Pre-Delivery Inspections (PDIs)

Construction checks at the vendor site before delivery — value and scope

Original Text (English)

PDIs are construction checks (inspection and testing) of systems or major system components before delivery to the owner site. These are typically done to verify construction progress and quality standards and to ensure delivery as scheduled. PDIs include inspection of parts (e.g., baffles in a heating jacket) that would not be able to be inspected during FAT or where a FAT cannot be performed for the system. This allows for remedy of any failings and avoids the delays to schedule (and associated costs) that would result from discovering problems later on-site.

中文解說 Commentary

🔍 PDI（交貨前檢查）：為什麼要去廠商工廠？

PDI 的核心邏輯是：「在問題最容易解決的地方發現問題」。

在廠商廠房發現缺陷：

  • 修復成本低（廠商設備、工具、人員齊全）
  • 不影響現場施工進度
  • 可以檢查「交貨後就看不到」的隱藏部件（如加熱夾套內的擋板）

等設備到現場才發現問題：

  • 可能需要拆機返廠（高成本）
  • 佔用現場空間與進度
  • 可能拖延整個廠房啟動計劃

💡 比喻：PDI 像汽車出廠前的「出廠檢驗」

就像汽車在離開組裝線前進行全車品質檢驗，PDI 讓業主有機會在「設備出廠前」確認品質。差別在於：製藥設備往往是定製品，廠商不會庫存同型號備品，一旦出廠後發現問題，修復時間和成本都遠高於汽車行業。

⚠️ PDI vs FAT 的區別

面向PDIFAT
時機設備建造中（進度確認）設備完成後（功能驗收）
焦點施工進度、品質標準、隱藏部件功能運作、設計要求達成
正式性較非正式，工程性質正式，依協議/測試計劃執行
可替代現場測試部分可以（如材料符合性）部分可以（需適當核准）

🤔 思考題：PDI 的價值何時最高？

以下哪種情況最值得安排 PDI？

  1. 採購一台現成的蠕動泵（off-the-shelf peristaltic pump）
  2. 訂製一套 10,000L WFI 蒸餾水機（multi-column still，需定製設計）
  3. 採購標準 316L 不鏽鋼管件和閥門

答案：情況 2 最值得安排 PDI。定製複雜設備的製造偏差風險高，且交貨後發現問題的修復成本極高。標準現成品（情況 1、3）風險相對低，PDI 的邊際效益較小。

本節摘要 Section Summary (Chapter 7, Part 1: pp. 49–56)

  • C&Q 測試定義：從設計到系統驗收的完整測試過程，涵蓋靜態測試（文件審查）與動態測試（實際運作），並以整合系統的方式進行（機械+電氣+自動化）。
  • 七大測試原則：工程驅動、預定義文件標準、培訓、見證要求預定義、廠商評估、變更管理、偏差管理程序預定義。
  • Table 7.1 & 7.2：提供不同系統類型（高壓滅菌器、HVAC、凍乾機、秤量器、WFI）所需測試/檢查文件組合的參考選項——靈活選擇，重要的是在 C&Q Plan 中預先定義。
  • QU 監督四種模式：程序預核、C&Q Plan 批准+摘要報告審核、IOQ 協議前後審批、標記法整合工程記錄——依系統風險與組織能力靈活選用。
  • C&Q 團隊四角色：測試協調員（進度管理）、生產使用者（系統所有人）、技術專家（SME 支援）、品保代表（CDE 確認監督）。
  • 測試前提條件：計劃先行（PDI/FAT 策略）、培訓完成、DR/DQ 批准、廠商文件策略確認、SRA 和變更記錄審查——五項缺一不可。
  • TOP 移交文件包：系統生命週期基礎文件，13 類典型內容應在合約下訂前確認；Loop Calibration 文件是 CDE 驗證的重要支持。
  • PDI（交貨前檢查）：在廠商廠房提前發現問題，可避免現場啟動延誤和高額修復成本；尤其對定製複雜設備（如 WFI 系統）效益最高。
