Chapter 12: Change Management — 變更管理

12.1 Introduction — 導論 | Pages 89–90

📖 Original Text (English)

12.1 Introduction

Change management processes should be established and applied throughout the lifecycle of manufacturing systems. The risk-based application of SME-led change management is one of the biggest challenges in the implementation of QRM-based C&Q as it applies the principles of ICH Q9. This Guide presents an approach which involves two modes of change management:

  • Engineering Change Management (ECM)
  • Quality Change Control (QCC)

Project change management that covers the elements of project scope, cost, and schedule is outside the scope of this Guide.

A system is considered to be changed when it is modified, altered, added to, removed, or improved in a way that makes its functions, physical features, or performance different from what they were prior to the change.

Replacing an existing part of a system with an identical one (like-for-like) may not be considered as a change. Organizations should define and follow a robust assessment process for classifying changes as like-for-like.

12.1.1 Purpose and Benefits

Change management is a documented program that:

  • Defines what is subject to change
  • Determines the risk for product impact caused by the change
  • Establishes a process for initiation, review, and approval of the request for change
  • Defines when the Quality Unit should be involved
  • Establishes a process for evaluation of the actual impact of the change

Change management is needed for the following reasons:

  • Ensures control of the impact on the current state of the system
  • Provides a basis for peer (SME) review and approval
  • Is a regulatory requirement (e.g., 21 CFR 211.100 and EU GMP Volume 4 §5.23)
  • Is a good business practice

Change management processes should not be (or perceived to be) an obstruction to fostering innovation and continual improvement. Efficient use of change management adds value by delivering technically sound solutions in an efficient manner.

12.1.2 Principles/Concepts

Figure 12.1 illustrates the differences between the two basic types of change management processes in this chapter, ECM and QCC. Table 12.1 outlines their differences in more detail.

Engineering Change Management (ECM) Quality Change Control (QCC)
Managed by Engineering or Operations unit Managed by Quality Assurance (QA)
Changes to CAs/CDEs require Quality Unit approval Changes require pre-approval by Quality Unit prior to initiation
Approvals performed by appropriate SMEs and system owners Impact on system's qualified/validated status must be evaluated and documented
Applicable during projects prior to acceptance and release Applicable following Quality Unit acceptance and release and during subsequent lifecycle management
May also be applied during lifecycle management for non-critical aspects (per System Risk Assessment) Requalification needs QA approval; post-change verification documentation required

Table 12.1: Comparison of Change Management Processes

💬 中文解說 Commentary

🔧 核心概念：兩種變更管理模式

ISPE Vol.5 將變更管理分為兩種截然不同的機制，對應C&Q生命週期的不同階段：

  • ECM（工程變更管理）：適用於系統尚未被QA接受與放行之前，由工程或運營單位主導，重點在於控制設計與施工過程中的技術變更。
  • QCC（品質變更管制）：適用於系統已完成資格確認並正式投入生產之後，由QA主導，任何變更均需事前取得QA預先核准。

🏗 生活比喻：蓋房子 vs. 住房子之後

想像蓋一棟房子：

  • 施工階段（ECM）：牆壁位置、管線走向可以由工程師決定修改，只要記錄在施工圖並通知相關人員即可。
  • 入住後（QCC）：要拆牆或改電線，必須先向管理委員會（=QA）提出申請，獲准後才能動工，完工後還要驗收。

C&Q 中的「入住」時刻就是 QA 接受與放行（Acceptance and Release）。

⚠ 實務要點：Like-for-Like 的判定

同類替換（like-for-like）可能不構成「變更」，但這不是免費通行證。組織必須建立明確的評估程序，包含：

  • 零件型號、規格、製造商是否完全相同
  • 性能特性（如流量、壓力）是否無任何差異
  • 若有任何不同，即使微小，也應視為變更啟動評估

FDA 查廠常見缺失之一：企業聲稱 like-for-like，但缺乏書面評估記錄。

🏭 CDMO 實務應用

在 CDMO 環境中，ECM 與 QCC 的界線格外重要：

  • 新廠設施建造期間：使用 ECM，由工程部門主導，CDE 相關變更須通知QA
  • PQ 執行前後：即使系統還在試運行，一旦QA已正式放行，任何設計修改就必須走 QCC
  • 客戶導入新產品期間：若需修改現有已確認設備的參數或硬體，均屬 QCC 範疇
12

12.2 Engineering Change Management (ECM) — 工程變更管理

Pages 91–92

📖 Original Text (English)

ECM is a key component of the Engineering Quality Process. It provides the primary control mechanism and is fundamental in supporting the execution of regulatory/quality change control for CQAs. Appropriate SMEs, process owners, and the Quality Unit (where CAs/CDEs are impacted) should be involved in the evaluation, review, and approval.

There are three primary areas of application for ECM:

  • Provide lifecycle management for systems supporting both GMP and non-GMP regulated processes during operation
  • Provide the primary change management mechanism during a project phase including work intended to support C&Q (e.g., during DR/DQ, fabrication, FAT/SAT, and verification)
  • Manage and document technical changes for non-critical aspects of qualified systems

The review and approval method for the ECM system should enable effective and rapid change management that is sufficiently flexible to adapt to:

  • The stage of the project and related regulatory impact
  • The impact on manufacturing, maintenance, and system lifecycle

The level of documentation of the change should be commensurate with the level of risk related to the change.

12.2.1 Scope and Sequence of ECM

International GMPs require that changes that have the potential to impact product quality and patient safety be handled within the PQS (Pharmaceutical Quality System). This drives the need to establish a defined endpoint for application of ECM to GMP and non-GMP changes within the project lifecycle; from this point forward, full application of QCC to CAs/CDEs commences.

From a regulatory perspective, it is only after the acceptance and release of a system (for execution of PQ/Process Validation, if applicable, or for manufacturing for commercial use) that changes to systems with CAs/CDEs should go through QA-managed QCC.

During the operational phase of a system, ECM should continue to be applied to non-critical aspects of the system. Each change should be evaluated on whether CAs/CDEs are affected.

12.2.2 Application of ECM

Table 12.2 provides examples of types of changes and the suggested change management mechanism for each type. These examples are for illustrative purposes; actual application should be based on organization procedures.

Change Description ECM (No QA) ECM + QA Approval QCC
New system impacting only non-GMP regulations ✓
Changes to GMP-supporting system without CAs/CDEs ✓
Changes during C&Q that do NOT impact CAs/CDEs ✓
Changes during C&Q that DO impact CAs/CDEs ✓
Changes to any document previously approved by QA ✓
Acceptance and release for systems with CAs/CDEs ✓
Changes after acceptance and release to qualified system with CAs/CDEs ✓
Post-release changes to non-critical aspects (if justified by risk assessment) ✓
Key Note: The difference between QCC and ECM with QA Approval:
  • QCC requires Quality Unit pre-approval of a change
  • ECM with QA approval only requires QA approval for ECM-managed changes prior to acceptance and release or after approval of the project activity
💬 中文解說 Commentary

🧩 名詞解釋：ECM 的三大應用領域

ECM 並非只存在於建造期間，它在三個情境下均發揮作用：

  1. GMP 與非GMP系統運營期間的生命週期管理：廠房設備的長期維護更改
  2. C&Q 專案期間的主要變更機制：從 DR/DQ 到 FAT/SAT 都適用
  3. 已確認系統非關鍵面向的技術變更：例如更換非 CDE 的零件

📊 風險相稱原則

「文件程度應與變更風險相稱」是 ISPE 的一貫哲學。

低風險變更（非GMP管道）：簡單的工程記錄即可

中風險變更（GMP但非CDE）：需完整ECM記錄，通知相關SME

高風險變更（涉及CDE/CA）：ECM + QA核准，或直接走QCC

這與 ICH Q9 的風險管理原則一致——不應對所有變更一律採用最繁瑣的程序。

⚠ 常見混淆：ECM + QA核准 vs. QCC

許多實務人員容易混淆這兩種模式：

  • ECM + QA核准：適用於 放行前，QA 在工程框架內核准變更，不需要「預先批准」的正式變更單
  • QCC：適用於 放行後，正式品質管理系統（PQS）內的變更控制，必須在實施前取得QA預先批准

核心區別在於：時間點（放行前/後）和誰主導（工程/QA）。

🏭 CDMO 決策樹：ECM vs. QCC

遇到變更請求時，CDMO 工程師可依此判斷：

  1. 系統已被QA正式放行了嗎？→ 是 → 走 QCC
  2. 變更影響到 CA 或 CDE 嗎？→ 是 → 需QA核准（ECM或QCC視放行狀態而定）
  3. 變更只涉及非關鍵面向，且有System Risk Assessment支持嗎？→ 是 → ECM 即可，不需QA
  4. 以上皆否 → 與QA共同評估
12

12.3 Change Management during C&Q Projects — C&Q 期間的變更管理

Pages 92–93

📖 Original Text (English)

Before new systems are used for commercial or clinical operations, there is no risk to the patient associated with changes to design or function during the C&Q or project lifecycle. There is therefore no regulatory requirement for Quality Unit approval prior to implementation of a change.

There is, however, potential risk to the successful delivery of product and process user requirements and the risk control strategies determined as part of the approved System Risk Assessment. The Quality Unit should approve, prior to verification testing, any changes to the design or intended function or acceptance criteria associated with CAs/CDEs (including any new CAs/CDEs driven by changes in design).

In addition to maintaining the intended design after DR/DQ, ECM also plays a role in ensuring the integrity of data and evidence generated during C&Q. Fixes and repairs during C&Q have the potential to affect and invalidate testing and other evidence previously generated and compiled against the original configuration.

Test results from commissioning that do not meet acceptance criteria require:

  • Documented description of the incident
  • Description of corrective action(s) taken
  • Retest or re-verification of results following the correction
  • Assessment of the impact of the corrective action on any test results or other evidence already collected, and determination of any associated retesting requirements

A note should be made in the C&Q record and action taken to correct the item to meet the acceptance criteria. If the acceptance criteria cannot be met after corrective actions have been made, an SME should evaluate the issue and determine if it can be accepted as-is. A note should be made in the commissioning record to indicate why the item is acceptable as-is.

For more information on handling of discrepancies, refer to Section 7.4.

💬 中文解說 Commentary

🚦 重要原則：放行前不需QA預先核准

ISPE 明確指出：在系統尚未用於商業或臨床生產之前，設計或功能的改變 不會對病患造成直接風險，因此法規上並不要求 QA 在變更實施前預先核准。

這個原則打破了許多人的直覺。但這不代表可以隨意更改——ECM 仍然要求記錄所有變更，且涉及 CDE 的變更必須在驗證測試前取得 QA 核准。

⚠ 數據完整性警示：修正後的重測義務

C&Q 期間的修復工作（fix & repair）可能使已完成的測試數據失效。例如：

  • 儀器校正偏差被修正後，之前的測量結果需重新評估
  • 管線重新焊接後，之前的壓力測試可能需重做
  • 軟體邏輯修改後，相關的 IQ/OQ 測試步驟需重新確認

因此，ECM 記錄中必須包含「此次修正對現有測試數據的影響評估」，這是常被忽略的環節。

🔧 「As-Is 接受」的正確做法

當問題無法修正時（如設計限制），「接受現狀（accept as-is）」是允許的，但必須：

  1. 由有資格的 SME 評估可接受性
  2. 在試車記錄中明確說明為何可接受
  3. 評估是否影響 CDE/CQA（若有，則需QA認可）

空白的接受理由或僅寫「OK」是不合規的記錄。

12

12.4 Change Management during Operation — 運營期間的變更管理

Page 93

📖 Original Text (English)

After acceptance and release and after the system is placed into production use, any changes to the qualified system has the potential to affect product quality and patient safety. GMP regulations usually require Quality Unit pre-approval (approval prior to non-emergency implementation) of changes with the potential to affect product quality. When using a risk-based approach, QA-managed QCC should be applied when the change impacts CAs/CDEs.

After acceptance and release, there are scenarios that allow for application of ECM without Quality Unit involvement. Organizations should establish procedures that state the specific requirements for use of ECM within the organization or facility. Routine operations that may allow for application of ECM without Quality Unit involvement include, for example:

  • Changes to non-GMP aspects of systems
  • Changes to non-critical aspects of systems (as established by the System Risk Assessment)
  • Certain categories of changes, such as like-for-like, as documented in the completed verification and approved acceptance and release documentation

When QCC is used to manage changes, a log or tracking system should be used to maintain change histories for systems with CAs/CDEs. IT tools providing this functionality may be commercially available. A complete record of all changes to qualified systems should be able to be retrieved on demand.

💬 中文解說 Commentary

🏭 運營期間的變更管理框架

系統正式投入生產後，變更管理進入最嚴格的階段：

  • 影響 CDE/CA 的變更：必須走 QCC，QA 必須在實施前預先核准
  • 非關鍵面向的變更：可繼續使用 ECM，但需有 System Risk Assessment 支持
  • 緊急情況：GMP 通常允許緊急實施，但事後必須補正式核准程序

⚠ 法規要求：21 CFR 211.100 & EU GMP §5.23

美國 FDA（21 CFR 211.100）和歐盟 GMP（Volume 4, §5.23）均明確要求：

  • 書面程序（SOP）必須由有資格人員審核和核准
  • 任何偏離已核准程序的行為必須調查
  • 變更控制必須評估對已確認狀態的影響

這是為何 QCC 在放行後成為強制要求的法規基礎。

💻 變更追蹤系統的要求

QCC 要求維護完整的變更歷史，現代製藥企業通常使用以下工具：

  • 電子化變更控制系統（如 Veeva Vault QualityDocs、MasterControl）
  • 系統應能提供隨時調閱（on demand）的完整變更記錄
  • 稽核追蹤（audit trail）功能確保每筆變更均有時間戳記和核准人員記錄

FDA 查廠時，審查員可能要求即時調閱特定設備的完整變更歷史，因此系統的查詢功能至關重要。

12

12.5 Engineering Change Management Process — ECM 流程詳述

Pages 94–95

📖 Original Text (English)

ECM is defined as a process by which qualified representative(s) reviews proposed changes for its impact, approves or denies the requests, and manages and tracks their implementation. ECM is a good engineering practice to effectively manage project execution.

An ECM process may contain the following attributes:

  • Recorded name of the originator and date
  • Description of the change, including the affected system or area and intended purpose
  • Assessment of the potential impact of the change on:
    • Quality requirements
    • Project schedule
    • Project budget (relative to the latest approved budget)
    • System scope, design, or performance requirements (including safety, operability, reliability, construction, commissioning, operations, and maintenance)
    • Other systems
    • Engineering documentation
    • Qualification documents (including system classification)
  • Notification of the proposed change to stakeholders
  • Record of the approval or denial of the proposed change
  • Tracking through completion

ECM Application by Project Phase:

Project Conceptual Phase: There needs to be a clear definition of which documents are controlled by QA and where QA is only involved on request. Key product and process knowledge documents (such as the URS, pilot scale process reports, System Risk Assessment, and VMP) provide the basis for basic design and the requirements for CQAs and CPPs. Changes to these key documents should be addressed using ECM with Quality Unit approval.

Design Phase: Change management should be applied in alignment with the principles of GEP, with approval by SMEs. The mechanics of proposing, approving, implementing, and tracking changes should be simple since the design phase is very fluid. At the completion of the design phase, DR/DQ is completed. At this point, ECM is applied to GEP changes, and ECM with Quality Unit approval is applied to changes in CAs/CDEs.

Construction, C&Q Phase: For large projects, the site and project are primarily under the control of a contract organization. Changes should be implemented using the contract organization's change management policy with input by the owner. During construction, many changes are driven by the reality of the installed environment versus the design intent. Typical changes include:

  • Field inspections and testing performance — Controlled by ECM; may require retesting post-change
  • Departures from specification:
    • Readily corrected (e.g., pipe labels): Correct, reinspect, and document
    • Corrected later (or impacting other inspections/tests): Use discrepancy/punch list or change management
    • Cannot correct: Needs evaluation by the technical reviewer
  • Deviations — Only occur during performance testing when a product/process user requirement is not met. Steps:
    • Documentation and evaluation by Quality and Manufacturing Units
    • Determination of an assignable cause
    • Corrective action: definition, approval, implementation, test, confirmation, and documentation

Correction of deviations should be addressed in the following preferred order:

  1. Design change
  2. Installation change
  3. Operational change

Non-correctable deviations may require an SOP or other procedural change (procedural control) to compensate for the shortcoming.

💬 中文解說 Commentary

📋 ECM 表單的必要元素

一份完整的 ECM 變更申請記錄應包含以下內容，這也是稽核員查閱時的核查清單：

  • 發起人姓名與日期（可歸責性 Attributability）
  • 變更描述：影響的系統、區域、目的
  • 多維度影響評估：品質、進度、預算、其他系統、文件
  • 利益相關者通知記錄
  • 核准/拒絕記錄
  • 完成追蹤：確認已按核准內容實施

📅 各階段ECM彈性度比較

專案階段變更頻率ECM 嚴格度
概念設計低中（關鍵文件需QA核准）
詳細設計高低（SME主導，快速）
施工/C&Q高中-高（視CDE是否受影響）
運營低高（QCC主導）

⚠ 偏差優先處理順序：設計 > 安裝 > 程序

ISPE 明確規定偏差改正的優先順序：

  1. 設計變更（最優先）：從根本解決問題，修改設計或規格
  2. 安裝變更：修改物理安裝方式，如管線位置、設備位置
  3. 操作程序變更（最後手段）：用 SOP 彌補設計/安裝的不足

這個優先順序反映了一個重要理念：依賴操作人員執行特殊程序來彌補硬體缺陷，比修改硬體本身風險更高。

🏭 CDMO 施工期間的 ECM 實例

典型的CDMO建廠 ECM 情境：

  • 管線路徑調整（非CDE）→ ECM，工程師核准，更新P&ID
  • WFI 分配管線設計壓力修改（可能涉及CDE）→ ECM + QA核准，更新URS
  • 無菌灌裝機 HEPA 過濾器規格由H13改H14（CDE）→ ECM + QA核准，評估對OQ的影響
  • 天花板石膏板牆面更換材質（非GMP）→ ECM，無需通知QA
13

Chapter 13: Good Documentation Practice for C&Q — C&Q 良好文件管理規範

13.1 Introduction & 13.1.1–13.1.2 | Pages 97–98

📖 Original Text (English)

13.1 Introduction

The goal of Good Documentation Practice (GDocP) is to create clear, concise documents that a knowledgeable peer may review without questions. Good Documentation Practice supports data integrity. Documents should be:

  • Attributable
  • Legible
  • Contemporaneous
  • Original
  • Accurate

These five attributes form the acronym ALCOA.

13.1.1 Scope and Purpose

This chapter applies to all C&Q documentation, including test documents and reports. In this chapter, GEP documents are considered to be the engineering records used to support commissioning, and GMP records are considered to be the documentation supporting qualification.

Aspect Commissioning (GEP) Qualification (GMP)
Testing approach Iterative testing and adjustment permitted; final results permanently recorded Protocols followed exactly; all events recorded as they occur; all deviations documented
Standards Engineering standard testing practices (ISO, NEBB); acceptance criteria in approved specifications Custom protocols with pre-approved acceptance criteria
Acceptability Engineering judgment used to verify spec and design for non-critical aspects Quality Unit reviews and approves acceptability; confirms CAs/CDEs
Documentation standard Generally accepted GDocP (Section 13.3.2) Organization/site-specific practices required for GMP records
Approval Typically not approved by Quality Unit; Engineering approves testing strategy Testing strategy and acceptance approved by Quality Unit

Table 13.1: Differences Between Commissioning vs. Qualification Testing and Documentation

13.1.2 Requirements for Vendor Documentation to Support Qualification

When the decision is made to use vendor documentation to support system qualification of CAs/CDEs, the justification should be documented and approved by SMEs and the Quality Unit. Considerations should include:

  • Vendor assessment
  • Acceptable vendor quality system
  • Vendor technical capability
  • Vendor application of GEP such that information obtained will be accurate and suitable for the purpose of qualification
💬 中文解說 Commentary

📑 ALCOA 原則詳解 — 數據完整性的基石

ALCOA 是全球製藥法規（FDA、EMA、WHO）要求的數據完整性核心框架：

  • A – Attributable（可歸責）：清楚記錄誰在何時執行了什麼操作。每筆記錄都必須有識別資訊（簽名/姓名縮寫 + 日期）。
  • L – Legible（清晰易讀）：記錄必須永久且清晰可讀。潦草、褪色、被遮蓋的記錄均不合規。
  • C – Contemporaneous（當時記錄）：在操作執行的當下立即記錄，不允許事後補記（backdating）。
  • O – Original（原始資料）：保留第一手記錄；若需謄抄，原始資料必須保留並標註。
  • A – Accurate（準確）：數據必須真實反映實際結果，不得捏造或篡改。

⚠ ALCOA+ 的延伸要求

現代法規（特別是 FDA 2018年數據完整性指南）在 ALCOA 基礎上加入四個「+」：

  • Complete（完整）：不得選擇性記錄；所有測試（包含不合格）都必須記錄
  • Consistent（一致）：記錄方式應跨人員、跨時間保持一致
  • Enduring（永久性）：記錄必須以不易損壞的方式保存（如不用鉛筆、可擦鋼筆）
  • Available（可取得）：稽核時可即時提供給主管機關審閱

🧪 GEP vs. GMP 文件的關鍵差異

一個容易理解的比較：

  • GEP（試車文件）：像工程師的工作筆記——可以反覆試驗，記錄最終結果；工程判斷足夠
  • GMP（確認文件）：像法庭證據——必須按計畫執行，逐步記錄，任何偏差都要記錄和說明

這個區別決定了試車報告能否被當作確認文件使用——必須達到 GMP 文件標準才行。

🏭 廠商文件用於確認的風險

許多 CDMO 希望使用設備廠商的 FAT/SAT 文件替代自己的 IQ/OQ，ISPE 允許此做法，但前提是：

  • 廠商已通過評估（Vendor Qualification/Audit）
  • 廠商的 QMS 達到可接受標準
  • 廠商文件已按 GDocP 要求執行
  • 使用理由已由 SME 和 QA 書面核准

若廠商文件品質不足，引用它可能使整個確認包的可信度受損。

13

13.2 C&Q Document Development Basics — 文件開發基礎

Pages 98–99

📖 Original Text (English)

Testing and verification documentation are usually written in the local language. Summary documents are generally in English to facilitate regulatory review.

The use of forms/templates is encouraged to promote consistency. Forms/templates can be approved once when created and then utilized multiple times without pre-approval if the relevant content is not changed. Where this approach is used, there should be a procedure to ensure that the form/template used for data entry is current at the time of use.

When forms/templates are used, the SME should review the form to ensure that it includes all of the required testing for the system being verified; if additional tests are required, the form/template should be supplemented with additional testing.

Test scripts may be approved individually and assembled into a test plan/report. If test data sheets are used to supplement test scripts, they should be approved in accordance with the requirements defined in the test plan.

The test procedures should be clear and unambiguous such that the results are repeatable and reproducible:

  • Repeatable: The same result would be achieved if the same procedure is repeated by the same trained and qualified personnel.
  • Reproducible: The same result would be achieved by different trained and qualified personnel following the same procedure.

The test document should indicate the order that the cases are to be executed. Acceptance criteria needs to be established and it should be clear that the tests demonstrate that the acceptance criteria have been met.

💬 中文解說 Commentary

📝 範本（Template）管理的最佳實踐

使用已核准的標準範本執行測試，是提升效率的聰明做法。關鍵要求：

  • 範本核准一次，多次使用，無需每次重新核准
  • 但必須確認使用時範本為最新版本（即文件管控有效）
  • SME 必須確認範本涵蓋該特定系統的所有必要測試——若不足，必須增補

🔄 可重複性 vs. 可再現性

這兩個概念源自量測系統分析（MSA）：

  • Repeatability（可重複性）：同一人、同一設備、同一條件，重複執行得到相同結果。測試的「自身一致性」。
  • Reproducibility（可再現性）：不同人、不同地點、不同設備，執行相同程序得到相同結果。測試的「跨人員一致性」。

若測試程序寫得模糊，不同人執行可能得到不同結果，確認的可信度就會下降。

⚠ 語言選擇與法規審查

執行文件可以用本地語言（如中文、日文）撰寫，但總結報告建議以英文撰寫，原因是：

  • FDA/EMA 查廠時審查員通常只能閱讀英文
  • 英文摘要讓跨國監管機構無需翻譯即可評估
  • CDMO 為多國客戶服務時，英文摘要減少溝通障礙
13

13.3 Document Execution — 文件執行規範

13.3.1 Test Execution Basics & 13.3.2 Good Test Execution Documentation | Pages 99–102

📖 Original Text (English)

13.3.1 Test Execution Basics

13.3.1.1 Executor Qualification and Signature Log

Individuals who enter information in a test document (i.e., executors) must possess the education, training, experience, or any combination thereof to perform their work and record their printed name, signature, and initials in a signature log. An executor cannot review or approve his/her own work.

13.3.1.2 Contemporaneous Records

Documents should be completed as work is performed. Results should be recorded at the time of activity. Backdating is not permitted.

The steps within a test case should be executed in order unless specified otherwise. Provide an explanation for any step or task performed out of sequence.

If a test script takes more than one calendar day to execute, indicate where testing stopped and initial and date this entry at the appropriate test step.

13.3.1.3 Transcribed Data

It is permissible to transcribe data from one form to another (e.g., printed tabular summary of manual entries or manually transcribing single entries from computer generated printouts). Transcribed data should be signed and dated. The date of the actual data should be included. Transcribed data should be checked by a second person. If data is transcribed, the raw data should be included — labeled, initialed and dated.

13.3.1.4 Printouts

Test steps should indicate when printouts are to be used. Printouts should be attached to the test plan/report appendix or contained in the appropriate reference file.

Where the output is from a thermal printer (e.g., for a particle counter), a photocopy should be used, signed and dated as a true copy by the individual responsible for the test. A footnote should be annotated in the test document to reference the location of the original.

13.3.1.5 Supporting Documentation

Attach or reference supporting documentation as necessary. Original data sheets and checklists should be available for review until the transcribed document has been accepted and approved. Refer to organization requirements or relevant regional regulations regarding any specific documentation requirements prior to destroying supporting documentation for GMP records/documents.

13.3.1.6 Proper Handling of Documents

It is understood and accepted that testing documents will experience some wear and tear typical of field executed documentation. However, care should be taken to protect documents from spills, excessive folding, or other physical damage.

13.3.1.7 Document Changes

Changes to approved documents require approval by representatives of the original approving groups.

13.3.2 Good Test Execution Documentation

The typical requirements for recording a GEP document should include:

  • Use permanent, non-fading, non-smearing ink.
    • Blue or black ink is preferred.
    • If colors are used for redline drawings, the definition of color meaning must be clear.
    • GEP field documentation recorded in pencil: a photocopy should be used, signed and dated as a true copy.
  • Ditto marks (") or arrows (↓) to indicate duplicate entries are not permitted.
  • Writing over an existing entry is not permitted (see Section 13.5 for corrections).
  • No scribbling on the record. When adding notes, use unique alpha/numeric identifiers to trace each entry to the corresponding footnote.
  • If a signature log is maintained, initials are acceptable in lieu of signatures everywhere except for document approvals.
  • Initial and date any handwritten changes or comments. If the reason for the change is not clear, provide an explanatory note.
  • Initial and date each page with an entry at least once.
  • Date format needs to be unambiguous. DD-MMM-YYYY is preferred (e.g., 30-MAY-2019).
  • Time format: use 24-hour clock (e.g., 1425) or am/pm (e.g., 2:25 pm).
  • For significant figures:
    • Use a zero before a decimal point if there is no other digit.
    • Record all figures as shown on the measuring instrument or readout.
    • Ensure calculations indicate the correct unit of measure and use the correct number of significant digits.
    • For final reported data, round to the number of places that agrees with the stated specification or limit.
  • For quantitative results, record the number. Examples of unacceptable entries:
    • "Pass", "Fail", "As Expected", "Same", "OK", "Yes", Checkmark "✓"
  • Record the observed system response from the test step execution in the results column. Use unambiguous terminology; it is not necessary to record verbatim the expected results.
  • Line out, initial, and date all blank spaces. Be careful to distinguish "N/A" (Not Applicable) and "N/AV" (Not Available). "N/A" should only be used prior to approval to execute.
  • Where entire sections, columns, rows, or whole pages are not utilized, cross out with a single diagonal line; initial and date.
  • Data superseded by a subsequent test or inspection may be deleted. The final record should be annotated to indicate if a repair, engineering change, or correction has been made.
  • Test reports should include a summary of the results including a conclusion that the system is or is not suitable for the intended purpose.
  • The completed record should be able to be copied/scanned legibly.
💬 中文解說 Commentary

👥 執行者資格與簽名記錄

執行者（Executor）必須具備相應的教育背景、培訓和經驗。關鍵要求：

  • 每位執行者必須在簽名記錄表（Signature Log）中登記：印刷全名、正式簽名、縮寫（Initials）
  • 自我審核原則：任何人不得審核或核准自己的工作——這是 GDocP 的基本原則，也是利益衝突的防範機制

⏰ 當時記錄原則 — FDA 最常引用的缺失

「事後補記」（backdating）是 FDA 483 觀察和 Warning Letter 中最常見的 GDocP 缺失之一。

合規要求：測試步驟執行時立即記錄，不論是好是壞的結果。

常見違規情境：

  • 測試當天忘記記錄，隔天才填寫
  • 先記錄在便利貼，之後再謄抄到正式文件
  • 批次記錄在一天結束時集中填寫，而非操作當下填寫

電子記錄系統的稽核追蹤（Audit Trail）可以顯示記錄時間，使事後補記容易被發現。

📄 謄抄數據（Transcribed Data）的要求

當數據需要從原始記錄謄抄到另一份文件時：

  1. 謄抄者必須簽名並標注日期
  2. 包含原始數據的採集日期（不是謄抄日期）
  3. 必須由第二人核查謄抄準確性
  4. 原始數據必須保留，標記清楚並附上姓名縮寫和日期

🖨 熱感紙打印件的特殊處理

粒子計數器、天平等儀器常使用熱感紙（thermal paper），熱感紙容易褪色，違反「Legible」和「Enduring」原則。

正確做法：立即複印（photocopy），複印件由執行人員簽名並標注「True Copy」和日期，原件注明存放位置。

✏ 13.3.2 書面記錄的核心要求匯總

墨水要求：永久性、不褪色、不暈開；建議藍色或黑色；禁用鉛筆（除非立即複印存檔）

日期格式：DD-MMM-YYYY（如 30-MAY-2019）最佳，避免歧義（01/02/03 可能是1月2日或2月1日）

數量結果禁止寫：Pass / Fail / OK / Yes / ✓ — 必須記錄實際測量數值

空白格處理：必須劃線並簽名縮寫+日期，或標注 N/A，不得留空

文件標識：每頁至少簽名縮寫+日期一次

📈 N/A vs. N/AV 的區別

這個細節常被忽略但很重要：

  • N/A（Not Applicable，不適用）：只能在文件核准執行之前標注，表示這個測試項目根本不適用於該系統。一旦文件已核准開始執行，事後再標 N/A 通常需要解釋說明。
  • N/AV（Not Available，無法取得）：表示在執行時該項目無法評估，通常需要偏差記錄和說明。

🏭 CDMO GDocP 訓練重點

CDMO 在操作員 GDocP 培訓中最應強調的行為準則：

  • 「執行即記錄」文化——不接受「先做後記」
  • 記錄實際觀察值，不得記錄「意見」（Pass/OK）
  • 空白必須處理（N/A + 縮寫 + 日期）
  • 任何修改要可追溯（見13.5節）
  • 不得使用修正液（Whiteout）
13

13.4 Attachments and Supporting Documentation — 附件與佐證文件

Page 102

📖 Original Text (English)

The integrity of all original records should be maintained.

Printouts should indicate data dates. Data dates should coincide with test step execution. It is acceptable for printout dates to be later.

All screen printouts and printed reports should include the following labeling information:

  • Protocol number
  • Unique attachment number
  • Test script ID
  • Step number
  • Tester's initials
  • Date
  • Pagination: Page X of Y, where X represents the page number and Y represents the number of pages in the attachment

Every page should include Page X of Y pagination. If records are paginated as described and have a unique identifier, it is acceptable to initial and date only the first and last pages. Multiple attachments should have a summary cover sheet.

Use of sticky notes or other unofficial media for recording original data or information should not be permitted.

💬 中文解說 Commentary

📎 附件標識的完整要求

每份附件（printout、報告、截圖）必須標注7個資訊才算合規：

  1. 方案/協議號（Protocol No.）
  2. 唯一附件編號（Attachment No.）
  3. 測試腳本 ID
  4. 步驟編號
  5. 測試員縮寫
  6. 日期
  7. 頁碼格式：第 X 頁，共 Y 頁

「第X頁，共Y頁」的設計確保任何頁面的缺失都能立即被發現。

📌 便利貼的禁令

便利貼（sticky notes / Post-it）絕對禁止用於記錄原始數據，原因：

  • 容易脫落遺失，導致數據無法追溯
  • 無法確保「Enduring（永久性）」
  • 無編號頁碼，無法確認完整性

FDA 查廠中，在批次記錄或確認文件中發現便利貼記錄，是典型的 GDocP 觀察缺失。

📅 數據日期 vs. 打印日期

一個常見疑問：「儀器打印日期可以晚於測試執行日期嗎？」

答案：可以。ISPE 明確允許打印日期晚於數據日期（例如測試是週三做的，週四才打印出來）。

重要的是：打印件上的數據日期必須與測試步驟執行時間一致——這才是當時記錄的體現。

13

13.5 Corrections — 文件更正規範

Pages 102–103

📖 Original Text (English)

Mistakes and errors happen. Do not erase, overwrite, or corrupt original recorded data. Correction fluid, correction tape, pencil, and erasable ink should be avoided. Data should not be altered, obliterated, erased, or overwritten.

Corrections are acceptable when:

  • Correcting test procedures or instructions that do not change the intent of the step
  • Correcting typographical errors
  • Correcting test/sampling instructions
  • Correcting test data with no impact on interpretation

Corrections can be handled in the following manner:

  • Mark a single line through the error
    • The cross-out should permit the original information to be read
    • Always cross out the full number/word rather than an individual digit/letter
  • Record the correct information near the error and initial and date when the correction was made
  • If the reason for the change is not obvious, add a unique alpha/numeric identifier to reference the change, and record the justification on the same page using the reference alpha/numeric identifier

Situations may arise where the person needed for making a correction is no longer available. Any corrections made by a different person than the one making the initial entry needs to be compliant with the document/protocol and/or site procedures.

💬 中文解說 Commentary

✊ GDocP 更正的黃金法則 — 單線劃除

這是 GDocP 中最基本也最常被違反的規定：

23.5 24.2 [縮寫] [日期]

正確步驟：

  1. 用單一橫線劃過錯誤內容（原始數據仍可辨識）
  2. 在旁邊寫上正確值
  3. 簽上縮寫（Initials）和更正日期
  4. 若原因不明顯，加上唯一參照碼並在同頁附上說明

絕對禁止：修正液（Whiteout）、修正帶、覆蓋書寫、橡皮擦

🤔 為什麼原始數據必須可見？

「原始數據仍可辨識」這個要求背後是法規邏輯：

  • 若看不到原始數據，無法判斷更正是否合理
  • 若錯誤被完全遮蓋，看起來像資料造假
  • 稽核員需要能追蹤「原始紀錄 → 更正原因 → 最終值」的完整鏈條

使用修正液讓原始數據不可見，即使更正值是正確的，也可能被認定為違反數據完整性。

🏭 CDMO 實際情境：他人代為更正

當原始記錄者已離職或無法聯繫時，需要他人代為更正，必須：

  • 確認此情況符合公司/場地 SOP 的規定
  • 更正者必須說明為何由本人代為更正
  • 記錄更正者的縮寫和日期（而非原始記錄者）
  • 通常需要額外的說明文件或偏差記錄支持

這種情況在長期 C&Q 專案中並不少見，特別是使用臨時工程人員或承包商的情況下。

📝 練習思考：以下哪些更正方式合規？

  • 用白色修正液蓋住錯誤，然後在上面寫正確值 → 不合規（原始數據無法辨識）
  • 用雙線劃過錯誤的完整數字，旁邊寫正確值並簽名縮寫和日期 → 合規
  • 只劃掉錯誤數字中的一個位數，保留其他位數 → 不合規（應劃掉完整數值）
  • 劃掉錯誤值後添加更正值，但沒有日期 → 不合規（缺少日期，違反 Attributable）
  • 原因不明顯的更正，添加腳注說明更正理由 → 合規
13

13.6 Document Review and Approval — 文件審核與核准

Page 103

📖 Original Text (English)

Approvers should have the education, training, experience, or any combination thereof to review and/or approve the record. Quality review of commissioning documents can be limited to the product impact relevant tests by executing pre-approved test scripts or by assembling specific test scripts into a separate test plan.

Reviewers and approvers should ensure that:

  • All appendices and registers have been filled out in accordance with the applicable procedures
  • The document is complete, legible, and unambiguous
  • All test results conform to established acceptance criteria
  • All discrepancies should be closed and approvals for discrepancy closure should have been obtained
💬 中文解說 Commentary

✅ 審核者/核准者的職責

批准文件不只是「蓋章」，審核者必須確認四大事項：

  1. 完整性：所有附件、記錄表都已正確填寫
  2. 可讀性：文件清晰易讀，沒有模糊不清的部分
  3. 合格性：所有測試結果均符合預先設定的接受標準
  4. 偏差已關閉：所有偏差記錄均已經過調查、採取行動並獲核准關閉

⚠ 偏差未關閉即核准文件的後果

若核准者在未完全解決所有偏差的情況下核准文件，可能導致：

  • 確認包（Validation Package）被認定為不完整
  • 法規查廠時被列為重大觀察項目
  • 需要重新執行確認活動
  • 產品上市延遲

核准者的簽名代表對整份文件品質的背書——這是重大責任。

🏭 CDMO 試車文件的 QA 審核範圍

ISPE 允許QA對試車文件的審核範圍限縮到「與產品影響相關的測試」，即：

  • 涉及 CDE 的測試項目 → QA 必須審核
  • 純工程性能測試（如管道承壓、電氣接地）→ QA 可選擇性審核

這個彈性設計讓 CDMO 的 QA 部門可以將稽核資源集中在真正有品質影響的項目上，提高效率。

13

13.7–13.8 Storage, Retrieval, Retention & Disaster Recovery — 文件儲存與災難復原

Pages 103–104

📖 Original Text (English)

13.7 Storage, Retrieval, and Retention of Documents

Methods of document storage should be established, as dictated by organization/site policies and procedures and in a manner that allows documents to be located and retrieved within a reasonable time period, as required. The methods should include access control and tracking. The storage area should be secure.

Copies and original documents should be labeled as such. Executed documents can be scanned after final approval and archived as electronic records in a validated document management system. Once archiving is completed, the hard copy can be destroyed. Retention of records should follow organization/site specific records management policy. Check the specific requirements of authorities for the regions that the site will supply before destroying GMP records/documents.

13.8 Disaster Recovery

There should be a system in place to handle the reconstruction of records. All measures should be taken to recover the original document. For a record that is lost or destroyed and not recoverable, a copy of the original record is acceptable as the official copy, which should be approved by Management.

Note: Storage and management of documents during the execution of a project should be defined to minimize risk of loss and/or damage.
💬 中文解說 Commentary

📂 文件儲存的三大要求

  1. 可及時取得：法規要求能在合理時間內找到並提供文件——查廠時通常是「立即」或「數小時內」
  2. 存取控制：文件室（或電子系統）必須有存取管理，防止未授權存取或修改
  3. 安全存放：防潮、防火、防損毀的儲存環境

⚠ 電子化歸檔的法規要求

將紙本文件掃描後以電子檔歸檔是允許的，但必須滿足：

  • 電子文件管理系統（EDMS）必須是已確認的（validated）系統
  • 掃描後可以銷毀紙本，但需有書面程序規範此流程
  • 適用法規的特定保存期限必須查明並遵守（各國法規不同）
  • 美國 FDA：GMP 記錄通常需保存至少2年（藥品有效期後），或更長
  • 歐盟 EMA / PICS：類似要求，但具體依產品類型而定

📦 21 CFR Part 11 與電子記錄

若使用電子系統儲存和管理確認文件，美國法規 21 CFR Part 11（電子記錄與電子簽名）即適用，要求：

  • 稽核追蹤（Audit Trail）：自動記錄誰在何時建立、修改、刪除記錄
  • 電子簽名：必須與簽署人唯一連結，不可否認（non-repudiation）
  • 系統確認：EDMS 本身需要通過 GAMP 5 等框架進行 CSV（電腦系統確認）
  • 數據保護：防止未授權修改，電子記錄的完整性必須受到保護

歐盟對應法規為 EU Annex 11（電腦化系統）。

🚨 災難復原程序

文件損毀（如火災、水災、電腦崩潰）時的應對程序：

  1. 優先嘗試復原原始文件（如從備份系統、其他副本）
  2. 若無法復原，可接受原始文件的副本作為正式記錄
  3. 副本必須由管理層（Management）核准，確認其為有效替代
  4. 建立事件記錄，說明原始文件損失的原因和過程

預防勝於治療——C&Q 執行期間即應規劃文件儲存策略，最小化損失風險。

🏭 CDMO 文件保存的實務建議

  • 多重備份：重要文件（如確認包）建議保有：原件 + 數位掃描件（EDMS）+ 異地備份
  • 保存期限管理：建立文件銷毀排程，確保在監管保存期限結束前不得銷毀 GMP 記錄
  • 客戶交付物管理：CDMO 為客戶執行的確認工作，文件的所有權和保存責任需在合約中明確約定
  • 查廠準備：確保查廠時能在30分鐘內提供任意指定的歷史確認文件——這是衡量文件管理體系效率的實際指標

📋 本節重點摘要 Section Summary

Chapter 12：變更管理兩大支柱

  • ECM（工程變更管理）適用於系統放行前的C&Q及建造期間，由工程/運營主導，CDE相關變更須QA核准但不需預先批准；非關鍵面向在放行後亦可繼續使用ECM。
  • QCC（品質變更管制）適用於系統放行後的所有CDE/CA相關變更，由QA主導，所有變更必須在實施前取得QA預先核准；法規依據為21 CFR 211.100及EU GMP §5.23。
  • 偏差修正優先順序：設計變更 > 安裝變更 > 程序變更，依賴SOP彌補硬體缺陷是最後手段。

Chapter 13：GDocP 六大核心原則

  • ALCOA+（可歸責、清晰易讀、當時記錄、原始資料、準確 + 完整、一致、永久性、可取得）是文件管理的基石，直接對應 FDA 數據完整性要求。
  • 當時記錄（Contemporaneous）是最常被違反的原則之一；事後補記（backdating）是FDA 483最常引用的缺失。
  • 更正規範：單線劃除（原始數據仍可辨識）+ 正確值 + 縮寫 + 日期；絕對禁止修正液、塗改、覆蓋書寫。
  • 試車文件（GEP）可用於支持確認（GMP），前提是達到GMP文件標準（事先確認廠商文件品質）。
  • 電子記錄須符合21 CFR Part 11（美國）或EU Annex 11（歐盟），確認EDMS系統並維護稽核追蹤。
  • 文件儲存需確保隨時可取得；C&Q期間即應建立防損失計畫，並在災難發生時有復原程序。
14+App

Chapter 14+App: Implementation Strategies & Key Appendices

導入策略與重要附錄 | p105-p212

Pages 105+ | Section 9 of 9

本節學習目標 Learning Objectives

  1. 理解 ISPE 科學與風險基礎 C&Q 導入策略的六大準備步驟，以及「無需重複確效」原則對遺留系統的意義。
  2. 掌握針對新系統、既有系統（小改動）、既有系統（重大改動）三種情境的不同 C&Q 導入路徑與文件要求。
  3. 了解 ISPE C&Q 方法與主要法規（FDA 21 CFR、EU GMP Annex 15、ICH Q8/Q9/Q10）之間的對應關係，掌握法規基礎。
  4. 能夠規劃一個分階段的組織導入計畫，以促進高階管理層的支持與跨部門協作。
  5. 能將 ISPE 導入策略應用於 CDMO 情境，制定從傳統 V-Model 過渡至 ISPE 2nd Ed. 方法的實際步驟。

本節內容 Contents

14.1 Introduction 14.2 Preparing for Implementation 14.3 Approaches for Implementation 14.4 Table 14.1 — Implementation Matrix Appendix 1: Regulatory Basis Ch.14 Regulatory Basis Appendix Overview Table

章節摘要 Section Summary

第 14 章（策略導入）說明組織如何有效轉型至科學與風險基礎的 C&Q 流程。核心訊息是：採用本指引方法並不會使現有文件失效——確效文件代表系統在某一時間點的狀態，只要配合現有品質系統（變更管理、維護、校正、定期審查），現有文件仍可繼續使用。

Appendix 1（第 15 章）提供本指引與主要法規（EU GMP Annex 15、FDA Process Validation Guidance、ICH Q8/Q9/Q10）的對應，從法規角度確認 ISPE C&Q 方法的合規性基礎。本節末提供 Appendix 2–17 的概覽總表。

14.1

14.1 Introduction

Transitioning to the science and risk-based C&Q approach | Page 105

14.1 Introduction

This chapter describes strategies how organizations can effectively transition to the science and risk-based C&Q process described in this Guide. Implementing change successfully often requires high-level sponsorship due to the numerous stakeholders impacted.

The key to a successful transition is to recognize that there are multiple ways that the regulatory expectations can be met; adopting the science and risk-based approach does not invalidate current work or existing documentation. It should be noted that any process used for C&Q is expected to be science and risk-based.

Qualification documents represent a picture of the system at a point in time; this information changes with time and there are quality systems in place to manage this change (including associated revision of the qualification and engineering record documents), such as change management, maintenance, calibration, and periodic review. Therefore, existing documentation can remain acceptable to provide the documented evidence that the system is suitable for the intended purpose.

Figure 14.1 provides a flow chart of the suggested steps for implementation of the science and risk-based C&Q approach described in this Guide.

導讀與解析

核心原則：不需重複確效 (No Need to Repeat Qualification)

這是第 14 章最重要的一句話，也是許多企業最擔心的問題：「採用 ISPE 新方法，是否意味著我過去做的 IQ/OQ/PQ 都要重做？」

答案是否定的。ISPE 明確指出：採用科學與風險基礎方法，並不會使現有確效文件失效。確效文件代表「系統在某一時間點的狀態快照」，只要配合現有的品質系統（變更管理、維護、校正、定期審查），現有文件仍可繼續作為系統適用性的有效證明。

重點提示：高階贊助的重要性

ISPE 特別指出，成功的轉型「往往需要高階贊助」，因為涉及眾多利害關係人。這不只是技術問題，更是組織變革管理（Change Management）的挑戰：

  • 研發部門：需要提供科學與製程知識
  • 品質部門：需要接受不同的文件交付物
  • 工程部門：需要按 GDocP 標準交付文件
  • 系統負責人：需要接受訓練以執行必要審查

比喻：確效文件如同「體檢報告」

把確效文件想像成體檢報告：去年的體檢報告不會因為今年有了新的體檢標準就「失效」。舊報告仍然記錄了當時的身體狀況。只要在此期間有持續的健康管理（維護、校正、定期審查），就可以認定系統仍處於受控狀態。

新方法就像更好的體檢問卷——它幫助你更精準地找出關鍵指標（CDEs）並驗證它們，但並不要求你把所有舊報告全部推翻重做。

14.2

14.2 Preparing for Implementation

Six suggested steps for implementation preparation | Page 107

14.2 Preparing for Implementation

The suggested steps for implementation preparation are described in more detail as follows:

  1. Define the organization approach:
    This Guide describes a suggested approach for organizations to adopt, but it may need to be tailored to fit the specific structure of the organization.
  2. Evaluate the organizational maturity:
    It is useful to perform a documented assessment of organizational maturity, considering the quality systems and GEP, to determine the degree and pace of organizational transition. The assessment should consider all relevant aspects (e.g., experience, personnel resources, organizational culture). Examples of criteria for relevant departments include:
    • Research and Development/Process Development: Does this department have robust documentation and clear communication channels to provide data to enable the process?
    • Quality: Is the Quality Unit open to an alternative approach to C&Q and to the different documentation deliverables?
    • Engineering: Is the engineering department ready to deliver documents per Good Documentation Practice? Do they have adequate change management systems in place? Is there adequate document storage?
    • System Owners: Are the system owners adequately trained to perform the necessary reviews?
  3. Develop an implementation plan:
    A critical requirement for successful implementation is to have a well-defined implementation strategy with support from senior management. The use of initial small-scale proof of concept projects can help to identify any program aspects that require augmentation for a specific organization.
  4. Develop supporting quality systems and associated procedures:
    The procedures defining the engineering, quality, and documentation standards, as covered in this Guide, should be developed.
  5. Train staff on the approach:
    An important aspect for implementation is to provide overview training and ensure there is a good understanding of the key concepts. Considerations should also be made for how to present the approach to regulatory inspectors.
  6. Train staff on the procedures:
    The relevant staff should be sufficiently trained on the new procedures and have a good understanding of the overall program and its goals.

導讀與解析

六步驟準備框架

ISPE 提出六個實施準備步驟，本質上是一個組織成熟度評估與計畫制定的框架：

  • 步驟 1：定義組織方法（客製化指引）
  • 步驟 2：評估組織成熟度（從四個部門角度）
  • 步驟 3：制定導入計畫（含試點專案）
  • 步驟 4：建立支持性品質系統與 SOP
  • 步驟 5：對方法論進行員工培訓
  • 步驟 6：對具體程序進行員工培訓

組織成熟度評估的四個維度

步驟 2 的組織成熟度評估要從四個部門同時審視，任何一個短板都會影響整體導入：

  • 研發/製程開發：科學知識是否有足夠的文件基礎？資訊傳遞通道是否順暢？
  • 品質部門：是否願意接受「不一樣的文件交付物」？這需要品質部門的思維轉變。
  • 工程部門：是否有足夠的 GDocP 文件能力？變更管理系統是否完善？
  • 系統負責人：是否具備足夠訓練以執行審查？

評估結果決定轉型的「程度與速度」——這是非常務實的考量，允許不同成熟度的組織以不同步調推進。

試點專案（Pilot Project）的策略價值

步驟 3 特別強調「初始小規模概念驗證試點專案」的重要性。這如同軟體開發中的 MVP（最小可行產品）：

  • 在一個小型、低風險的系統上先行試跑
  • 找出組織特有的流程障礙
  • 獲得實際成果作為說服高階管理層的依據
  • 培養內部「先行者」成為方法論的推廣者

建議選擇新購設備或下一個小型確效專案作為試點，而非從最複雜的關鍵系統開始。

思考練習：如何說服高階管理層？

如果您需要向公司高階管理層提案採用 ISPE 2nd Ed. 方法，您會如何建構商業論述？提示：

  • 舊方法有哪些痛點（過度確效、文件冗余、成本過高）？
  • 新方法帶來哪些效益（聚焦關鍵、降低成本、符合稽查趨勢）？
  • 風險是什麼？如何降低風險（從試點專案開始）？
14.3

14.3 Approaches for Implementation

New projects, existing systems, and the champion model | Page 108

14.3 Approaches for Implementation

For new projects or facilities, the use of a champion for the new approach is recommended. This individual helps with the transition and implementation of the new approach and should have a good understanding of the process concepts/goals.

While implementation is more straightforward for new systems (for which there are no existing procedures/documentation), organizations also need to determine how the approach can be applied to a change on an existing qualified system. The most cost-effective way for implementation of the risk-based approach is to supplement the legacy approach as gaps are identified or changes to the system are made, thus maximizing the use of existing documentation.

A best practice approach would be to first assess if the system requires qualification — does the system have the potential to impact product quality? (see Chapter 3 for system classification criteria)

  • If it does not have the potential to impact product quality, then recategorize the system and commission the changes.
  • If it has the potential to impact product quality, then it requires qualification:
    • Review the existing documentation to determine if it meets current expectations.
    • If it does not, then qualify the system using the new approach, and remediate any gaps identified.

Table 14.1 shows the typical situations that may arise when implementing the science and risk-based C&Q approach within organizations with legacy systems, and the suggested approach.

Refer to Chapter 28 (Appendix 14) for an organizational maturity model and Chapter 29 (Appendix 15) for an approach to qualifying legacy systems or systems with inadequate qualification.

導讀與解析

三種導入情境

ISPE 區分了三種情境，每種情境的導入路徑不同：

  • 新系統（New System）：最直接，沒有現有文件包袱，從一開始就全面使用新方法。
  • 既有系統 + 小幅改動（Minor Change）：最常見，以現有文件為基礎，僅針對變更部分補充新方法要求。
  • 既有系統 + 重大改動（Major Change）：需要更全面地審查現有確效文件，找出差距並補充確效。

核心策略：最大化利用現有文件，只在發現差距或系統發生變更時才補充。

「Champion」角色的重要性

ISPE 特別提到「champion」（方法論推廣者/倡導者）這個角色。在組織轉型中，這個人至關重要：

  • 深入理解 ISPE C&Q 的概念與目標
  • 協助解決跨部門的阻力與誤解
  • 作為試點專案的技術主導
  • 建立組織的內部能力

通常由資深工程師或品質保證人員擔任，最好曾接受 ISPE 培訓或有相關實際經驗。

遺留系統的決策樹

面對遺留系統時，ISPE 提供了一個清晰的決策邏輯：

  1. 第一步：判斷系統是否有潛力影響產品品質？
  2. 如否：重新分類（可能降為 Indirect/No Impact），按 Commissioning 處理，不需要確效。
  3. 如是：需要確效 → 審查現有文件是否符合現行要求
  4. 文件符合：現有文件繼續有效，配合現有品質系統維護
  5. 文件不符合：使用新方法確效，並補救已識別的差距

這個邏輯避免了「一刀切」的重新確效，同時確保法規合規性。

14.4

Table 14.1 — Suggested Approach for Implementation of Science and Risk-Based C&Q

Three-scenario matrix: Major Change / Minor Change / New System | Page 109

Table 14.1: Suggested Approach for Implementation of Science and Risk-Based C&Q Approach

Step Major Change
(major change to an existing qualified system or existing system with potential compliance gaps)		 Minor Change
(minor change to existing system with good qualification package)		 New System
URS Review process requirements and gaps; identify CAs (based on risk) and proposed technical (CDEs) and procedural controls Requirements definition of the change control is required to describe the change Required
System Risk Assessment Risk assessment is required to determine the impact of the change Risk assessment is required to determine the impact of the change Required
DR/DQ Review the design to ensure change requirements are met Review the design to ensure change requirements are met Required
C&Q Plan Develop the plan to describe the approach Content is typically included in the change control Required
Test Plan Develop the plan Content is typically contained in change control (depending on complexity of testing required) Required
Testing Review existing qualification documentation to confirm technical controls (CDEs) that were identified based on risk have been tested; supplement with additional testing if required; review procedures to confirm procedural controls are in place; update if required Required to address the change Required
Procedures (operations and maintenance) Revise to address the change as required Revise to address the change as required Required
Acceptance and Release (Qualification Summary Report) Required Recorded and approved through closeout of the change control Required

Note: Any of these aspects may be combined depending on the magnitude and complexity of the project.

導讀與解析

Table 14.1 解讀：三種情境比較

這張表是第 14 章最核心的實務工具，清楚地說明了不同情境下的 C&Q 文件要求差異：

  • 新系統：全套文件均為「Required」——URS、SRA、DR/DQ、C&Q Plan、Test Plan、Testing、程序文件、最終報告
  • 小幅改動：大部分內容可以整合進「變更控制（Change Control）」文件，不需要獨立的完整確效文件包
  • 重大改動：需要補充審查——重點是確認現有確效文件已涵蓋基於風險識別的 CDEs，如有不足則補充

重大改動情境的關鍵動作：Gap Review

對於重大改動（Major Change），Table 14.1 的 Testing 欄位特別強調：

  1. 審查現有確效文件，確認基於風險識別的 CDEs 已被測試
  2. 如有不足，補充額外測試
  3. 審查 SOP，確認程序性控制措施已就位
  4. 如有需要，更新 SOP

這種「差距審查（Gap Review）」方式比全面重做更有效率，也是 ISPE 推薦的遺留系統處理方式。

CDMO 實務應用：三類系統的分類處理策略

對於一家中型 CDMO，建議按以下方式將現有設備分類處理：

  • A 類（新購設備）：全面導入 ISPE 2nd Ed. 方法，從 URS 開始即採用風險基礎分類與 SRA
  • B 類（既有設備 + 計畫變更）：在下一次變更控制時，附帶執行「Gap Review」，審查是否有未被涵蓋的 CDEs
  • C 類（既有設備 + 無計畫變更）：在下一次定期審查（Periodic Review）時評估現有文件的充分性，記錄評估結論

這種分類方式確保資源集中在最有價值的地方，同時逐步完成全廠系統的方法論轉型。

App.1

Chapter 15 / Appendix 1: Regulatory Basis

Key regulatory citations supporting the ISPE C&Q approach | Pages 111–122

15. Appendix 1 — Regulatory Basis

This Guide is intended to assist organizations in achieving compliance with regulatory expectations regarding C&Q. This appendix references key regulatory and guidance documents, highlighting text associated with the topics covered in each chapter of this Guide.

These lists are not intended to be all inclusive. It is recognized that there are ongoing developments with regulatory guidelines and this Guide reflects an understanding of them as of the publication date.

Primary Regulatory References

The regulatory expectations for C&Q are primarily described in the following documents:

  • EU GMP Annex 15 Qualification and Validation (October 2015)
  • PIC/S Annex 15 Qualification and validation (July 2018) — identical to EU GMP Annex 15 from Version 12
  • US FDA Guidance for Industry: Process Validation: General Principles and Practices (January 2011)
  • ICH Q8 Pharmaceutical Development (August 2009)
  • ICH Q9 Quality Risk Management (November 2005)
  • ICH Q10 Pharmaceutical Quality System (June 2008)
  • EU GMP Annex 3 (Radiopharmaceuticals)
  • EU GMP Annex 11 (Computerised Systems)

Note: ASTM E2500-13 is consistent with the regulatory references and provides additional clarity on the topics of this Guide.

Key Regulatory Citations — Chapter 1 (Introduction)

"The CGMP regulations require that manufacturing processes be designed and controlled to assure that in-process materials and the finished product meet predetermined quality requirements and do so consistently and reliably." [FDA Process Validation Guidance 2011]
"A quality risk management approach should be applied throughout the lifecycle of a medicinal product. As part of a quality risk management system, decisions on the scope and extent of qualification and validation should be based on a justified and documented risk assessment of the facilities, equipment, utilities and processes." [EU GMP Annex 15]
"Quality by Design (QbD): A systematic approach to development that begins with predefined objectives and emphasizes product and process understanding and process control, based on sound science and quality risk management." [ICH Q8]

Key Regulatory Citations — Chapter 2 (URS)

"The specification for equipment, facilities, utilities or systems should be defined in a URS and/or a functional specification. The essential elements of quality need to be built in at this stage and any GMP risks mitigated to an acceptable level. The URS should be a point of reference throughout the validation life cycle." [EU GMP Annex 15]

Key Regulatory Citations — Chapter 4 (Risk Assessment)

"With a lifecycle approach to process validation that employs risk based decision making throughout that lifecycle, the perception of criticality as a continuum rather than a binary state is more useful. All attributes and parameters should be evaluated in terms of their roles in the process and impact on the product or in-process material, and reevaluated as new information becomes available." [FDA Process Validation Guidance 2011]
"The level of effort, formality and documentation of the quality risk management process should be commensurate with the level of risk." [ICH Q9]

Key Regulatory Citations — Chapter 6 (C&Q Planning)

"Project plans, along with the full support of senior management, are essential elements for success." [FDA Process Validation Guidance 2011]
"The key elements of the site qualification and validation programme should be clearly defined and documented in a validation master plan (VMP) or equivalent document." [EU GMP Annex 15]

Key Regulatory Citations — Chapter 8 (Acceptance and Release)

"A formal release for the next stage in the qualification and validation process should be authorised by the relevant responsible personnel either as part of the validation report approval or as a separate summary document." [EU GMP Annex 15]

Key Regulatory Citations — Chapter 9 (Periodic Review)

"Equipment, facilities, utilities and systems should be evaluated at an appropriate frequency to confirm that they remain in a state of control." [EU GMP Annex 15]
"Once established, qualification status must be maintained through routine monitoring, maintenance, and calibration procedures and schedules (21 CFR part 211, subparts C and D)." [FDA Process Validation Guidance 2011]

Key Regulatory Citations — Chapter 12 (Change Management)

"Quality risk management should be used to evaluate planned changes to determine the potential impact on product quality, pharmaceutical quality systems, documentation, validation, regulatory status, calibration, maintenance and on any other system to avoid unintended consequences." [EU GMP Annex 15]

導讀與解析

Appendix 1 的作用：法規基礎的「對應表」

Appendix 1 逐章列出 ISPE C&Q 方法與主要法規的對應引用，其核心訊息是：ISPE C&Q 方法並非更寬鬆的替代品，而是法規期望的體現。

這份對應表的戰略意義在於：當稽查員質疑新方法的合規性時，可以直接引用這些法規原文作為依據。

主要法規文件解析

法規文件 全名與重點
EU GMP Annex 15 歐盟 GMP 附錄 15（確效與驗證，2015）— 最詳細的 IQ/OQ/PQ 要求，是歐盟市場的核心法規
FDA PV Guidance 2011 美國 FDA 製程驗證指引（2011）— 引入生命週期方法，支持科學與風險基礎方法
ICH Q8 藥品開發（QbD 的概念來源）— 將科學設計原則帶入 C&Q
ICH Q9 品質風險管理（QRM）— 提供風險評估框架，是 SRA 的法規基礎
ICH Q10 藥品品質系統（PQS）— 生命週期方法與知識管理的法規基礎
21 CFR 210/211 美國 cGMP 法規（藥品製造與管制的基本要求）

關鍵法規訊息解讀

Appendix 1 中有幾段引文特別值得注意：

  • 「風險程度相稱原則」（ICH Q9）：品質風險管理的力度、正式程度和文件要求，應與風險程度相稱。這直接支持了 ISPE 的比例原則——低風險系統不需要過度確效。
  • 「連續而非二元」（FDA 2011）：FDA 明確指出，關鍵性是一個「連續體」而非「非此即彼的二元狀態」。這為 CDEs 的風險分級提供了法規支持。
  • 「高階管理層的支持」（FDA 2011）：FDA 直接在法規指引中提到，「專案計畫以及高階管理層的全力支持是成功的關鍵要素」。

比喻：法規是地圖，ISPE 是導航

把主要法規（FDA、EU GMP Annex 15、ICH）想像成「地圖」：它們說明了你需要到達的目的地（確保品質、管理風險、生命週期管理），但沒有詳細說明如何開車。

ISPE C&Q 指引就像「導航系統」：它根據地圖規劃出一條具體、高效的路線。Appendix 1 就是在確認這條路線確實通往法規要求的目的地，沒有走捷徑，也沒有繞遠路。

15.14

15.14 Regulatory Basis for Chapter 14 (Implementation)

Regulatory grounding for the implementation strategy itself | Page 122

15.14 Chapter 14: Implementation of Science and Risk-Based C&Q Process

Regulatory guidance highlights the importance of product quality risk management and risk assessment to determine the scope and extent of qualification as described in the following regulatory text:

"A quality risk management approach should be applied throughout the lifecycle of a medicinal product. As part of a quality risk management system, decisions on the scope and extent of qualification and validation should be based on a justified and documented risk assessment of the facilities, equipment, utilities and processes." [EU GMP Annex 15]

The entire framework of Chapter 14's implementation strategy is underpinned by this single principle: the scope and extent of C&Q activities should be proportionate to risk, determined by a justified and documented risk assessment. This applies equally to the decision of how to implement the new approach — whether for new systems, existing systems with minor changes, or existing systems requiring major remediation.

導讀與解析

法規授權：以風險決定 C&Q 的範圍與程度

第 14 章的法規基礎只有一段核心引文，但這段話實際上授權了整個 ISPE 方法論的核心邏輯：

「確效的範圍與程度，應基於有正當理由且有文件記錄的風險評估。」

這意味著：

  • 不是所有系統都需要完整的 IQ/OQ/PQ
  • 不是所有測試都需要相同的嚴格程度
  • 這不是在放寬標準——而是在更準確地將資源聚焦在真正重要的地方

給稽查準備的核心論述

如果在 FDA 或 EMA 稽查中被質疑「為何你的確效文件與傳統 IQ/OQ/PQ 格式不同？」，正確的回應論述是：

  1. 我們遵循 EU GMP Annex 15（或 FDA Process Validation Guidance）的要求
  2. 法規明確要求以有文件記錄的風險評估來決定確效的範圍與程度
  3. 我們的方法（ISPE C&Q）正是該法規期望的體現
  4. 我們的 SRA 文件（系統風險評估）就是「有正當理由且有文件記錄的風險評估」

這個論述將方法論的合法性建立在法規原文之上，而非僅依賴 ISPE 指引本身的權威性。

導讀與解析

附錄體系的整體架構

ISPE Vol.5 的附錄體系（Appendix 1–17）提供了完整的「工具箱」，對應主體各章節：

  • 法規依據類（App.1）：提供合規論述的法規引文基礎
  • 文件模板類（App.2, 3, 5, 6, 7, 8, 9, 11, 13）：可直接修改使用的 SOP 表格與模板
  • 參考清單類（App.4）：提供典型 Direct Impact 系統清單供參考
  • 成熟度評估類（App.14）：用於評估組織轉型準備度
  • 遺留系統專用類（App.15）：專門處理遺留系統確效問題
  • 術語定義類（App.17）：確保全組織使用一致的術語

最重要的附錄：App.2（URS）與 App.5（SRA）

從實務角度，新導入 ISPE 方法的組織最常使用的兩個附錄：

  • Appendix 2（URS 模板）：提供完整的 URS 文件格式，包含「合適」與「不合適」需求的範例說明，非常有教學價值。例如，純粹的工程規格（如 HMI 解析度）不應寫在 URS 中。
  • Appendix 5（SRA 模板）：系統風險評估是 ISPE 方法的核心工具，決定了哪些系統元件是 CDEs，進而決定確效測試的範圍。有了標準模板可以確保評估的一致性。

CDMO 導入路線圖：從零到全面導入的 12 個月計畫

建議中型 CDMO 按以下時程推進 ISPE 2nd Ed. 導入：

  • 月 1-2：組織準備 — 指定 Champion、完成組織成熟度評估（App.14）、高階管理層簡報
  • 月 3-4：SOP 建立 — 依據本指引修訂確效主計畫（VMP）、制定系統分類 SOP、SRA SOP
  • 月 5-6：試點專案 — 選定一個新購設備，全程採用 ISPE 方法（URS → SRA → DR → C&Q）
  • 月 7-8：稽查準備 — 整理法規對應文件（App.1 引文）、培訓稽查應對話術
  • 月 9-12：全面推廣 — 對所有新系統採用新方法；對既有系統在下次 Periodic Review 或變更時按 Table 14.1 處理

附錄如同「標準套件」

把 ISPE 附錄體系想像成一個品質管理「標準套件」，類似 ISO 9001 的文件模板包。你不需要從頭發明文件格式，只需要按照組織需求客製化這些模板，再加上適當的版本控制與審核流程，即可建立符合 ISPE 標準的 C&Q 文件體系。

對於資源有限的中小型製造商或 CDMO，直接使用這些模板可以節省大量的文件開發時間，並確保符合業界最佳實踐。

Implementation Summary: The ISPE Vol.5 Complete Lifecycle

This section represents the culmination of the ISPE Baseline Guide Vol.5 Commissioning and Qualification (2nd Edition). The Guide has described a complete, science and risk-based framework for C&Q that:

  • Starts with understanding intended use (URS, Chapter 2)
  • Classifies systems by GMP impact (Chapter 3)
  • Uses risk assessment to scope qualification activities (Chapter 4)
  • Reviews and qualifies design (Chapter 5)
  • Plans C&Q activities systematically (Chapter 6)
  • Executes testing based on risk-identified CDEs (Chapter 7)
  • Formally accepts and releases qualified systems (Chapter 8)
  • Maintains qualified state through periodic review (Chapter 9)
  • Leverages vendor data appropriately (Chapter 10)
  • Ensures engineering quality throughout (Chapter 11)
  • Manages changes systematically (Chapter 12)
  • Documents everything per GDocP (Chapter 13)
  • Implements strategically with legacy consideration (Chapter 14)

All of this is underpinned by regulatory expectations from FDA, EU GMP Annex 15, and ICH Q8/Q9/Q10, as documented in Appendix 1 (Chapter 15).

最終綜合應用練習

假設您是一家 CDMO 的驗證部門主管，剛收到以下三個任務，請根據 Table 14.1 判斷各應採用哪種方法：

  1. 公司新購入一台全自動灌裝機，尚未安裝。
  2. 既有凍乾機（15 年前做過 IQ/OQ/PQ）需要更換一個冷凝器，屬於非設計變更的同規格替換。
  3. 既有 WFI 系統計畫擴建新的分配迴路，新增 3 個使用點。

提示：情境 1 = 新系統；情境 2 = 小幅改動；情境 3 = 重大改動（重新評估 URS 和 SRA）。
